braised_veal_chop_with_sweetbreads.txt - Braised Veal Chop with Sweetbreads, Lemon, and Herbs

Objectives

  • Learn to braise veal chops and sweetbreads with lemon and herbs.
  • Master the art of preparing and cooking sweetbreads.
  • Create a flavorful and elegant family dish.

Ingredients

  • 3 veal chops (about 10 ounces each)
  • 1 cup white wine vinegar
  • 3/4 cup sugar
  • 1 stem rosemary
  • 1 lemon (cut into slices)
  • Sweetbreads (soaked and trimmed)
  • 1 head garlic (peeled)
  • 1 sweet onion (cut into wedges)
  • 1 small heart of celery (peeled and cut into large pieces)
  • 1 carrot (cut into large pieces)
  • Baby turnips (peeled with a knife)
  • 2 fennel bulbs (cut into small wedges)
  • Radishes (about 1.5 cups)
  • Olive oil
  • Butter (about 1 tablespoon)
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Fresh rosemary
  • Fresh chives
  • Fresh chervil
  • Fresh tarragon
  • Fresh parsley

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 475 degrees F (246 degrees C).
  2. Blanch lemon slices in boiling water until slightly tender.
  3. Combine white wine vinegar and sugar in a pot.
  4. Add rosemary stem to the vinegar and sugar mixture.
  5. Transfer lemon slices to the vinegar and sugar mixture and simmer for 20-30 minutes.
  6. Trim sweetbreads of any excess fat and membrane.
  7. Insert a rosemary skewer into each sweetbread.
  8. Tie veal chops with string, twisting the string around the front bone to keep the meat tight.
  9. Season veal chops with salt and pepper.
  10. Lightly dust veal chops with Wondra flour.
  11. Heat olive oil in a roasting pan over medium heat.
  12. Add veal chops to the pan and roast for 10 minutes, or until browned.
  13. Add veal jus to the pan and continue braising for 10-15 minutes.
  14. Remove veal chops from the pan and let rest.
  15. Add garlic, sweet onion, celery, carrot, baby turnips, fennel, and radishes to the pan.
  16. Season vegetables with salt, pepper, and a pinch of sugar.
  17. Deglaze the pan with a little lemon juice and white wine.
  18. Braise vegetables in the oven for 15-20 minutes, or until tender.
  19. Remove vegetables from the oven and add fresh herbs: rosemary, chives, chervil, tarragon, and parsley.
  20. Drain lemon slices.
  21. Cut veal chops into 3-4 slices.
  22. Slice sweetbreads.
  23. Place veal chops on a platter.
  24. Top each veal chop slice with a sweet and sour lemon slice.
  25. Arrange vegetables around the veal chops.
  26. Drizzle sauce over the dish.
  27. Garnish with fresh herbs.
  28. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lV238hdxpn0

bread_machine_recipes.txt - Bread Machine Recipes

Objectives

  • Learn how to make bread using a bread machine
  • Explore the versatility of a bread machine by making different recipes
  • Understand the importance of checking dough consistency and using a clean teaspoon for yeast

Ingredients

White Buttermilk Bread - 2½ teaspoons instant yeast - 3 tablespoons powdered buttermilk - 1 teaspoon salt - 3 cups unbleached, unbromated flour - 1 tablespoon very soft butter - 3 tablespoons maple syrup - 1 cup room temperature water

Spicy Bean Bread - 1 tablespoon instant yeast - ½ cup cornmeal - 3 tablespoons nonfat dry milk - 2 teaspoons chili powder - 1½ teaspoons salt - 1 cup white wheat flour - 2 cups all-purpose flour - 1 cup refried beans - ¼ cup Taos red-chili honey - ¼ cup oil - 1 egg - 1 cup water

Quitza - 1 package instant yeast - 1 teaspoon sugar - 1 teaspoon salt - 2 cups all-purpose flour - 1 cup warm water - 1 cup softened cream cheese - 1 cup chunky salsa - 1 cup grated cheddar cheese

Instructions

  1. White Buttermilk Bread: Remove the bread pan from the machine. Add the dry ingredients in the following order: yeast, buttermilk powder, salt, flour. Add the wet ingredients in the following order: butter, maple syrup, water. Place the pan in the bread machine and close the lid. Check the dough after five minutes to see if you need to add more flour or water.
  2. Spicy Bean Bread: Remove the bread pan from the machine. Add the dry ingredients in the following order: yeast, cornmeal, nonfat dry milk, chili powder, salt, white wheat flour, all-purpose flour. Add the wet ingredients in the following order: refried beans, red-chili honey, oil, egg, water. Place the pan in the bread machine and close the lid. Check the dough after five minutes to see if you need to add more flour or water.
  3. Quitza: Combine the dry ingredients in the bread machine. Add the warm water and start the dough cycle. After the dough cycle is complete, spread the cream cheese on the bottom of the springform pan. Top with salsa and cheddar cheese. Let rise until double in bulk. Bake at 475 degrees for 20-25 minutes.

Cloverleaf Rolls 1. Prepare: Grease muffin tins with butter. 2. Form: Cut the dough into three little balls. Using your finger, form a hole in the center of each ball. 3. Assemble: Place the balls in the muffin tin, three per tin. 4. Let Rise: Let rise for about 20 minutes. 5. Bake: Bake at 450 degrees for 12-15 minutes.

Twisty Rolls 1. Form: Cut a strip of dough and tie it into a knot. Place the knot on a baking sheet. 2. Let Rise: Let rise for about 20 minutes. 3. Bake: Bake at 450 degrees for 12-15 minutes.

Breadsticks 1. Form: Roll out a long rope of dough and twist it. Place on a baking sheet. 2. Let Rise: Let rise for about 20 minutes. 3. Glaze: Brush with egg glaze and sprinkle with poppy seeds. 4. Bake: Bake at 450 degrees for 12-15 minutes.

Baking Bread 1. Remove the Bread Pan: After 10 minutes of baking, remove the bread pan from the oven to allow the bread to brown on all sides. 2. Check the Temperature: To determine if the bread is done, insert a meat thermometer into the center of the loaf. The internal temperature should be 200 degrees. 3. Cool: Remove the bread from the oven and place it on a cooling rack. Let cool completely before slicing.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xPJwwfHzjDg

brioche_sticky_buns_and_savory_brioche_pockets.txt - Brioche Sticky Buns and Savory Brioche Pockets

Objectives

  • Learn to make brioche dough using the sponge method
  • Master the technique of incorporating butter into brioche dough
  • Create delicious sticky buns with a rich, buttery flavor
  • Explore savory brioche pockets filled with goat cheese, asparagus, and potatoes

Ingredients

Sponge - 2 1/4 teaspoons dried yeast - 1/3 cup warm milk - 1 egg - 1 cup all-purpose flour

Brioche Dough - 1/3 cup sugar - 1 teaspoon kosher salt - 4 eggs - 1 1/2 cups all-purpose flour - 1 cup (2 sticks) unsalted butter, softened - 3 ounces unsalted butter, softened

Sticky Buns - 2 tablespoons sugar - 1/8 teaspoon cinnamon - 1/2 cup pecans, chopped - 1 egg - 1/2 cup pecans, halves

Savory Brioche Pockets - 1 tablespoon caramelized onions - 2 tablespoons mashed potatoes - 2 asparagus tips - 1 tablespoon goat cheese - 2 tablespoons chives - 1 tablespoon poppy seeds - 1 fresh sage leaf - 1 egg

Instructions

  1. In a large bowl, combine the yeast, milk, egg, and 1 cup of flour. Mix well until combined.
  2. Cover the bowl with a cup of flour and let it rest for 30-40 minutes.
  3. Once the sponge has risen and cracked, add the sugar, salt, and 4 eggs to the bowl.
  4. Add 1 cup of flour and mix on low speed until combined.
  5. Slowly increase the speed to medium and add the remaining 1/2 cup of flour.
  6. Continue mixing until the dough starts to wrap around the hook of the mixer.
  7. Add the softened butter, 1 cup at a time, mixing on low speed until incorporated.
  8. Turn off the mixer and scrape down the sides of the bowl.
  9. Continue mixing until the dough is smooth and elastic.
  10. Transfer the dough to a lightly oiled bowl and cover with plastic wrap.
  11. Let the dough rise in a warm place until doubled in size, about 1 hour.
  12. Gently punch down the dough and transfer it to a lightly floured surface.
  13. Divide the dough in half.
  14. Refrigerate one half of the dough for later use.
  15. On a lightly floured surface, roll out the other half of the dough to a 11x14 inch rectangle.
  16. Dot the dough with 3 ounces of softened butter.
  17. Fold the dough in thirds, like a letter.
  18. Refrigerate the dough for 30 minutes.
  19. Roll out the dough again to a 11x14 inch rectangle.
  20. Brush the dough with egg wash.
  21. Sprinkle with cinnamon sugar.
  22. Sprinkle with chopped pecans.
  23. Roll up the dough tightly, starting from the long side.
  24. Place the roll in the freezer for 45 minutes.
  25. While the dough is freezing, prepare the pan for the sticky buns.
  26. Spread softened butter on the bottom of a baking pan.
  27. Sprinkle with brown sugar.
  28. Remove the dough from the freezer and cut it into 1 1/2 inch slices.
  29. Place the slices in the prepared pan, pressing them gently into the brown sugar mixture.
  30. Top each slice with a pecan half.
  31. Let the sticky buns rise in a warm place until doubled in size, about 1 1/2-2 hours.
  32. Bake the sticky buns at 325 degrees Fahrenheit for 20-25 minutes, or until golden brown.
  33. Let the sticky buns cool completely before serving.
  34. For the savory brioche pockets, roll out the refrigerated dough to a thin rectangle on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  35. Using a 4 1/2 inch round cutter, cut out circles of dough.
  36. Place the dough circles on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  37. In a bowl, combine the mashed potatoes, goat cheese, chives, poppy seeds, and sage. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  38. Place a tablespoon of caramelized onions in the center of each dough circle.
  39. Top with 2 tablespoons of the potato mixture and 2 asparagus tips.
  40. Gently fold the dough over the filling and crimp the edges to seal.
  41. Brush the pockets with egg wash.
  42. Let the pockets rest for 20 minutes.
  43. Bake the pockets at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 20-25 minutes, or until golden brown.
  44. Serve the pockets warm or at room temperature.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wnAFcR8U7-A

brioche.txt - Brioche

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic brioche dough
  • Understand the importance of yeast activation and dough kneading
  • Explore different ways to shape and bake brioche

Ingredients

  • 1 package of dry active yeast
  • 3 tablespoons of hot water (110 degrees Fahrenheit)
  • 1/4 teaspoon of salt
  • 1/2 tablespoon of sugar
  • 3 large eggs (at room temperature)
  • 1/2 tablespoon of sugar
  • 3/4 teaspoon of salt
  • 2 cups of all-purpose flour
  • 1 1/2 sticks of unsalted butter (6 ounces)

Instructions

  1. In a small bowl, dissolve the yeast in the hot water.
  2. Add the salt and sugar to the yeast mixture and set aside for 5-6 minutes to proof.
  3. In a separate bowl, beat the eggs until combined.
  4. Add the sugar, salt, and flour to the eggs and mix well.
  5. Gradually add the softened butter to the dough, kneading until it is smooth and elastic.
  6. Place the dough in a greased bowl, cover with plastic wrap, and let rise in a warm place until doubled in size.
  7. Punch down the dough and let it rise again until doubled in size.
  8. Place the dough in the refrigerator for at least 4 hours, or overnight.
  9. Once the dough is chilled, divide it into portions for shaping.
  10. For small brioche, form a small ball of dough for the base and a pear-shaped ball for the top.
  11. Place the base in a greased fluted tin, then push the pear-shaped ball into the base to create a "head."
  12. For a large brioche, form a large ball of dough and place it in a greased ovenware casserole or bowl.
  13. Make a hole in the center of the dough and place a smaller ball of dough in the hole to create a "head."
  14. For a crown brioche, shape the dough into a ring on a wet baking sheet.
  15. Brush all the brioche with an egg glaze (1 egg beaten with 1 teaspoon of water).
  16. Bake the brioche in a preheated 475-degree oven.
  17. Baking times vary depending on the size of the brioche:
    • Small brioche: 15 minutes
    • Large brioche: 20-30 minutes (reduce oven temperature to 350 degrees after the first 15 minutes)
    • Crown brioche: 15-20 minutes
  18. Check for doneness by inserting a needle or straw into the side of the brioche. If it comes out clean, it is done.
  19. Let the brioche cool completely before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=5vzo6q3epC4

broccoli_and_cauliflower.txt - Broccoli and Cauliflower

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and cook broccoli and cauliflower in the French style
  • Understand the importance of peeling and separating vegetables for optimal tenderness and flavor
  • Explore different ways to serve broccoli and cauliflower, including sauce polonaise and mock hollandaise

Ingredients

  • Broccoli
  • Cauliflower
  • Water
  • Kosher salt
  • Butter
  • White bread
  • Egg
  • Granular flour
  • Cream
  • Lemon
  • Parsley

Instructions

  1. Peel the broccoli stalks:
    • Cut the broccoli stalk into pieces where the stems are attached.
    • Cut off the butt end of the stalk.
    • Peel the green part of the stalk until you reach the tender flesh underneath.
    • Peel the lower part of the stem on the top part of the broccoli.
    • Save the peelings for soup.
  2. Cut the broccoli into smaller pieces:
    • Cut the broccoli stems in half and then in half again.
    • Pull off the outer skin.
  3. Wash the broccoli:
    • Wash the prepared broccoli under cold water.
  4. Cook the broccoli:
    • Bring a pot of water to a rapid boil.
    • Add the broccoli to the boiling water, making sure it's covered.
    • Add kosher salt to the water.
    • Cook for 5 minutes.
    • Test the broccoli for doneness by tasting a piece. It should be slightly crunchy.
  5. Prepare the sauce polonaise:
    • Melt butter in a saucepan.
    • Make bread crumbs in an electric blender by breaking up white bread and blending one piece at a time.
    • Add bread crumbs to melted butter.
    • Push an egg through a strainer with your hands.
    • Add the egg to the bread crumbs and butter mixture.
  6. Serve the broccoli:
    • Arrange the cooked broccoli on a hot serving dish.
    • Sprinkle with salt, pepper, the egg mixture, and bread crumbs.
  7. Peel the cauliflower:
    • Remove the outer leaves of the cauliflower.
    • Save the tender leaves for soup or salad.
    • Cut out the central stem of the cauliflower.
  8. Separate the cauliflower:
    • Cut the cauliflower head into flowerets.
    • Peel the stem of each floweret.
    • Save the peelings for soup.
    • Cut the smaller flowerets into desired sizes.
  9. Cook the cauliflower:
    • Bring a pot of water to a rapid boil.
    • Add the cauliflower flowerets to the boiling water, making sure they're covered.
    • Add kosher salt to the water.
    • Cook for 5-6 minutes.
    • Test the cauliflower for doneness by tasting a piece. It should be slightly crunchy.
  10. Prepare the mock hollandaise sauce:
    • Mix 2 tablespoons of soft butter and 2 heaping tablespoons of granular flour with a rubber spatula.
    • Add hot cauliflower water to the mixture and beat with a wire whip.
    • Cook over heat until the sauce thickens.
    • Add more water as needed to reach desired consistency.
    • Beat an egg yolk with a third of a cup of cream.
    • Gradually add the hot sauce base to the egg yolk mixture.
    • Heat the sauce until it just barely comes to a simmer.
    • Add lemon juice to taste.
    • Set aside and add butter just before serving.
  11. Mold the cauliflower:
    • Heat a bowl over simmering water.
    • Place the cooked cauliflower in the hot bowl, heads down.
    • Add salt, pepper, and a little bit of the sauce in layers.
    • Continue building up the cauliflower in the bowl, heads down.
  12. Serve the cauliflower:
    • Place a hot serving dish upside down over the cauliflower in the bowl.
    • Push down on the serving dish and remove the bowl.
    • Turn the serving dish over and center the cauliflower.
    • Pour the remaining sauce over the cauliflower.
    • Garnish with parsley.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=k4k1VgWeuxM

broiled_chicken.txt - Broiled Chicken

Objectives

  • Learn two methods for broiling chicken: plain and with a mustard coating
  • Understand the importance of basting for a crispy, juicy chicken
  • Explore French techniques for preparing chicken and peas

Ingredients

Plain Broiled Chicken

  • 1 broiler chicken (2-2.25 pounds)
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1/2 tablespoon oil
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Mustard-Coated Broiled Chicken

  • 1 broiler chicken (2-2.25 pounds)
  • 1/3 cup strong French mustard (Dijon type)
  • 1/2 teaspoon thyme
  • 1 1/2 tablespoons chopped shallots or scallions
  • 1 1/2 tablespoons bread crumbs
  • Butter and basting juices from chicken

French Peas

  • 2 cups peas
  • 1/2 cup lettuce, chopped
  • 1 1/2 tablespoons shallots or onions
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1 teaspoon sugar
  • 1 1/2 tablespoons butter

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Chicken:
  2. Remove the backbone by cutting down each side with a sharp knife or poultry shears.
  3. Flatten the chicken by pressing down on the breastbone to break the rib cage.
  4. Cut off the wing tip.
  5. Slit the ball joints on the legs to prevent them from popping up during cooking.

  6. Fold the wing tip back under the shoulder.

  7. Baste the Chicken:

  8. Melt butter and oil in a broiling pan.
  9. Brush the melted butter and oil over both sides of the chicken.

  10. Do not season with salt until later.

  11. Broil the Chicken (Plain Method):

  12. Preheat broiler to high heat.
  13. Broil chicken skin side down for 10-12 minutes.
  14. Turn chicken skin side up and broil for another 12-15 minutes.
  15. Baste the chicken every 4-5 minutes during broiling.

  16. Season with salt and pepper after turning the chicken over.

  17. Make the Deglazing Sauce (Optional):

  18. Leave a tablespoon of butter in the broiling pan.
  19. Add chopped shallots or green onions and cook for a moment.
  20. Deglaze the pan with a little brown chicken or beef stock.
  21. Add a spoonful of vermouth (optional).

  22. Let the sauce boil down and spoon it over the chicken.

  23. Serve the Plain Broiled Chicken:

  24. Serve the chicken immediately.

  25. Garnish with watercress or parsley.

  26. Broil the Chicken (Mustard-Coated Method):

  27. Broil the chicken skin side down for 8-9 minutes.

  28. Turn the chicken skin side up and broil for another 8-9 minutes.

  29. Prepare the Mustard Coating:

  30. Combine Dijon mustard, hot pepper sauce (or regular pepper), thyme, and shallots or scallions in a bowl.

  31. Gradually beat in the basting juices from the chicken until the mixture reaches a mayonnaise-like consistency.

  32. Coat the Chicken:

  33. Spread the mustard mixture over the underside of the chicken.
  34. Sprinkle with bread crumbs.

  35. Baste with butter and basting juices.

  36. Broil the Chicken (Mustard-Coated Method):

  37. Broil the chicken skin side down for 5 minutes until browned.

  38. Coat the other side with the mustard mixture and broil for another 5 minutes.

  39. Prepare the French Peas:

  40. Combine peas, lettuce, shallots or onions, salt, sugar, and butter in a pot.
  41. Bruise the peas with your hands to break the shell and allow the seasonings to penetrate.
  42. Cover with cold water and bring to a boil.
  43. Reduce heat to a medium boil and cook until peas are tender (20-30 minutes).

  44. Add more water if needed to prevent burning.

  45. Serve the Mustard-Coated Chicken with Peas:

  46. Serve the chicken immediately with the French peas.

  47. Garnish with broiled tomatoes (optional).

  48. Reheating the Mustard-Coated Chicken:

  49. To reheat, broil the chicken under a low broiler or bake in a 375 degree oven for 20 minutes until heated through.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IADblWE21LI

buche_de_noel.txt - Buche de Noel

Objectives

  • Learn to create a Buche de Noel (Yule Log) with chocolate bark, meringue mushrooms, and powdered sugar snow.
  • Understand the process of making a sponge sheet and rolling it up with frosting.
  • Explore different techniques for decorating the Buche de Noel, including frosting, piping, and caramel.

Ingredients

Cake - Sponge sheet (recipe from a cookbook) - Chocolate buttercream frosting

Mushrooms - 3 egg whites - 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar - Pinch of salt - 1 1/3 cups granulated sugar - 1/3 cup water - Buttercream frosting

Moss - 1/2 cup sugar - 1/4 cup water - Oiled pole or broomstick

Other - Powdered sugar - Cocoa powder - Wax paper

Instructions

  1. Prepare the sponge sheet according to a cookbook recipe.
  2. Roll the sponge sheet up with chocolate buttercream frosting.
  3. Make saw marks on each side of the log with a knife.
  4. Cut a small hole in the log to create a twig.
  5. Frost the log with chocolate buttercream frosting using a spatula or pastry tool.
  6. Pipe frosting onto the twig to complete its appearance.
  7. Refrigerate the log to allow the frosting to set.
  8. Boil 1 1/3 cups sugar and 1/3 cup water until it reaches the soft ball stage (238 degrees Fahrenheit).
  9. Beat three egg whites with a pinch of salt and a scant 1/4 teaspoon of cream of tartar until stiff peaks form.
  10. Gradually pour the hot sugar syrup into the beaten egg whites, beating until the mixture is cool and glossy.
  11. Using a pastry bag with a small spoon tip, pipe out large and small meringue mushrooms onto a buttered and floured baking sheet.
  12. Bake the mushrooms in a 200-degree oven for 40 minutes to an hour, or until they make a crackling noise.
  13. Fill the large mushroom heads with buttercream frosting and attach the smaller mushroom bottoms.
  14. Decorate the log with the meringue mushrooms, cocoa powder, and powdered sugar.
  15. Boil 1/2 cup sugar and 1/4 cup water until it turns into caramel.
  16. Let the caramel cool slightly until it spins a thread when lifted on a fork.
  17. Using a fork, wave the caramel over an oiled pole or broomstick to create moss.
  18. Arrange the moss around the log.
  19. Serve the Buche de Noel with coffee, tea, or champagne.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MK6RGdAfIGM

caramel_custard.txt - Caramel Custard and Apple Custard

Objectives

  • Learn to make a caramel syrup for lining molds.
  • Learn to make a French custard called crème renversée au caramel.
  • Learn to make an apple custard.
  • Learn to unmold baked custards.
  • Learn to make a nut brittle to top the apple custard.

Ingredients

Caramel Syrup - 1/2 cup granulated sugar - 2 1/2 tablespoons water

Crème Renversée au Caramel - 5 whole eggs - 4 egg yolks - 3 3/4 cups hot milk - 3/4 cup granulated sugar - 2 teaspoons vanilla extract

Apple Custard - 12 cups sliced apples (about 3 quarts) - 2 tablespoons lemon juice - 1 teaspoon cinnamon - 1/2 cup granulated sugar - 1/2 cup melted butter - 1 lemon, zested - 4 whole eggs - 1 egg white - 2 tablespoons dark rum (optional)

Nut Brittle - Caramel syrup (leftover from lining molds) - Chopped almonds (amount to taste)

Instructions

  1. Make the Caramel Syrup:
  2. Combine sugar and water in a heavy pan.
  3. Swirl the pan until sugar is melted and begins to boil.
  4. Continue cooking, watching for syrupy bubbles.
  5. Once sugar reaches the brittle stage, pour it into the mold.
  6. Let the caramel cool and harden before reversing the mold onto a plate.
  7. Make the Crème Renversée au Caramel:
  8. Beat 5 whole eggs and 4 egg yolks with 3/4 cup sugar until foamy.
  9. Gradually beat in 3 3/4 cups hot milk.
  10. Add 2 teaspoons vanilla extract.
  11. Strain the custard mixture into the caramel-lined mold.
  12. Place the mold in a baking pan and fill the pan with water halfway up the sides of the mold.
  13. Bake at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 40 minutes, or until the custard is set.
  14. Let the custard cool completely before unmolding.
  15. Make the Apple Custard:
  16. Slice 12 cups of apples into quarters.
  17. Core and peel the apples.
  18. Place the apples in a roasting pan and toss with 2 tablespoons lemon juice, 1 teaspoon cinnamon, 1/2 cup sugar, and 1/2 cup melted butter.
  19. Bake at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 20 minutes, or until softened.
  20. While the apples bake, beat 4 whole eggs and 1 egg white with the zest of 1 lemon and 2 tablespoons dark rum (optional).
  21. Fold the baked apples into the egg mixture.
  22. Pour the apple custard mixture into the caramel-lined mold.
  23. Bake at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 1 1/2 hours, or until set.
  24. Let the custard cool completely before unmolding.
  25. Make the Nut Brittle:
  26. Heat leftover caramel syrup until melted.
  27. Pour the caramel over chopped almonds in a smaller pan.
  28. Stir to combine the nuts and caramel.
  29. Spread the mixture on a plate and let it cool and harden.
  30. Once hardened, pound the brittle into smaller pieces.
  31. Serve the Custards:
  32. Unmold the custards by running a knife around the edge of the mold and inverting it onto a serving plate.
  33. Serve the custards hot, warm, or cold.
  34. Top the apple custard with the nut brittle.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=RQ_RIEQREJQ

carbonnade_de_boeuf_a_la_provencale.txt - Carbonnade de Boeuf à la Provençale

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French beef stew, Carbonnade de Boeuf à la Provençale
  • Understand the importance of marinating the beef for flavor and tenderness
  • Explore different methods for slicing potatoes and onions

Ingredients

  • 5-6 cups sliced onions (about 2 lbs)
  • 2/3 cup fresh pork butt, cut into 1/2 inch pieces
  • 1 tablespoon oil
  • 6-7 cups sliced potatoes (boiling or all-purpose)
  • 1/4 cup red wine vinegar
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1/8 teaspoon black pepper
  • 3/4 teaspoon ground dried savory
  • 3/4 teaspoon ground dried thyme
  • 2 large cloves garlic
  • 3 lbs chuck steak, sliced into serving pieces (about 3.5 x 2.5 x 0.5 inches)
  • 6 cups brown beef stock (homemade or canned)
  • 1/4 cup freshly grated Parmesan cheese

Instructions

  1. Chop onions: Slice onions in half, remove root ends, and slice thinly.
  2. Marinate the beef: Combine red wine vinegar, olive oil, pepper, savory, thyme, and garlic in a bowl. Marinate the beef for at least 6 hours, up to 2-3 days.
  3. Cook the pork butt: Heat oil in a pan over medium heat. Add the pork butt and cook for 3-4 minutes until rendered.
  4. Cook the onions: Add sliced onions to the pan with the rendered pork fat. Cook slowly for 20 minutes, covered, stirring occasionally, until lightly browned.
  5. Slice the potatoes: Slice potatoes using a knife, mandoline, or electric slicer.
  6. Assemble the Carbonnade: Preheat oven to 350°F. In a 5-6 quart casserole, layer 1/3 of the cooked onions, the marinated beef, salt and pepper, more onions, more beef, salt and pepper, and then the sliced potatoes. Season with salt and pepper.
  7. Add liquid and cook: Pour in beef stock until it reaches the top level of the beef. Bring to a simmer, cover, and cook in the oven for 1 hour.
  8. Check for tenderness: After an hour, use a fork to check if the beef is almost tender. If not, cook for an additional 30 minutes.
  9. Final cooking: Uncover the casserole, sprinkle with Parmesan cheese, and add a little olive oil if desired. Cook uncovered in a 425°F oven for 30 minutes, or until the top is browned and bubbling.
  10. Serve: Serve the Carbonnade de Boeuf à la Provençale hot.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=6C92c-nDRd0

cardinale_cake.txt - Cardinale Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic Viennese pastry with layers of meringue, cake batter, and espresso cream.
  • Understand the importance of proper meringue and batter preparation.
  • Learn to make a caramel cage decoration for the cake.

Ingredients

Meringue: - 4 egg whites - 6 tablespoons of sugar - 3/4 cup of powdered sugar

Sponge Batter: - 4 egg yolks - 4 whole eggs - 4 1/2 tablespoons of sugar - 3/4 cup of all-purpose flour

Caramel: - 1 cup of sugar - 1 tablespoon of water

Espresso Cream: - 1 cup of heavy cream - 2 tablespoons of sugar - 2 tablespoons of espresso extract

Other: - Parchment paper - Sheet pan - Piping bag - Wooden spoon - White cardboard

Instructions

  1. Prepare the parchment paper and sheet pan:
  2. Butter the sheet pan.
  3. Cut parchment paper into strips about 3 inches wide.
  4. Place the strips on the sheet pan, leaving a small space from the edge.
  5. Make the meringue:
  6. Crack 4 eggs into a bowl and separate the whites from the yolks.
  7. Add 6 tablespoons of sugar to the egg whites and whisk with your hands to combine.
  8. Beat the egg whites on low speed for a few minutes, then increase to high speed until stiff peaks form.
  9. Fold in 3/4 cup of powdered sugar, being careful not to deflate the meringue.
  10. Make the sponge batter:
  11. Combine 4 egg yolks, 4 whole eggs, and 4 1/2 tablespoons of sugar in a bowl.
  12. Beat on medium speed for a few minutes, then increase to high speed until the mixture is foamy.
  13. Fold in 3/4 cup of flour, being careful not to deflate the batter.
  14. Pipe the meringue and batter onto the prepared sheet pan:
  15. Fill a piping bag with the meringue and pipe it onto the parchment paper strips.
  16. Fill the piping bag with the batter and pipe it over the meringue.
  17. Bake the cake:
  18. Bake in a preheated oven at 300 degrees Fahrenheit for 40 minutes.
  19. Insert a wooden spoon into the oven door to allow steam to escape.
  20. Make the caramel:
  21. Preheat a wide pan over medium heat.
  22. Sprinkle sugar into the pan and allow it to melt.
  23. Continue sprinkling sugar and stirring until it is completely molten.
  24. Add water in small stages until the caramel reaches a thick honey consistency.
  25. Shock the caramel:
  26. Carefully pour the caramel into a bowl of ice water to stop the cooking process.
  27. Make the caramel cones:
  28. Cut parchment paper into 4-inch squares.
  29. Fold the squares in half twice to create a cone shape.
  30. Drizzle the caramel onto the cones, making sure to cover the tip.
  31. Make the espresso extract:
  32. Heat the caramel in a pan until it turns dark.
  33. Add hot espresso to the caramel and stir until the sugar is dissolved.
  34. Make the whipped cream:
  35. Whip 1 cup of heavy cream with 2 tablespoons of sugar until soft peaks form.
  36. Add 2 tablespoons of cooled espresso extract and fold it into the whipped cream.
  37. Assemble the cake:
  38. Spread a layer of whipped cream onto the first layer of cake.
  39. Top with another layer of cake and repeat until all layers are used.
  40. Place the caramel cones on top of the cake.
  41. Chill the cake:
  42. Refrigerate the cake for at least an hour.
  43. Cut and serve:
  44. Use a serrated knife dipped in hot water to cut the cake.
  45. Garnish with fresh fruit, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4I9-0sD-b8I

cassoulet.txt - Cassoulet

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French cassoulet dish.
  • Understand the importance of soaking beans for optimal cooking.
  • Discover the nuances of flavoring beans with pork products.

Ingredients

  • 2 pounds white beans (cannellini, pea beans, or navy beans)
  • 1 piece of fresh pork belly (or salt pork)
  • 1 piece of pork rind
  • 1 tablespoon kosher salt
  • 1 1/2 cups onions, sliced
  • 6 parsley sprigs
  • 2 bay leaves (French or American)
  • 3-4 cloves garlic
  • 1/2 teaspoon thyme
  • 2 1/2 pounds boned lamb shoulder, cut into 2-inch pieces
  • 2 cups browned onions
  • 2 cups dry white wine or dry white vermouth
  • 1/3 cup tomato paste
  • 4 cups beef stock or good brown stock
  • 1 boned loin of pork, tied and roasted, sliced into 1/2-inch pieces
  • 1/2 cup bacon, cooked with the beans, sliced into 1/4-inch pieces
  • Sausage cakes (homemade or store-bought)
  • Bread crumbs
  • Parsley

Instructions

  1. Soak the beans in boiling water for two minutes, then let them soak for one hour.
  2. Blanch the pork rind twice by boiling it in cold water for one minute, then draining.
  3. Cut the blanched pork rind into strips and then dice them.
  4. Brown the lamb shoulder in a pan over medium heat, making sure to dry the meat before browning.
  5. Brown the lamb bones in a 450-degree oven for about 20 minutes.
  6. Combine the browned lamb, lamb bones, browned onions, two cups of dry white wine or vermouth, 1/3 cup tomato paste, four cups of beef stock, and salt in a large pot.
  7. Bring the mixture to a simmer and cook for 1 1/2 hours.
  8. While the lamb mixture is simmering, cook the beans in a separate pot with the pork rind, bacon, onions, herb bouquet (parsley, bay leaves, garlic, and thyme), and salt.
  9. Simmer the beans for 1 1/2 hours, uncovered, adding more water if necessary.
  10. When both the lamb and bean mixtures are cooked, assemble the casserole:
    • Layer beans in the bottom of the casserole dish.
    • Add lamb, sausage cakes, bacon, and pork.
    • Continue layering with beans, lamb, bacon, and sausage cakes, ending with sausage cakes.
    • Pour the lamb braising juices over the casserole.
    • Sprinkle with a mixture of bread crumbs and parsley.
  11. Bake the cassoulet in a 400-degree oven until it simmers, then reduce the oven temperature to 350 degrees and cook for one hour.
  12. Break the crust formed on top of the cassoulet into the beans with the back of a spoon every 15-20 minutes.
  13. Serve the cassoulet with a light first course, a salad, and a dry rosé wine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=f5vciqvJTEo

champignon_sous_cloche.txt - Champignons Sous Cloche

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a classic French dish: Champignons Sous Cloche
  • Understand the importance of using fresh, high-quality mushrooms
  • Master the technique of fluted mushrooms for a decorative touch

Ingredients

  • 2 rounds of white bread, sautéed in butter
  • 1 large mushroom
  • 3 small mushrooms
  • 2 tablespoons of butter
  • 1 tablespoon of parsley
  • 1/2 tablespoon of shallot
  • 1 teaspoon of lemon juice
  • 1 teaspoon of heavy cream
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Instructions

  1. Sauté 2 rounds of white bread in butter until golden brown.
  2. Peel off a small portion from the bottom of the large mushroom to create a flat surface.
  3. Peel off a small portion from the bottom of each small mushroom.
  4. Place the mushrooms on top of the sautéed bread rounds.
  5. In a bowl, combine 2 tablespoons of butter, 1 tablespoon of parsley, 1/2 tablespoon of shallot, and a pinch of pepper.
  6. Lightly salt the cavities of the mushrooms.
  7. Add 1 teaspoon of lemon juice to the butter mixture and stir until combined.
  8. Fill the mushroom cavities with the mâitre d'hôtel butter mixture.
  9. Add 1 teaspoon of heavy cream to each mushroom.
  10. Place a cloche or a fireproof bowl on top of each mushroom.
  11. Bake in a 325-degree oven for 25 minutes.
  12. Serve immediately.

chestnut_recipes.txt - Chestnuts Recipes

Objectives

  • Learn how to peel and cook fresh chestnuts
  • Discover the versatility of chestnuts in both savory and sweet dishes
  • Explore the use of canned chestnuts as a time-saving alternative

Ingredients

  • Chestnuts (fresh or canned)
  • Meat or chicken stock
  • Celery
  • Parsley
  • Bay leaf
  • Thyme (fresh or dried)
  • Cornstarch
  • Port wine
  • Cream or butter
  • Sugar
  • Chocolate (melted)
  • Butter
  • Rum
  • Vanilla
  • Salt
  • Pepper
  • Cookies (optional)

Instructions

  1. Peel the fresh chestnuts by making a small incision in the shell and boiling for one minute. The skin and shell should come off easily.
  2. Cook the peeled chestnuts in a pan with stock, celery, parsley, bay leaf, and thyme for 35-40 minutes.
  3. Glaze the cooked chestnuts by simmering them in a mixture of stock, cornstarch, and port wine.
  4. Make chestnut puree by pushing cooked chestnuts through a food mill and flavoring with stock, butter, salt, and pepper.
  5. For a quick and elegant dessert, combine canned chestnuts, melted sugar, melted chocolate, butter, rum, vanilla, and salt.
  6. To make a palissade au marron, line a mold with cookies and fill with the chestnut mixture. Chill for at least 6 hours before unmolding.
  7. Serve the palissade au marron with lightly whipped cream flavored with rum.

chicken_breast_supremes.txt - Chicken Breast Supremes

Objectives

  • Learn how to bone and skin chicken breasts for a French-style "supremes de volaille" dish.
  • Master the art of braising rice, known as "risotto" in French cuisine.
  • Prepare a simple yet elegant chicken breast dish with vegetables and a creamy sauce.

Ingredients

  • 1 chicken breast (about 3 pounds)
  • 1.25 cups long grain rice
  • 1.5 tablespoons butter
  • 2 tablespoons minced onion
  • 2.5 cups liquid (half chicken broth, half water)
  • 1 sprig parsley
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 3 tablespoons butter
  • 1 cup chopped vegetables (celery, carrots, mushrooms, onion)
  • Salt and pepper
  • Lemon juice
  • 1/4 cup port wine
  • 1/4 cup brown chicken stock
  • 1/2 cup heavy cream
  • 2 tablespoons cornstarch

Instructions

  1. Start by preparing the braised rice.
    • Melt 1.5 tablespoons of butter in a saucepan over medium heat.
    • Add 2 tablespoons of minced onion and cook until translucent.
    • Add 1.25 cups of long grain rice and cook for 2-3 minutes, stirring frequently, until the rice turns milky white.
    • Tie a sprig of parsley and a bay leaf together with white string to create an herb bouquet.
    • Pour 2.5 cups of liquid (half chicken broth, half water) into the saucepan, ensuring the liquid level is about 1 inch above the rice.
    • Add the herb bouquet and bring the mixture to a boil.
    • Reduce heat to a simmer, cover the pan, and cook for 18 minutes without stirring.
  2. Prepare the chicken breasts.
    • While the rice simmers, bone and skin the chicken breast.
    • Cut along the breastbone, separating the breast from the ribs.
    • Remove the skin by peeling it off.
    • Trim any rough edges from the breast.
    • Flatten the breast slightly.
  3. Cook the chicken breasts.
    • Heat 3 tablespoons of butter in a casserole dish over medium heat.
    • Add 1 cup of chopped vegetables and cook until tender, about 3-4 minutes.
    • Add the chicken breasts to the casserole dish, ensuring they are fully submerged in the butter and vegetables.
    • Cover the casserole dish with wax paper and then the lid.
    • Bake in a 400-degree oven for 5-6 minutes.
  4. Prepare the sauce.
    • Remove the chicken breasts from the casserole dish and set aside.
    • Add 1/4 cup of port wine and 1/4 cup of brown chicken stock to the casserole dish.
    • Bring the mixture to a boil and reduce until slightly syrupy.
    • In a separate bowl, whisk together 1/2 cup of heavy cream and 2 tablespoons of cornstarch until smooth.
    • Add the cream mixture to the boiling sauce, stirring constantly.
    • Simmer for 1-2 minutes, stirring occasionally, until the sauce thickens.
    • Season the sauce with salt, pepper, and a squeeze of lemon juice, if desired.
  5. Assemble the dish.
    • Check the rice by lifting up an edge of the pan to see if any liquid remains. If not, stir the rice and season with salt and pepper.
    • Remove the herb bouquet from the rice.
    • Place the rice on a platter.
    • Arrange the chicken breasts on top of the rice.
    • Spoon the sauce over the chicken breasts.
    • Garnish with fresh parsley.
    • Serve immediately with hot French bread.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-QHWiF-SdDw

chicken_cocotte.txt - Poulet en Cocotte

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare a whole chicken for roasting
  • Master the French technique of trussing a chicken
  • Create a flavorful chicken dish using aromatic vegetables and herbs

Ingredients

  • 1 (5-pound) chicken
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1/2 teaspoon dried tarragon
  • 1/4 cup chopped celery
  • 1 small onion, chopped
  • 1/2 carrot, chopped
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1/3 cup port wine (optional)
  • 1/2 teaspoon coarse or kosher salt
  • 1 teaspoon dried herbs

Instructions

  1. Remove any remaining feathers from the chicken.
  2. Cut off the hard little thing at the edge of the elbow and add it to the giblet pile.
  3. Remove the wishbone by cutting up right against it on either side and loosening the bottom.
  4. Cut off the neck.
  5. Truss the chicken by bending the wings back and the legs under the armpits.
  6. Use a trussing needle and white kitchen string to secure the legs and wings to the body.
  7. Insert the filling: 1/2 teaspoon salt, 1/2 teaspoon dried tarragon, chopped onions or scallions, a little celery, and 1 tablespoon butter.
  8. Truss the bottom of the chicken by threading the needle through the tail piece, the top of each drumstick, and the point of the breast.
  9. Massage the chicken with softened butter.
  10. Heat a large skillet over moderately high heat and add cooking oil.
  11. Brown the chicken for 1-2 minutes on each side.
  12. While the chicken is browning, prepare the casserole (cocotte) by adding butter, chopped celery, onion, and carrot.
  13. Add the giblets to the casserole.
  14. Place the browned chicken in the casserole, breast up.
  15. Add a tablespoon of butter, 1/2 teaspoon coarse salt, and 1 teaspoon dried herbs to the casserole.
  16. Cover the casserole with aluminum foil and place it in a preheated 325-degree oven.
  17. Cook for 1 1/2 hours, checking every 15 minutes to ensure the chicken is cooking slowly.
  18. To check if the chicken is done, lift the legs up, press a fork into the thickest part of the drumstick, and drain the chicken. The juices should be clear yellow.
  19. If the juices are rosy, cook for 5 minutes more.
  20. To make a sauce, add 1/3 cup of port wine to the chicken juices and boil.
  21. Carve the chicken by cutting around the skin on each side of the drumstick and pushing it toward the tail.
  22. Cut the drumstick in half.
  23. Cut off the wing by following the breast line.
  24. Repeat on the other side.
  25. Separate the breast by cutting it in half.
  26. Arrange the carved chicken on a platter, using the backbone as a base.
  27. Pour the juices over the chicken.
  28. Serve with roast potatoes, French bread, a green salad, and a bottle of red Bordeaux wine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EkuoG_d2KpQ

chicken_liver_recipes.txt - Chicken Livers: Sautéed and Timbales

Objectives

  • Learn how to properly prepare and sauté chicken livers.
  • Explore the versatility of chicken livers in creating both a simple sauté and a sophisticated timbale.
  • Master the technique of making a classic béchamel sauce and transforming it into a rich and flavorful sauce aurore.

Ingredients

Sautéed Chicken Livers - 1/2 pound chicken livers - 2 tablespoons butter - 1/2 tablespoon oil - Salt and pepper to taste - 1/2 cup flour - 1/4 cup quartered mushrooms - 1/4 cup diced boiled ham - 2 tablespoons chopped shallot or scallion - 1/4 cup port wine, Madeira, dry white wine, or dry white vermouth (optional) - 1 cup chicken stock or beef bouillon - 1 tablespoon cornstarch

Chicken Liver Timbales - 2 cups chicken livers (about 1 pound) - 1 cup thick white sauce (béchamel) - 2 whole eggs - 2 egg yolks - 1/3 cup heavy cream - 1/3 cup port wine, Madeira, cognac, or no wine at all - Butter for greasing molds - 1/2 cup heavy cream - 1 teaspoon tomato paste - 1 tablespoon chopped parsley and chives - 1 tablespoon butter (for beurre le sauce)

Instructions

Sautéed Chicken Livers 1. Clean chicken livers by removing any white lines or tough bits. Cut into bite-sized pieces and dry with paper towels. 2. Season livers with salt and pepper, then dredge in flour. Shake off excess flour. 3. Heat butter and oil in a frying pan over medium heat. 4. Once the butter foam subsides, add livers to the pan, ensuring not to overcrowd. 5. Sauté livers for 3-4 minutes, shaking the pan occasionally, until they are no longer soft when pressed with a finger. 6. While livers are sautéing, heat butter in a second pan and sauté mushrooms until lightly browned. 7. Add ham and shallot to the mushrooms and cook briefly. 8. Once livers are cooked, transfer them to the pan with mushrooms, ham, and shallot. 9. Deglaze the liver pan with port wine (if using) and add chicken stock or bouillon. 10. Thicken the sauce with cornstarch, whisking until smooth. 11. Bring sauce to a simmer and add livers and mushrooms. Cook for a few minutes to blend flavors.

Chicken Liver Timbales 1. Blend chicken livers, eggs, egg yolks, cream, and wine (if using) until smooth. Strain through a sieve to remove any filaments. 2. Butter small molds or ramekins. Fill them with the liver mixture, leaving about 1/8 inch of space at the top. 3. Place the molds in a pan of simmering water (bain-marie). 4. Bake in a 350°F oven for 25-30 minutes, or until a knife inserted into the center comes out clean. 5. To make the sauce aurore, bring the béchamel sauce to a simmer and whisk in heavy cream until it coats the spoon. 6. Season with salt and pepper. Stir in tomato paste for a rosy color. 7. Add chopped herbs and stir. Taste and adjust seasoning. 8. Just before serving, whisk in a tablespoon of butter for a smoother, velvetier sauce. 9. Spoon sauce over the timbales and garnish with additional chopped parsley.

Braised Rice Ring 1. Prepare braised rice according to your preferred recipe. 2. Pack the braised rice into a buttered ring mold. 3. Place the mold in a pan of simmering water with a cover. 4. Bake in a 350°F oven for 30 minutes. 5. To serve, carefully invert the rice ring onto a platter.

To Assemble the Meal 1. Arrange the sautéed chicken livers in the braised rice ring. 2. Garnish with parsley. 3. Serve with buttered peas and chilled white Burgundy or white Graves.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=XC5KQ7QMt1k

chicken_recipes.txt - Chicken Recipes

Objectives

  • Learn different ways to cook chicken from a master chef.
  • Explore various chicken preparations, including grilling, poaching, and roasting.
  • Discover flavor combinations and techniques for creating delicious chicken dishes.

Ingredients

Grilling:

  • 1 Poussin (small chicken, about 3 1/2 weeks old) or Cornish Game Hen
  • Olive oil
  • Fresh thyme (whole sprigs)
  • Salt
  • Freshly ground pepper

Poaching:

  • 1 Boiling Hen or Stewing Fowl (15-20 weeks old)
  • Chopped smoky bacon
  • Chopped mushrooms
  • Ground bacon (paste)
  • Chopped fresh tarragon
  • Salt
  • Freshly ground pepper
  • Cheesecloth
  • String
  • Bouquet Garni (leek tops, celery tops, fresh thyme, bay leaves)
  • Carrots (chopped)
  • Onions (chopped)
  • Celery (chopped)
  • Salt
  • Potatoes (small, whole)
  • Turnips (whole)
  • More mushrooms (whole)
  • Carrots (soaked in water)
  • Leeks (trimmed and cut in half)
  • Fresh tarragon
  • Fresh thyme

Roasting:

  • 1 Roasting Chicken (about 10 1/2 weeks old)
  • Salt
  • Freshly ground pepper
  • Garlic cloves (unpeeled)
  • Lemon (fresh)
  • String
  • Fresh rosemary
  • Olive oil
  • Chicken fat
  • Watercress
  • Garlic (pureed)
  • Chicken juices
  • Walnut oil
  • Salt
  • Freshly ground pepper

Instructions

Grilled Poussin:

  1. Flatten the poussin by cutting out the backbone with poultry shears.
  2. Truss the wings and legs to hold them in place.
  3. Marinate the poussin in olive oil and fresh thyme for one hour.
  4. Season the poussin with salt and freshly ground pepper.
  5. Grill the poussin breast-side down for five minutes.
  6. Turn over and cook for ten minutes on the bone side.
  7. Five minutes before the poussin is cooked, add the marinated thyme to the fire for smoky flavor.

Poached Chicken:

  1. Prepare the stuffing by mixing chopped bacon, mushrooms, ground bacon paste, and tarragon. Season with salt and pepper.
  2. Stuff the chicken by pushing the stuffing under the skin of the breast and legs.
  3. Wrap the chicken in cheesecloth and tie it securely, leaving a handle for easy removal.
  4. Marinate the stuffed chicken for one hour.
  5. Prepare a bouquet garni by tying together leek tops, celery tops, thyme, and bay leaves.
  6. Place the bouquet garni, chicken, chopped carrots, onions, and celery in a pot.
  7. Add salt to the water and bring to a gentle simmer.
  8. Poach the chicken for three hours.
  9. Remove the chicken from the poaching liquid and drain.
  10. Replace the old vegetables with new ones (potatoes, turnips, mushrooms, carrots, and leeks) for garnish.
  11. Poach the vegetables until tender.
  12. Remove the cheesecloth from the chicken.
  13. Garnish the plate with the poached vegetables and decorate with tarragon.
  14. Spoon some of the hot broth over the chicken and vegetables.

Roasted Chicken:

  1. Remove the fat from the chicken cavity and set aside.
  2. Season the cavity with salt and pepper.
  3. Add unpeeled garlic cloves and lemon wedges to the cavity.
  4. Truss the chicken using a string.
  5. Place half the garlic and rosemary in the bottom of a casserole dish.
  6. Rub lemon juice and olive oil over the chicken.
  7. Place the chicken in the casserole dish.
  8. Add the remaining garlic, rosemary, and lemon wedges.
  9. Cover the chicken and roast in the oven.
  10. Uncover the chicken for the last 15 minutes of cooking to crisp the skin.
  11. Remove the trussing string.
  12. Carve the chicken and serve with a watercress salad dressed with garlic, chicken juices, walnut oil, salt, and pepper.
  13. Garnish the salad with cooked garlic cloves.
  14. Serve with the de-fatted and heated roasting juices.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MkuNWExW-1g

Instructions

chocolate_buttercream_frosting.txt - Chocolate Buttercream Frosting

Objectives

  • Learn how to melt chocolate for decorations
  • Create a French chocolate buttercream frosting
  • Decorate a cake with chocolate leaves, cigarettes, and other designs

Ingredients

French Chocolate Buttercream

  • 2/3 cup sugar
  • 3 tablespoons water
  • 3 egg yolks
  • 1 egg
  • 2 sticks unsalted butter, softened
  • 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
  • 2 ounces melted chocolate

Chocolate Decorations

  • 4 ounces semi-sweet chocolate
  • 1 ounce bitter chocolate
  • Melted couverture chocolate
  • Almond paste
  • Fondant
  • Glucose
  • Food coloring

Instructions

  1. Melt the chocolate. Combine 4 ounces of semi-sweet chocolate and 1 ounce of bitter chocolate. Melt slowly in a warming oven at 110-115 degrees Fahrenheit. The chocolate should be smooth and liquid.
  2. Prepare the chocolate decorations. Chef Dublieu demonstrates how to make chocolate leaves, cigarettes, and other designs.
    • Spread melted couverture chocolate onto a sheet of parchment paper, making it about as thick as a piece of paper.
    • Once cool, peel the chocolate off the paper.
    • Use a paper cone filled with melted chocolate to create small figures.
    • To make cigarettes, spread a thin layer of melted chocolate on a surface. Slide a knife through the chocolate at an angle, starting at one end.
  3. Make the French chocolate buttercream.
    • Make a sugar syrup by melting 2/3 cup sugar and 3 tablespoons water over medium heat. Bring to a boil and cook until the syrup reaches the softball stage (238 degrees Fahrenheit).
    • Pour the hot syrup into a blender containing 3 egg yolks and 1 egg.
    • Blend until combined.
    • Beat the mixture over hot water until it thickens, about 5-8 minutes.
    • Beat the mixture until cool, thick, and foamy.
    • Beat in 2 sticks of softened, unsalted butter.
    • Add 1 teaspoon vanilla extract.
    • Beat in 2 ounces of melted chocolate.
  4. Decorate the cake.
    • Frost the cake layers with the French chocolate buttercream.
    • Decorate the cake with chocolate leaves, cigarettes, and other designs.
    • Use almond paste, fondant, and food coloring to create additional decorations.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YTIw6wuXAr0

chocolate_cake_le_marquis_au_chocolat.txt - Le Marquis au Chocolat

Objectives

  • Learn to make a French chocolate sponge cake (pate au biscuit)
  • Understand the importance of separating egg yolks and egg whites
  • Master the technique of making French buttercream (crème au beurre)

Ingredients

Cake: - 3 eggs (separated into yolks and whites) - 1/2 cup granulated sugar - 1 cup melted chocolate bits - 2 tablespoons strong coffee - 3 1/2 tablespoons softened butter (salted or unsalted) - 2/3 cup sifted cake flour - 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar - 1/8 teaspoon salt

Buttercream: - 4 egg yolks - 2/3 cup granulated sugar - 1/2 cup hot milk - 2 sticks unsalted butter (softened) - 1/2 tablespoon vanilla extract - 1-2 tablespoons dark rum (optional)

Chocolate Coating: - 3 packages chocolate bits - 1/2 cup coffee

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees Fahrenheit.
  2. Grease and flour an 8-inch round cake pan.
  3. Make the cake batter:
  4. In a bowl of an electric mixer, beat 3 egg yolks with 1/2 cup sugar until pale yellow and forms a ribbon when lifted.
  5. In a separate bowl, beat 3 egg whites with a pinch of cream of tartar and 1/8 teaspoon salt until stiff peaks form.
  6. In a separate bowl, melt 1 cup chocolate bits with 2 tablespoons strong coffee.
  7. Add 3 1/2 tablespoons softened butter to the melted chocolate and stir until combined.
  8. Gently fold the chocolate mixture into the beaten egg yolks.
  9. Gradually fold in 2/3 cup sifted cake flour, alternating with the beaten egg whites.
  10. Pour the batter into the prepared pan, tap to remove air bubbles, and bake for 25-30 minutes.
  11. Let the cake cool in the pan for 5 minutes before unmolding it onto a wire rack.
  12. Make the buttercream:
  13. In a saucepan, whisk together 4 egg yolks and 2/3 cup sugar.
  14. Gradually whisk in 1/2 cup hot milk.
  15. Cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the mixture thickens and coats the back of a spoon.
  16. Strain the custard sauce and let it cool completely.
  17. In a bowl of an electric mixer, beat the cooled custard sauce until smooth.
  18. Gradually add 2 sticks softened unsalted butter, beating until well combined and smooth.
  19. Stir in 1/2 tablespoon vanilla extract and 1-2 tablespoons dark rum (optional).
  20. Assemble the cake:
  21. Once the cake is completely cool, slice it horizontally in half.
  22. Spread half of the buttercream on one cake layer.
  23. Top with the other cake layer.
  24. Frost the entire cake with the remaining buttercream.
  25. Chill the frosted cake in the refrigerator for at least 30 minutes.
  26. Make the chocolate covering:
  27. Melt 3 packages of chocolate bits with 1/2 cup coffee in a heatproof bowl set over a pan of simmering water.
  28. Remove the bowl from the heat and stir until the chocolate is completely smooth.
  29. Finish the cake:
  30. Pour the melted chocolate over the chilled cake, ensuring it covers the entire surface.
  31. Chill the cake in the refrigerator until the chocolate coating is set.
  32. Serve chilled.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZRtqFEtE5dQ

chocolate_cake.txt - Le Gateau Au Chocolat L'Eminence Brune

Objectives

  • Learn to make a rich, buttery, bittersweet chocolate cake.
  • Understand the importance of carefully melting chocolate.
  • Master the techniques of separating and beating eggs.

Ingredients

  • 2 teaspoons instant espresso coffee
  • 1/4 cup hot water
  • 7 ounces semisweet chocolate
  • 2 ounces bitter chocolate
  • 1 stick (4 ounces) unsalted butter
  • 4 large eggs
  • 2/3 cup sugar
  • 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar
  • 3/4 cup cornstarch

Instructions

  1. Combine 2 teaspoons of instant espresso coffee and 1/4 cup of hot water in a bowl.
  2. Add 7 ounces of semisweet chocolate and 2 ounces of bitter chocolate to the bowl.
  3. Place the bowl over a pot of warm water, ensuring the water is not simmering.
  4. Stir the chocolate mixture until melted and smooth.
  5. Preheat the oven to 350 degrees Fahrenheit and place the rack in the lower middle position.
  6. Prepare a 4-cup cake pan by buttering it thoroughly, lining it with wax paper, buttering the wax paper, and dusting with flour.
  7. Separate the egg yolks from the whites, placing each into separate bowls.
  8. Beat the egg yolks gradually with 2/3 cup of sugar until thick and lemon-colored, forming a ribbon.
  9. Add 1 stick (4 ounces) of unsalted butter to the melted chocolate mixture and beat until smooth.
  10. Pour the chocolate mixture into the beaten egg yolks and stir until combined.
  11. Beat the egg whites in a clean, dry bowl until foamy.
  12. Add 1/4 teaspoon of cream of tartar to the egg whites and continue beating until they are seven times their original volume, smooth, and silky.
  13. Fold 1/4 of the beaten egg whites into the chocolate mixture.
  14. Sift 3/4 cup of cornstarch into the remaining egg whites, then fold the egg whites into the chocolate mixture, alternating with the remaining cornstarch.
  15. Pour the batter into the prepared cake pans, ensuring each pan is about half full.
  16. Bake the cakes in the preheated oven for 15-18 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out almost clean.
  17. Let the cakes cool in the pans for 10 minutes before unmolding onto a cake stand.
  18. Remove the wax paper from the cakes.
  19. For the icing, melt 4 ounces of semisweet chocolate and 1 ounce of bitter chocolate over warm water.
  20. Add 4 tablespoons of butter to the melted chocolate and stir until smooth.
  21. Spread the chocolate icing evenly over the tops of the cakes.
  22. Let the cakes cool and set at room temperature before serving.
  23. Serve the cake at room temperature with a dollop of whipped cream, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=x3hk-hdhepI

chocolate_centerpiece.txt - Chocolate Centerpiece

Objectives

  • Learn how to temper chocolate for a smooth, shiny finish.
  • Discover different techniques for creating a unique chocolate centerpiece.
  • Understand the importance of using high-quality, natural ingredients.

Ingredients

  • Dark chocolate
  • White chocolate
  • 1 cup sugar
  • 1 1/2 - 2 cups nuts (almonds, peanuts, pecans, hazelnuts, walnuts, pine nuts, pistachios)

Instructions

  1. Cut chocolate into small pieces.
  2. Melt chocolate in a double boiler or microwave.
  3. Add a small amount of crystallized chocolate to the melted chocolate and mix until smooth.
  4. Test if the chocolate is tempered by placing a small amount on a cold spoon or knife. If the chocolate starts to set in less than a minute, it is tempered.
  5. Spread tempered chocolate onto a piece of plastic wrap.
  6. Create a design with the chocolate using a metal scraper, a finger, or a small mold.
  7. Let the chocolate cool and set.
  8. Peel off the plastic wrap.
  9. Cut the chocolate into desired shapes.
  10. Assemble the chocolate centerpiece by sticking the pieces together with a small amount of melted chocolate.
  11. Arrange the pralines and other sweets around the centerpiece.
  12. Refrigerate the centerpiece for 10 minutes.

Pralines

  1. Combine 1 cup of sugar and 1 1/2 to 2 cups of nuts in a saucepan.
  2. Bring the mixture to a boil.
  3. Scrape any sugar crystals from the side of the pan to the middle.
  4. Continue stirring until the sugar crystallizes and turns brown.
  5. Remove from heat and let cool.
  6. Spread the pralines on a cutting board and let cool for 5 minutes.

chocolate_cinnamon_beignets.txt - Chocolate Cinnamon Beignets

Objectives

  • Make a classic choux pastry with a creative twist
  • Create a chocolate cinnamon beignet with a delicious filling
  • Assemble and decorate the beignets with a beautiful presentation

Ingredients

Pate-à-choux: - 1/2 cup water - 1/2 cup milk - 3/4 stick (6 tablespoons) unsalted butter - 1 1/2 tablespoons cocoa powder - 1 teaspoon cinnamon - 2 tablespoons sugar - 1/4 teaspoon salt - 6 large eggs - 1 cup all-purpose flour - Additional flour for kneading and rolling

Pastry Cream: - 1/2 vanilla bean - 3 egg yolks - 1/3 cup sugar - 2 tablespoons cornstarch - 1 cup milk

Roasted Walnut Sauce: - 1 pint (2 cups) heavy cream - 1 stick (8 tablespoons) unsalted butter - 1/2 cup sugar - 1/2 cup ground or finely chopped roasted walnuts - 1 tablespoon walnut oil - Pinch of salt

Caramelized Bananas: - 2 ripe bananas - 1/4 cup sugar - 1 tablespoon butter - 3 tablespoons heavy cream

Assembly & Decoration: - Melted chocolate - Pastry bag - Strawberries - Raspberries - Fresh mint - Powdered sugar

Instructions

  1. Combine water, milk, butter, cocoa powder, cinnamon, sugar, and salt in a saucepan. Bring to a boil over medium heat, stirring constantly.
  2. Remove from heat and whisk in flour all at once. Stir until mixture forms a ball and leaves a skin on the bottom of the pan.
  3. Transfer the mixture to a large bowl. Gradually add eggs, one or two at a time, stirring until each egg is fully incorporated. The consistency should be soft but hold its shape.
  4. Refrigerate the choux paste for at least 30 minutes.
  5. Lightly flour a work surface. Turn out the chilled choux paste and knead in additional flour until pliable and able to be handled.
  6. Roll out the dough as thin as possible, adding flour as needed to prevent sticking. Cut out disks for the beignets.
  7. Refrigerate the cut beignet disks for at least an hour.
  8. To make the pastry cream, split a vanilla bean in half and scrape the seeds into a saucepan. Add the milk and bring to a boil.
  9. Meanwhile, whisk together egg yolks, sugar, and cornstarch in a bowl until light and frothy.
  10. Slowly pour half of the hot milk into the yolk mixture, whisking constantly.
  11. Pour the yolk mixture back into the saucepan with the remaining milk. Cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the mixture thickens.
  12. Remove from heat and transfer to a clean bowl. Cover with plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least an hour.
  13. To make the roasted walnut sauce, combine heavy cream, butter, sugar, ground walnuts, walnut oil, and salt in a saucepan. Bring to a simmer over medium heat, stirring constantly.
  14. Reduce the sauce until it coats the back of a spoon. Set aside to cool.
  15. To caramelize the bananas, heat a pan over medium heat. Add half of the sugar and let it melt until it turns a light amber color.
  16. Add the remaining sugar and stir until evenly caramelized.
  17. Add the butter and stir until melted.
  18. Add the bananas and stir until coated in caramel. Pour in the heavy cream and stir until the caramel sauce is smooth and the bananas are tender.
  19. Remove the bananas from the pan and set aside to cool.
  20. Whisk the chilled pastry cream until smooth. Fold in the caramelized bananas.
  21. To assemble the beignets, place a beignet disk in a pot sticker press. Fill with a tablespoon of the banana pastry cream. Top with another beignet disk.
  22. Press the beignets together using the pot sticker press, creating a scalloped edge. Lightly brush with egg wash.
  23. Alternatively, place a beignet disk on a lightly floured surface. Fill with a tablespoon of banana pastry cream, leaving a small border around the edge. Fold the beignet disk over and seal the edges with your finger. Press the edges with the back of a knife to seal.
  24. Freeze the assembled beignets for 3-4 hours.
  25. Heat vegetable oil in a deep fryer to 375-400 degrees Fahrenheit.
  26. Carefully drop the frozen beignets into the hot oil. Fry until golden brown, about 2-3 minutes per side.
  27. Remove the beignets from the oil and drain on paper towels.
  28. Dust the beignets with powdered sugar.
  29. To decorate, pipe melted chocolate over the beignets. Garnish with fresh strawberries, raspberries, and mint.
  30. Serve the beignets warm with a side of roasted walnut sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=s1FfMao_3Pw

chocolate_dome_cake.txt - Chocolate Dome Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make a chocolate dome cake using a French technique
  • Understand the importance of proper pan preparation and heat control
  • Learn how to make a chocolate mousse filling and assemble the cake
  • Learn how to make a chocolate ganache and assemble the cake
  • Learn how to make a chocolate ganache and assemble the cake
  • Learn how to make a chocolate ganache and assemble the cake
  • Learn how to make a chocolate ganache and assemble the cake
  • Learn how to make a chocolate ganache and assemble the cake

Ingredients

  • 4 eggs
  • 4 ounces of sugar
  • 1 pinch of salt
  • 4 ounces of flour
  • 1/2 cup of orange juice
  • 1/4 cup of sugar
  • Grand Marnier
  • 1/2 cup of heavy cream
  • 5 ounces of chocolate
  • 1 cup of raspberries
  • Cocoa powder
  • Raspberry sauce
  • 1/2 cup of flour
  • 2 eggs
  • 1/2 cup of bread crumbs
  • 1/4 cup of sugar
  • 1/4 cup of cinnamon
  • Peanut oil
  • Chocolate leaves (optional)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees.
  2. Grease and flour a dome-shaped bowl.
  3. In a large bowl, whisk together 4 eggs, 4 ounces of sugar, and 1 pinch of salt.
  4. Beat with an electric mixer for 5 minutes, until light and fluffy.
  5. Fold in 4 ounces of sifted flour.
  6. Pour batter into the prepared bowl and bake for 35 minutes.
  7. Let cool completely before unmolding.
  8. Make the chocolate mousse filling.
  9. In a bowl, whip 1/2 cup of heavy cream until stiff peaks form.
  10. In a separate bowl, melt 5 ounces of chocolate over a bain marie.
  11. Add half of the whipped cream to the melted chocolate and mix well.
  12. Fold in the remaining whipped cream.
  13. Make the orange syrup.
  14. Combine 1/2 cup of orange juice and 1/4 cup of sugar in a small saucepan.
  15. Bring to a simmer and cook until the sugar is dissolved.
  16. Stir in a splash of Grand Marnier.
  17. Assemble the cake.
  18. Cut the cooled cake into three even layers.
  19. Brush each layer with the orange syrup.
  20. Spread a layer of chocolate mousse on the bottom layer.
  21. Top with raspberries.
  22. Repeat layers 2 and 3.
  23. Cover the cake with plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours.
  24. Make the chocolate ganache.
  25. Melt 5 ounces of chocolate over a bain marie.
  26. Add 1/2 cup of heavy cream and stir until smooth.
  27. Finish the cake.
  28. Unwrap the cake and place it on a platter.
  29. Drizzle the ganache over the cake.
  30. Garnish with chocolate leaves, raspberries, and raspberry sauce.
  31. Serve immediately.

Instructions for Hot Chocolate Truffles

  1. Make the chocolate ganache.
  2. Melt chocolate over a bain marie and add heavy cream.
  3. Refrigerate until firm.
  4. Scoop out gobs of ganache and roll into one-inch balls.
  5. Freeze for at least one hour.
  6. Prepare the breading mixture.
  7. Combine 1/2 cup of breadcrumbs, 1/4 cup of sugar, and 1/4 cup of cinnamon.
  8. Beat two eggs with a pinch of salt.
  9. Bread the truffles.
  10. Roll each truffle in flour, then egg, then the breadcrumb mixture.
  11. Freeze for a few hours.
  12. Heat peanut oil to 350 degrees.
  13. Deep-fry the truffles for 30 seconds, or until golden brown.
  14. Serve immediately.

chocolate_mousse.txt - Mousseline au Chocolat

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French chocolate mousse, mousseline au chocolat.
  • Understand the techniques for beating egg yolks and whites for a light, airy mousse.
  • Learn how to melt chocolate correctly for a smooth, velvety texture.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup chocolate bits (6 ounces)
  • 4 tablespoons strong coffee
  • 4 egg yolks
  • 3/4 cup instant sugar
  • 1/4 cup orange liqueur (or strong coffee or orange juice)
  • 1 1/2 sticks unsalted butter
  • 4 egg whites
  • 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar (optional)
  • 2 tablespoons instant sugar
  • 1/2 pint heavy cream
  • 2 tablespoons powdered sugar
  • Orange liqueur (optional)
  • Chocolate shavings (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Melt the chocolate bits in a heatproof bowl set over a pot of simmering water. Stir until smooth. Remove from heat and set aside.
  2. Beat the egg yolks and sugar together in a heatproof bowl set over a pot of simmering water. Beat until thick and foamy, about 3-4 minutes.
  3. Remove the bowl from the heat and beat in the orange liqueur (or strong coffee or orange juice). Continue beating until cool, about 5 minutes.
  4. Beat the butter into the melted chocolate until smooth.
  5. Gradually add the beaten egg yolk mixture to the chocolate mixture, beating until combined.
  6. Beat the egg whites until foamy. Add a pinch of salt (or 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar) and continue beating until stiff peaks form.
  7. Fold about 1/4 of the beaten egg whites into the chocolate mixture. Gently fold in the remaining egg whites.
  8. Pour the mousse into individual serving dishes or a ring mold. Refrigerate for at least 2 hours or freeze for a quicker chill.
  9. To make the Chantilly cream, beat the heavy cream until it thickens slightly and forms soft peaks. Add the powdered sugar and any desired flavoring, such as orange liqueur or vanilla extract.
  10. Serve the chocolate mousse with a dollop of Chantilly cream and a sprinkle of chocolate shavings.

chocolate_napolean.txt - Chocolate Napolean

Objectives

  • Learn to make a Chocolate Napolean dessert.
  • Understand how to work with phyllo dough.
  • Learn to poach pears and make cranberry compote.

Ingredients

  • 1 package phyllo dough
  • 1/4 cup cocoa powder
  • 1/2 cup melted butter
  • 1 tablespoon sugar
  • 2 cups sugar
  • 1 cup white wine
  • 4 cups water
  • 1 orange rind
  • 1 orange juice
  • 1 vanilla bean
  • 2 cinnamon sticks
  • 3 Bartlett pears
  • 1 cup cranberries
  • 1 cup orange juice
  • 1/4 cup sugar
  • 1/2 cup heavy cream
  • 1/2 cup milk
  • 1 tablespoon ground coffee
  • 1/3 cup sugar
  • 10 ounces bittersweet chocolate
  • 1 cup heavy cream
  • 2 tablespoons brown sugar
  • 2 leaves mint
  • 1/4 cup raspberry puree
  • 1 cup heavy cream
  • 1 tablespoon brown sugar
  • 1 wooden skewer
  • Blueberries
  • Raspberries
  • Blackberries
  • 1 strawberry
  • Vanilla ice cream

Instructions

  1. Thaw phyllo dough in the refrigerator overnight.
  2. Mix 1/4 cup cocoa powder with 1/2 cup melted butter.
  3. Cut phyllo sheets in half.
  4. Place one phyllo sheet on a sheet pan and drizzle with cocoa butter mixture.
  5. Sprinkle 1 tablespoon sugar on the phyllo sheet.
  6. Repeat steps 4 and 5 with two more phyllo sheets.
  7. Bake at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 8-10 minutes.
  8. In a saucepan, combine 2 cups sugar, 1 cup white wine, 4 cups water, orange rind, orange juice, vanilla bean, and cinnamon sticks.
  9. Bring to a simmer.
  10. Peel and core 3 Bartlett pears.
  11. Place pears in the simmering poaching liquid and cover with wax paper.
  12. Cook until pears are tender.
  13. In a saucepan, combine 1 cup cranberries, 1 cup orange juice, and 1/4 cup sugar.
  14. Bring to a boil and cook until skins break.
  15. In a saucepan, combine 1/2 cup heavy cream, 1/2 cup milk, 1 tablespoon ground coffee, and 1/3 cup sugar.
  16. Bring to a boil.
  17. Chop 10 ounces of bittersweet chocolate.
  18. Strain the boiling cream mixture over the chopped chocolate and whisk until melted and smooth.
  19. In a bowl, combine 1 cup heavy cream, 2 tablespoons brown sugar, and grated ginger.
  20. Whip until stiff peaks form.
  21. Drain poached pears, reserving liquid.
  22. Place a dab of chilled ganache on a plate.
  23. Place a phyllo sheet on top of the ganache and press down.
  24. Top with more ganache.
  25. Slice pears into thin slices and fan them out on top of the ganache.
  26. Top with a dollop of ginger cream.
  27. Repeat steps 22-26 to create a second layer.
  28. Top with a final phyllo sheet.
  29. Drizzle with cranberry compote.
  30. Garnish with a sprig of mint and a dusting of powdered sugar.
  31. Serve immediately.
  32. For the fettuccine ice cream sandwich:
  33. Cut phyllo dough into 1/4 inch thick slices.
  34. Remove waxed paper from phyllo slices and fluff them up.
  35. Drizzle with melted butter and sprinkle with sugar.
  36. Bake at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 5-10 minutes.
  37. In a bowl, combine 2 cups raspberries and 1/4 cup raspberry puree.
  38. In a bowl, combine 1 cup heavy cream and 1 tablespoon brown sugar.
  39. Whip until soft peaks form.
  40. Assemble the sandwich by placing a phyllo nest on a plate.
  41. Top with raspberries, vanilla ice cream, and a fruit skewer.
  42. Serve immediately.

chocolate_raspberry_ruffle_cake.txt - Chocolate Raspberry Ruffle Cake

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a chocolate raspberry ruffle cake.
  • Master the technique of creating chocolate ruffles.
  • Understand the importance of proper chocolate melting and cake assembly.

Ingredients

  • 15 ounces bittersweet or semisweet chocolate
  • 1/3 cup + 1 tablespoon all-purpose flour
  • 1/3 cup sifted cocoa powder (Dutch process preferred)
  • 4 large eggs
  • 2/3 cup sugar
  • 3 tablespoons clarified butter
  • 1/3 cup sugar
  • 1/3 cup water
  • 1/3 cup framboise liqueur (optional)
  • 1 cup crème fraîche
  • 2 teaspoons vanilla extract
  • 1/4 cup sugar (for crème fraîche)
  • 5 ounces bittersweet or semisweet chocolate
  • 3 tablespoons hot water
  • 1/4 cup crème fraîche
  • 1 1/2 to 2 cups whipped crème fraîche
  • 1 pint fresh raspberries
  • Powdered sugar, for dusting

Instructions

  1. Chop the chocolate into small pieces to avoid burning.
  2. Place the chopped chocolate in a clean, dry bowl and set it over a simmering water bath.
  3. Stir the chocolate occasionally until it is melted and smooth.
  4. Remove the bowl from the water bath and set aside.
  5. Warm a clean, dry pan over medium heat until it is warm to the touch.
  6. Spread a thin layer of melted chocolate onto the warm pan.
  7. Refrigerate the chocolate sheet until it is hard.
  8. Repeat steps 5-7 to create multiple chocolate sheets.
  9. Triple-sift the flour and cocoa powder together into a bowl.
  10. Crack four large eggs into a bowl and whisk until they are well combined.
  11. Add the sugar to the eggs and whisk until the sugar is dissolved.
  12. Warm the eggs and sugar over low heat until they are lukewarm.
  13. Beat the eggs and sugar with a whisk attachment on an electric mixer until they are tripled in volume and fluffy.
  14. Fold in half of the flour and cocoa powder mixture.
  15. Fold in the remaining flour and cocoa powder mixture.
  16. Heat the clarified butter until it is melted and hot.
  17. Fold a small amount of batter into the hot butter.
  18. Fold the butter mixture into the remaining batter.
  19. Pour the batter into a parchment-lined 8-inch cake pan.
  20. Bake the cake in a preheated 350-degree oven for 30 minutes, or until it springs back when touched.
  21. Let the cake cool completely in the pan.
  22. Use a thin spatula to loosen the cake from the sides of the pan.
  23. Invert the cake onto a rack to cool.
  24. Slice the cooled cake into three even layers.
  25. Combine the sugar and water in a saucepan and simmer for a few minutes until the sugar is dissolved.
  26. Stir in the framboise liqueur until well combined.
  27. Beat the crème fraîche with an electric mixer until it is soft peaks.
  28. Add the vanilla extract and sugar to taste.
  29. Set the whipped crème fraîche aside.
  30. Melt the chocolate in a bowl over a simmering water bath.
  31. Stir in the hot water until the chocolate is melted and smooth.
  32. Fold in the crème fraîche until well combined.
  33. Spread the chocolate filling onto the first cake layer.
  34. Moisten the second cake layer with the framboise syrup.
  35. Place the second cake layer on top of the chocolate filling.
  36. Sprinkle the raspberries over the second layer.
  37. Beat the crème fraîche until it is stiff peaks.
  38. Spread the whipped crème fraîche over the raspberries.
  39. Moisten the third cake layer with the framboise syrup.
  40. Place the third cake layer on top of the whipped crème fraîche.
  41. Refrigerate the cake for at least two hours, or up to 24 hours.
  42. To unmold the cake, place it on a can or canister to elevate it.
  43. Carefully remove the cake pan.
  44. Melt the remaining chocolate and spread it onto a piece of freezer wrap.
  45. Wrap the chocolate sheet around the cake.
  46. Refrigerate the cake for at least an hour.
  47. Peel back the freezer wrap from the cake.
  48. Use a small amount of melted chocolate to join any loose edges of the chocolate wrap.
  49. Dust the cake with powdered sugar.
  50. Serve immediately.

chocolate_souffle.txt - Chocolate Souffle

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a classic French chocolate souffle
  • Understand the importance of proper ingredient proportions and techniques
  • Master the art of beating egg whites and folding them into the souffle mixture

Ingredients

  • 3 tablespoons instant coffee
  • 3 tablespoons boiling water
  • 6 ounces semi-sweet chocolate bits (or 6 squares of semi-sweet chocolate)
  • 1/3 cup sifted cornstarch
  • 1 1/2 cups milk
  • 1/2 cup granulated sugar
  • 3 tablespoons butter
  • 5 egg yolks
  • 7 egg whites
  • 1/8 teaspoon salt
  • 1 1/2 tablespoons sugar (for stiffening egg whites)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 375 degrees Fahrenheit with the rack in the middle.
  2. Melt chocolate:
  3. Combine 3 tablespoons of instant coffee and 3 tablespoons of boiling water in a saucepan.
  4. Heat gently until the coffee is completely dissolved.
  5. Place a heatproof bowl over a pan of simmering water.
  6. Add 6 ounces of semi-sweet chocolate bits (or 6 squares of semi-sweet chocolate) to the bowl.
  7. Stir occasionally until the chocolate is melted and smooth.
  8. Prepare the souffle dish:
  9. Butter a 1 3/4 quart or 7-cup ovenproof, flameproof casserole dish thoroughly.
  10. Dust the dish with cornstarch or cake flour, coating the entire surface.
  11. Create a collar for the souffle by wrapping a large piece of aluminum foil around the dish.
  12. Butter the aluminum foil collar.
  13. Cut ear holes in the foil to accommodate the handles of the casserole dish.
  14. Pin the collar in place, ensuring the pin heads are on the bottom to avoid disturbing the souffle.
  15. Make the souffle base:
  16. In a saucepan, whisk together 1/3 cup of sifted cornstarch and a small amount of milk.
  17. Gradually whisk in the remaining 1 1/2 cups of milk.
  18. Add 1/2 cup of granulated sugar.
  19. Stir over medium heat until the sauce thickens.
  20. Stir in 3 tablespoons of butter.
  21. Combine the chocolate and sauce base:
  22. Pour the thickened sauce into a large bowl.
  23. Add the melted chocolate.
  24. Stir to combine.
  25. Beat the egg yolks:
  26. Add 5 egg yolks to the chocolate and sauce mixture.
  27. Beat until well combined.
  28. Beat the egg whites:
  29. In a clean, dry bowl, beat 7 egg whites with a pinch of salt until soft peaks form.
  30. Gradually add 1 1/2 tablespoons of sugar while beating to stiffen the egg whites.
  31. The egg whites should hold their shape in stiff peaks.
  32. Fold the egg whites into the souffle mixture:
  33. Fold a quarter of the beaten egg whites into the chocolate and yolk mixture to lighten the base.
  34. Gently fold in the remaining egg whites, being careful not to deflate them.
  35. Assemble the souffle:
  36. Pour the souffle mixture into the prepared casserole dish.
  37. Place the dish in the preheated oven.
  38. Bake for 55 minutes.
  39. Test for doneness:
  40. After about 40 minutes, carefully insert a sharp knife into the side of the souffle.
  41. If the knife comes out clean, the souffle is done.
  42. Serve immediately:
  43. Remove the souffle from the oven.
  44. Carefully remove the aluminum foil collar.
  45. Serve the souffle immediately with whipped cream, if desired.
