lobster_thermidor.txt - Lobster Thermidor

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare lobster for lobster thermidor.
  • Create a delicious lobster thermidor sauce.
  • Assemble and bake lobster thermidor for a memorable meal.

Ingredients

  • 3 fresh lobsters (1 1/4 pounds each, or 1 large lobster 2 1/2 pounds)
  • 2-3 tablespoons butter
  • 1/4 teaspoon salt
  • 1/4 teaspoon white pepper
  • 1/4 teaspoon tarragon
  • 1/4 cup cognac (optional)
  • 2 cups quartered fresh mushrooms
  • 2-3 tablespoons water
  • 1 tablespoon lemon juice
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 3 tablespoons butter
  • 1 tablespoon shallots
  • 2 1/2 cups lobster stock (or clam juice)
  • 3 tablespoons butter
  • 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1 tablespoon hot mustard
  • Pinch of cayenne pepper or several drops hot sauce
  • 1/4 cup heavy cream
  • 1/4 cup grated cheese (such as Gruyere or Parmesan)

Instructions

  1. Clean the lobsters:
  2. Using lobster shears or kitchen shears, remove the legs and claws from the underside of the lobster, cutting as close to the chest as possible.
  3. Cut along both sides of the tail between the edge of the tail and the stomach shell, up to the scalloped edge forming the back.
  4. Peel off the underskin of the tail meat, right up to the chest meat, and cut it off.
  5. Gently lift the tail up, being careful not to break the shell, and pull it out.
  6. Lift out the chest meat, starting with a scissor snip at the beginning and gently lifting it up.
  7. Save all trimmings for making lobster stock.
  8. Remove the inedible parts:
  9. Scrape the green matter (tomalley) and coral from the inside of the shell with a spoon and place in a sieve.
  10. Remove the sand sac (stomach) from the head, pulling it out gently with your fingers.
  11. Discard the sand sac and any white matter in a separate bowl.
  12. Pull off the gills from the chest and discard them.
  13. Pull apart the chest meat lengthwise, separating the joints and segments.
  14. Save all the meat in a separate bowl.
  15. Prepare the mushrooms:
  16. Quarter the mushrooms into pieces of equal size.
  17. Sauté the mushrooms in 2-3 tablespoons of water, 1 tablespoon of lemon juice, 1/2 teaspoon of salt, and 1 tablespoon of butter for 5-6 minutes.
  18. Flavor the lobster meat:
  19. Sauté the lobster meat in 3 tablespoons of butter and 1 tablespoon of shallots for 2-3 minutes, until it starts to turn pink.
  20. Add salt, white pepper, and tarragon to taste.
  21. Deglaze the pan with 1/4 cup of cognac (optional).
  22. Make the lobster stock:
  23. Simmer the lobster shells for 30 minutes with a cup of white wine or vermouth, a sliced carrot and onion, a bay leaf, more tarragon, and water to cover.
  24. Strain the stock and boil it down until it has a concentrated flavor.
  25. Make the velouté sauce:
  26. Melt 3 tablespoons of butter in a saucepan.
  27. Whisk in 1/4 cup of flour and cook slowly for 2 minutes to make a roux.
  28. Gradually whisk in the hot lobster stock.
  29. Bring to a boil and add more liquid as needed.
  30. Stir in the mushroom juices.
  31. Make the thermidor sauce:
  32. Combine the sieved tomalley, 2 egg yolks, 1 tablespoon of hot mustard, a pinch of cayenne pepper or hot sauce, and 1/4 cup of cream in a bowl.
  33. Gradually whisk in the hot velouté.
  34. Pour the sauce back into the velouté pan and simmer.
  35. Add more heavy cream if necessary to reach desired consistency.
  36. Assemble the lobster thermidor:
  37. Dice the tail meat into 1/2-inch pieces.
  38. Place the lobster meat, including the large claw pieces, in the lobster shells or a baking dish.
  39. Pour the lobster sauce over the meat, ensuring it is well coated.
  40. Top with grated cheese.
  41. Bake the lobster thermidor:
  42. Preheat the oven to 425 degrees Fahrenheit.
  43. Bake the lobster thermidor for 20-25 minutes, until the sauce is bubbling and the cheese is browned.
  44. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Q-WmnEwjptY

martha_stewart_almond_wedding_cake.txt - Martha Stewart's Almond Wedding Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make Martha Stewart's almond wedding cake.
  • Understand the process of making marzipan fruit decorations.
  • Learn to make a delicious buttercream frosting.

Ingredients

Almond Cake

  • 9.5 ounces almond paste
  • 1 cup granulated sugar
  • 18 tablespoons (2 sticks + 2 tablespoons) unsalted butter
  • 6 large eggs
  • 1 cup cake flour

Marzipan Fruits

  • 1 pound almond paste
  • 1 pound confectioners' sugar, sifted
  • 1/3 cup Karo syrup

Buttercream Frosting

  • 16 egg yolks
  • 2 pounds unsalted butter, softened
  • 2 cups sugar
  • 1 1/2 cups cold water
  • 1/2 tablespoon vanilla extract
  • 1/2 tablespoon dark rum

Instructions

  1. In a food processor, combine the almond paste, granulated sugar, and butter. Process until smooth.
  2. Transfer the mixture to the bowl of an electric mixer. Add the eggs one at a time and mix until smooth.
  3. Sift the cake flour and gradually add it to the batter, folding it in until just combined.
  4. Grease and flour a small diamond-shaped baking pan. Line the bottom with parchment paper.
  5. Pour the batter into the prepared pan and smooth the top.
  6. Bake in a preheated 300-325 degree oven for 1 1/2 to 2 hours, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
  7. Let the cake cool completely before frosting.

Marzipan Fruits

  1. In a food processor, combine the almond paste, confectioners' sugar, and Karo syrup. Process until smooth.
  2. Turn the mixture out onto a work surface and knead until it is well combined.
  3. Wrap the marzipan in plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours or overnight.
  4. To make the cherries, roll a small amount of marzipan into a ball. Using the edge of a knife, make indentations to resemble a cherry.
  5. Use a tool to make the cherry stem.
  6. To make the raspberries, roll a smaller amount of marzipan into a ball. Use the fine side of a grater to make indentations.
  7. Use a tool to create a top for the raspberry.
  8. To make the leaves, roll out a thin piece of marzipan. Use leaf cutters to shape the leaves.
  9. Use a rubber leaf with veining to create realistic veins on the leaves.
  10. To make the stems, roll out thin snakes of marzipan and taper them at one end.
  11. Use powdered food coloring to add color to the marzipan fruits and leaves.

Buttercream Frosting

  1. Strain the egg yolks through a fine-mesh sieve to remove any lumps.
  2. In the bowl of an electric mixer, beat the egg yolks until light and frothy.
  3. In a saucepan, combine the sugar and water. Heat over medium-high heat until the sugar syrup reaches 239 degrees Fahrenheit.
  4. Slowly pour the hot syrup into the beaten egg yolks while the mixer is running.
  5. Add a bowl of ice water to the mixer bowl to cool the mixture.
  6. Add the softened butter to the egg yolk mixture, beating until smooth and creamy.
  7. Stir in the vanilla extract and rum.
  8. Clean the mixer bowl and beaters thoroughly.
  9. Stir the frosting again with a rubber spatula to ensure it is well combined.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eNGlJ6IFt8M

meringues.txt - Meringues

Objectives

  • Learn how to make classic meringues with different shapes and flavors.
  • Understand the importance of proper beating and baking techniques for meringues.
  • Explore various applications of meringues in desserts, such as meringue sandwiches and Napoleons.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup egg whites (about 4 large egg whites)
  • 1 pinch salt
  • 2 cups granulated sugar
  • 1/2 cup cocoa powder
  • 1/2 cup powdered sugar
  • 1/2 cup sweetened coconut flakes
  • 1 teaspoon gelatin
  • 1/4 cup very cold water
  • 2 tablespoons rum
  • 3/4 cup sugar
  • Caramelized pecans
  • 6 egg yolks
  • 1 cup heavy cream
  • 4 ounces egg whites
  • 1 cup sugar
  • 3 sticks (3/4 pound) unsalted butter
  • 5 ounces semisweet chocolate
  • Fresh raspberries
  • Sprig of mint
  • Kiwi fruit
  • Pink papaya
  • Mango
  • Regular papaya
  • Starfruit
  • Strawberries
  • Whipped cream flavored with rum and powdered sugar

Instructions

  1. In a clean mixer bowl, add 1 cup of egg whites and a pinch of salt.
  2. Beat the egg whites on medium speed until soft peaks form.
  3. Gradually add 1 1/2 cups of sugar while beating.
  4. Once the meringue stiffens, add the remaining 1/2 cup of sugar and continue beating until stiff peaks form.
  5. To test if the meringue is done, insert the whisk into the meringue. It should hold its shape and be shiny.
  6. Transfer the meringue to a pastry bag fitted with a star tip.
  7. Pipe different shapes of meringues onto a parchment-lined baking sheet.
  8. Bake in a preheated oven at 200 degrees Fahrenheit for 30-45 minutes, or until dry and slightly crisp.
  9. For chocolate meringues, fold 1/2 cup of sifted cocoa powder and 1/2 cup of powdered sugar into the meringue.
  10. Pipe the chocolate meringue onto a parchment-lined baking sheet and bake as instructed.
  11. To make coconut meringues, fold 1/2 cup of sweetened coconut flakes into the meringue.
  12. Spread the coconut meringue onto a floured and buttered baking sheet using a template.
  13. Sprinkle with sesame seeds before baking.
  14. Bake in a preheated oven at 325 degrees Fahrenheit for 5 minutes, or until lightly golden.
  15. To make caramel mousse, heat 3/4 cup of sugar in a heavy-bottomed pan over high heat, stirring constantly until it melts and turns a dark amber color.
  16. While the sugar is melting, sprinkle 1 teaspoon of gelatin over 1/4 cup of very cold water.
  17. Once the sugar is caramelized, remove it from the heat and add the gelatin mixture.
  18. In a mixer bowl, beat 6 egg yolks until pale.
  19. Gradually add the caramelized sugar mixture to the egg yolks while beating on low speed.
  20. Whip 1 cup of heavy cream until soft peaks form.
  21. Fold the caramel mixture into the whipped cream.
  22. Refrigerate the caramel mousse for at least 1 hour.
  23. To make Swiss meringue buttercream, cook 4 ounces of egg whites and 1 cup of sugar in a saucepan over medium heat, stirring constantly until the sugar dissolves and the mixture is warm to the touch.
  24. Beat the cooked egg white mixture using a hand-held mixer until stiff peaks form.
  25. While beating on low speed, gradually add 3 sticks of unsalted butter to the meringue.
  26. Once the butter is incorporated, add 5 ounces of chopped semisweet chocolate and whisk until smooth.
  27. To assemble the meringue sandwiches, pipe Swiss meringue buttercream onto a plain meringue cookie.
  28. Top with another plain meringue cookie.
  29. To assemble the chocolate meringue shells, sprinkle one side of a chocolate meringue shell with cocoa powder and the other side with powdered sugar.
  30. Fill the shell with caramel mousse, pecan pralines, and fresh raspberries.
  31. Garnish with a sprig of mint.
  32. To assemble the Napoleon, place a wafer cookie on a plate.
  33. Top with a spoonful of rum-flavored whipped cream.
  34. Arrange assorted fruits, such as kiwi, papaya, mango, starfruit, and strawberries, on top of the cream.
  35. Top with another wafer cookie and repeat the process until desired layers are achieved.
  36. Finish with a sprinkle of powdered sugar and a sprig of mint.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kMOm6Yk2BT0

minty_sweet_and_sour_eggplant.txt - Minty Sweet and Sour Eggplant

Objectives

  • Learn to make a sweet and sour eggplant dish with a minty twist.
  • Understand the importance of using the right type of eggplant for this recipe.
  • Learn how to broil eggplant for a less oily and more flavorful result.

Ingredients

  • 1 eggplant (Japanese, Italian, or regular)
  • 3 tablespoons lemon juice
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1/4 teaspoon cayenne pepper
  • 2 tablespoons sugar
  • 1 tablespoon ground roasted cumin seeds
  • 1 tablespoon chopped mint
  • Olive oil or peanut oil

Instructions

  1. Cut the eggplant at a slight diagonal into slices about 1/3 inch thick.
  2. Brush each eggplant slice with a little olive oil or peanut oil on one side only.
  3. Sprinkle a little kosher salt and black pepper on the oiled side of each eggplant slice.
  4. Broil the eggplant slices until nicely browned on both sides, turning them over once they're browned.
  5. In a bowl, combine the lemon juice, salt, cayenne pepper, sugar, and ground roasted cumin seeds.
  6. Mix well until the sugar is dissolved.
  7. Add the chopped mint to the sauce and mix.
  8. Arrange the broiled eggplant slices in a shallow baking dish, overlapping them slightly to create layers.
  9. Drizzle a little of the sauce over each layer.
  10. Cover the baking dish with foil and let it sit until guests are almost ready to dine.
  11. Twenty minutes before serving, bake the eggplant at 350°F until heated through and the flavors have melded.
  12. Serve immediately, being careful of the steam.

mixed_game_grill.txt - Mixed Game Grill

Objectives

  • Learn how to create a mixed game grill with quail, venison, rabbit sausage, and duck liver.
  • Understand the importance of marinades in tenderizing and enhancing flavor.
  • Master the art of grilling with indirect heat for even cooking.

Ingredients

Quail: - 2-3 quail (bone-in or boneless) - 1/4 cup olive oil - 1/4 cup low-sodium soy sauce - 1/4 cup maple syrup - 1 orange (juiced and zested) - 1 lemon (juiced and zested) - 2 bay leaves - 1 tablespoon peppercorns - 1 tablespoon juniper berries

Venison: - 1 venison rack (French-style) - 1 tablespoon of chili paste (made with dried chipotle peppers) - 2 cloves of garlic - Kosher salt - Olive oil

Rabbit Sausage: - 1 pound of rabbit meat - 1/4 pound pork fatback - 1 tablespoon ground cumin - 1/2 teaspoon cayenne pepper - 1/4 cup chopped cilantro - Kosher salt - Black pepper - 1/4 cup port wine - Hog casing (or sheep casing) - String

Berry Relish: - 1 pound of red and black currants - 1/4 cup port wine - Brown sugar (to taste) - 1 orange (juiced and zested) - 1 lemon (juiced and zested) - 1 inch of ginger (grated) - 1 teaspoon cayenne pepper

Home-Fried Potatoes: - Small potatoes (enough to serve) - Olive oil - Butter - Vidalia onions (diced) - Kosher salt - Black pepper - Paprika - Fresh thyme

Instructions

  1. Marinate the quail: Combine olive oil, soy sauce, maple syrup, orange juice and zest, lemon juice and zest, bay leaves, peppercorns, and juniper berries in a bowl. Add the quail and marinate for at least a couple of hours, or overnight.
  2. Prepare the venison: Remove the silver skin from the venison rack. Combine the chili paste and garlic in a bowl. Spread the paste over the venison rack and marinate overnight.
  3. Make the rabbit sausage: Bone the rabbit leg. Dice the rabbit meat and pork fatback into small pieces. Grind the rabbit meat and pork fatback together. Mix in cumin, cayenne pepper, cilantro, salt, pepper, and port wine. Stuff the mixture into the casing, tying off the ends with string.
  4. Prepare the berry relish: Combine the currants, port wine, brown sugar, orange juice and zest, lemon juice and zest, ginger, and cayenne pepper in a saucepan. Bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer until the berries begin to pop. Remove from heat and let cool.
  5. Prepare the home-fried potatoes: Boil the potatoes for 10-12 minutes until firm. Cut the potatoes into wedges. Dice the Vidalia onions.
  6. Grill the meat: Build a fire in the grill with charcoal briquettes on either side to create indirect heat. Oil the grill grate. Season the venison rack, quail, and rabbit sausages with salt and pepper. Place the venison rack on one side of the grill, quail on the other, and rabbit sausage on the side with the fire. Close the lid and cook for 10 minutes.
  7. Smoke the meat: Add soaked hickory wood chips to the grill. Close the lid and continue to cook until the sausages are firm and the livers are cooked through.
  8. Finish the venison: Move the venison rack closer to the fire to finish cooking. Remove the other meats from the grill.
  9. Sauté the onions and potatoes: Heat olive oil in a pan over medium heat. Sauté the onions until golden brown and caramelized. In a separate pan, heat olive oil and butter. Sauté the potatoes until golden brown and crispy.
  10. Combine the onions and potatoes: Add the onions to the potatoes. Stir to combine. Season with salt, pepper, paprika, and fresh thyme.
  11. Serve: Serve the venison, quail, rabbit sausage, and duck liver with the berry relish, home-fried potatoes, and a jus made from reduced red wine, shallots, and veal stock.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Yk3_FEfgEfg

mousseline_de_poisson_a_la_marechale.txt - Mousseline de Poisson à la Maréchale

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French fish mousseline dish
  • Discover a unique way to cook fish that results in a tender and flavorful texture
  • Master the art of making a white butter sauce, a flavorful and elegant accompaniment to fish

Ingredients

  • 1 1/2 cups ground lean white fish (flounder, whiting, or baby halibut)
  • 1 egg white
  • 3-6 tablespoons heavy cream
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 1/4 teaspoon white pepper
  • Pinch of nutmeg
  • 1/4 cup white wine vinegar
  • 1/4 cup dry white wine or dry white vermouth
  • 1/4 cup lemon juice
  • 1 tablespoon minced shallot or green onion
  • 1/2 pound unsalted butter, cut into 1-tablespoon pieces
  • Creamed diced mushrooms (optional)
  • Asparagus (fresh or frozen)

Instructions

  1. Grind the fish fillets using an electric meat grinder or food mill until finely ground.
  2. In a chilled bowl, combine the ground fish with the egg white and beat vigorously for 2-3 minutes until the mixture starts to hold its shape.
  3. Gradually beat in the salt, white pepper, nutmeg, and chilled heavy cream, adding a tablespoon at a time, until the mixture is smooth and holds its shape.
  4. Shape the fish mixture into 6-8 flat triangles (côtelettes) on a floured surface.
  5. Heat a tablespoon of butter in a saucepan over medium-low heat.
  6. Gently cook the fish cakes for 6 minutes on each side, ensuring they do not brown.
  7. While the fish cakes are cooking, prepare the asparagus by boiling it in salted water for 2 minutes, then draining and tossing with butter, minced shallot, salt, and pepper.
  8. To make the white butter sauce (beurre blanc de Nantes), combine the vinegar, white wine or vermouth, lemon juice, and minced shallot in a saucepan and bring to a boil.
  9. Reduce the mixture over medium heat until it has reduced to about 2 tablespoons.
  10. Reduce the heat to low and gradually whisk in the cold butter, a piece at a time, until the sauce becomes thick and creamy.
  11. Serve the fish cakes on a bed of creamed mushrooms, surrounded by the asparagus and topped with the white butter sauce.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=wT_Ujg2gEy8

naan_bread.txt - Naan Bread

Objectives

  • Learn how to make naan bread from scratch.
  • Discover how to create a simple yeasted dough for flatbreads.
  • Understand the traditional techniques of making naan in a tandoor oven.

Ingredients

  • 2 teaspoons of yeast
  • 2 1/2 cups of water
  • 1 tablespoon of salt
  • Unbleached flour (about 6 cups)
  • Sesame seeds
  • Caraway seeds
  • Green onion
  • Water
  • Butter
  • Vegetable shortening
  • Sugar
  • Rolled oats (quick kind)
  • All-purpose flour
  • Salt
  • Baking soda
  • Buttermilk

Instructions

  1. Dissolve 2 teaspoons of yeast in 2 1/2 cups of water.
  2. Add 1 tablespoon of salt to the yeast mixture.
  3. Gradually add unbleached flour, stirring until a dough forms.
  4. Knead the dough for 10 minutes, until smooth and elastic.
  5. Place the dough in an oiled bowl, cover with plastic wrap, and let rise for 1 1/2 to 2 hours, or until doubled in size.
  6. Divide the dough in half.
  7. Shape half of the dough into 2 round flatbreads.
  8. Flatten the round flatbreads and roll them out to a thin, even thickness.
  9. Use a bread stamp or a fork to prick the center of each flatbread.
  10. Sprinkle water on the surface of the flatbreads.
  11. Sprinkle salt, caraway seeds, and green onions on the flatbreads.
  12. Bake the flatbreads in a preheated 500-degree oven on a baking sheet lined with quarry tiles for 6 minutes, or until brown.
  13. Shape the other half of the dough into 2 long, flatbreads.
  14. Dent the top surface of the long flatbreads with a lot of water.
  15. Sprinkle sesame seeds on the flatbreads.
  16. Bake the long flatbreads in a preheated 500-degree oven on a baking sheet lined with quarry tiles for 6 minutes, or until brown.
  17. While the flatbreads are baking, cream together 1/4 cup of vegetable shortening and 2 tablespoons of butter.
  18. Add 1/4 cup of sugar to the creamed mixture and mix well.
  19. In a separate bowl, combine 1 cup of rolled oats, 1 1/2 cups of all-purpose flour, 3/4 teaspoon of salt, and 1/2 teaspoon of baking soda.
  20. Add the dry ingredients to the creamed mixture and mix well.
  21. Stir in 3/4 cup of buttermilk.
  22. Chill the dough for 30 minutes.
  23. Roll out a quarter of the chilled dough on a flat cookie sheet.
  24. Use a hobnailed rolling pin to give the dough the desired texture.
  25. Cut the dough into desired shapes.
  26. Bake the crackers in a preheated 325-degree oven for 10 to 12 minutes, or until golden brown.
  27. Serve the naan bread hot with a mint yogurt sauce.
  28. Serve the hardtack crackers with cheese or a soft, spreadable cheese.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uUt-uLLypeo

nectarine_chiffon_cake.txt - Upside-Down Nectarine Lemon Chiffon Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to make an upside-down nectarine lemon chiffon cake.
  • Master the art of making a streusel topping.
  • Understand the importance of proper egg white whipping and folding.

Ingredients

Nectarine Chiffon Cake

  • 4 tablespoons of butter
  • 1 cup of dark brown sugar
  • 10-inch springform pan
  • 1 cup of dark brown sugar
  • Aluminum foil
  • 1 cup of sliced nectarines
  • 1/4 cup of toasted almonds
  • 1/3 cup of all-purpose flour (AP)
  • 4 tablespoons of brown sugar
  • 1 teaspoon of cinnamon
  • 1 teaspoon of brown ginger
  • 4 tablespoons of cold butter
  • 1/2 cup of quick oats

Lemon Chiffon Cake Batter

  • 1 cup of granulated sugar
  • 1 cup of all-purpose flour
  • 1 teaspoon of baking powder
  • 1 teaspoon of baking soda
  • 1/4 teaspoon of kosher salt
  • 4 egg yolks
  • 2 egg whites
  • 1/2 cup of vegetable oil
  • 1/2 cup of fresh-squeezed lemon juice
  • 1/2 cup of granulated sugar

Instructions

  1. Melt 4 tablespoons of butter over low heat in a 10-inch springform pan.
  2. Remove from heat and stir in 1 cup of brown sugar.
  3. Place pan on aluminum foil to prevent leaks.
  4. Arrange sliced nectarines in a concentric circle in the pan.
  5. Combine 1/4 cup of toasted almonds, 1/3 cup of flour, 4 tablespoons of brown sugar, 1 teaspoon of cinnamon, 1 teaspoon of brown ginger, 4 tablespoons of cold butter, and 1/2 cup of quick oats in a food processor.
  6. Process until mixture forms coarse crumbs.
  7. Set aside the nectarine pan.
  8. Sift together 1 cup of granulated sugar, 1 cup of all-purpose flour, 1 teaspoon of baking powder, 1 teaspoon of baking soda, and 1/4 teaspoon of kosher salt.
  9. Set aside the dry ingredients.
  10. Separate 4 eggs, reserving the yolks and adding 2 additional egg whites to the whites.
  11. Whisk together the 4 egg yolks, 1/2 cup of vegetable oil, and 1/2 cup of fresh-squeezed lemon juice.
  12. Gradually whisk in the dry ingredients.
  13. Beat the 6 egg whites in a mixer on low speed until foamy.
  14. Gradually add 1/2 cup of granulated sugar to the egg whites, beating until soft peaks form.
  15. Fold a small amount of the egg whites into the batter.
  16. Gently fold the batter into the remaining egg whites until combined.
  17. Pour half of the batter into the prepared nectarine pan.
  18. Sprinkle with half of the streusel.
  19. Pour the remaining batter over the streusel.
  20. Sprinkle with the remaining streusel.
  21. Bake in a 350-degree oven for 35-40 minutes.
  22. Let cake cool completely before unmolding.

new_england_fish_chowder.txt - New England Fish Chowder

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic New England fish chowder.
  • Understand the importance of making a strong fish stock.
  • Master the technique of pan-roasting lobster.

Ingredients

  • 1/4 pound salt pork, diced
  • 2 large onions, chopped
  • 1-2 pounds potatoes, peeled and cut into uniform pieces
  • 1/2 cup summer savory
  • 1/4 cup thyme
  • 1 haddock head (gills removed)
  • 1 haddock fillet
  • 1 cup fish stock
  • 1 1/2 cups heavy cream
  • salt and pepper to taste
  • 1/4 cup chopped chives
  • 1/4 cup chopped parsley
  • buttered and toasted crackers
  • salt pork cracklings

Instructions

  1. Make the fish stock:
  2. Sweat mirepoix (onions, carrots, celery) in a pot with butter, along with bay leaves, peppercorns, parsley stems, and thyme.
  3. Add fish bones and steam for 10 minutes.
  4. Add water to cover the bones and simmer for 10 minutes.
  5. Let the stock rest for 10 minutes.
  6. Prepare the chowder:
  7. Render salt pork in a pot over medium heat.
  8. Remove salt pork cracklings and set aside.
  9. Add onions and herbs to the rendered fat and sweat until soft.
  10. Add potatoes and strain the fish stock over them.
  11. Add enough stock to cover the potatoes.
  12. Simmer for 15-20 minutes, or until potatoes are soft.
  13. Season with salt and pepper.
  14. Add the fish:
  15. Add the haddock fillet to the chowder.
  16. Turn off the heat and let the chowder sit for 30 minutes.
  17. Finish the chowder:
  18. Stir in cream.
  19. Adjust seasoning.
  20. Ladle chowder into bowls.
  21. Garnish with chives, parsley, toasted crackers, and salt pork cracklings.
  22. Prepare the lobster:
  23. Blanch lobster claws in boiling water for 3 minutes.
  24. Remove claws and let cool.
  25. Twist claws from side to side to separate the meat.
  26. Crack the shells of the claws.
  27. Remove knuckle meat.
  28. Pan-roast the lobster:
  29. Heat a pan over high heat.
  30. Add peanut oil or clarified butter.
  31. Place lobster shell-side down in the pan.
  32. Sear evenly on all sides.
  33. Broil for 2-3 minutes, or until lightly charred.
  34. Finish the lobster:
  35. Return lobster to the pan.
  36. Add shallots and sprinkle with cognac.
  37. Flambe the cognac.
  38. Add white wine.
  39. Cook until the lobster is cooked through.
  40. Arrange lobster on a platter.
  41. Garnish with chopped chervil and chives.
  42. Drizzle with melted butter.
  43. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=YJ0nsLID5nI

non_collapsible_cheese_souffle.txt - Non-Collapsible Cheese Souffle

Objectives

  • Learn to make a non-collapsible cheese soufflé.
  • Understand the importance of proper egg white beating and folding.
  • Discover tips for storing and grating Swiss cheese.

Ingredients

English | Chinese ------- | -------- 2 1/2 tablespoons butter | 黄油 (huáng yóu) 3 tablespoons flour | 面粉 (miàn fěn) 3/4 cup milk | 牛奶 (niú nǎi) 1/2 teaspoon salt | 盐 (yán) Pinch of pepper | 胡椒粉 (hú jiāo fěn) Pinch of nutmeg | 肉豆蔻 (ròu dòu kòu) 3 egg yolks | 蛋黄 (dàn huáng) 6 egg whites | 蛋白 (dàn bái) 1 cup grated Swiss cheese | 切碎的瑞士奶酪 (qiē suì de ruì shì nǎi lào)

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C). Place a rack in the lower middle position and set a pan of water in the oven.
  2. Prepare an eight-cup soufflé dish by buttering it thoroughly, especially on the bottom.
  3. Sprinkle the interior of the dish with about two tablespoons of grated Swiss cheese.
  4. In a saucepan, melt the butter over low heat.
  5. Whisk in the flour and cook for two minutes, stirring constantly, until the mixture is smooth and frothy.
  6. Remove from heat and let cool for a moment.
  7. Heat the milk until it is hot.
  8. Slowly whisk the hot milk into the butter and flour mixture.
  9. Return to heat and cook, stirring constantly, until the sauce thickens.
  10. Stir in the salt, pepper, nutmeg, and egg yolks.
  11. In a clean, dry bowl, beat the egg whites until they form stiff peaks.
  12. Gently fold a large dollop of beaten egg whites into the sauce to lighten it.
  13. Fold in the grated Swiss cheese.
  14. Continue folding until the cheese is evenly distributed and the mixture is smooth.
  15. Pour the mixture into the prepared soufflé dish, filling it to about two-thirds full.
  16. Bake for 1 hour to 1 hour and 15 minutes, or until the soufflé is puffed and golden brown.
  17. Allow the soufflé to cool slightly before unmolding.
  18. To unmold, butter a serving platter and invert it over the soufflé dish.
  19. Carefully lift the dish off the platter, leaving the soufflé on the platter.
  20. Serve immediately with a sauce of your choice, such as mushroom, shrimp, or tomato sauce.

oven_roasted_plum_tart.txt - Oven-Roasted Plum Tart

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a delicious and easy plum tart.
  • Understand the importance of using light brown sugar for a balanced flavor.
  • Discover the secrets to creating a tender and flavorful plum tart.

Ingredients

  • 1/4 pound butter
  • 1/2 cup white sugar
  • 2 tablespoons light brown sugar
  • 2 large eggs
  • 1 teaspoon orange zest
  • 1/4 teaspoon vanilla extract
  • 1 cup all-purpose flour
  • 3/4 teaspoon baking soda
  • 1/4 cup buttermilk
  • Plums
  • 1 tablespoon light brown sugar

Instructions

  1. Cream together 1/4 pound of butter, 1/2 cup of white sugar, and 2 tablespoons of light brown sugar for 3 minutes on medium speed.
  2. Scrape down the sides of the bowl to ensure even mixing.
  3. Add 2 large eggs, one at a time, mixing for 30 seconds on medium speed after each addition.
  4. Add 1 teaspoon of orange zest and 1/4 teaspoon of vanilla extract, mix for 10 seconds.
  5. Add 1 cup of all-purpose flour and 3/4 teaspoon of baking soda, mix on low speed to combine.
  6. Add 1/4 cup of buttermilk and mix until just combined.
  7. Spoon 2 heaping tablespoons of batter into each soufflé dish.
  8. Place a plum in the center of each dish and press down gently.
  9. Sprinkle 1 tablespoon of light brown sugar over each plum.
  10. Bake in a 350-degree oven for 24-26 minutes.
  11. Allow the tarts to cool for 8-10 minutes before removing from the soufflé dishes.
  12. Drizzle with bittersweet chocolate sauce and top with whipped cream and a sprig of mint, if desired.

paella_americaine.txt - Paella à l'Americaine

Objectives

  • Learn to make a paella using American ingredients.
  • Understand the importance of rice quality and cooking technique.
  • Explore the versatility of paella and its adaptability to different tastes.

Ingredients

  • 1 pound of pork (fresh pork butt, bacon, or ham)
  • 1 pound of sausage (chorizo, chourico, or Italian sausage)
  • 6 chicken thighs
  • 1 large green bell pepper, sliced
  • 2 large onions, sliced
  • 2-3 whole tomatoes, peeled, seeded, juiced, and chopped
  • Fresh peas, boiled for 5 minutes and refreshed in cold water
  • 1 can of chickpeas (garbanzos)
  • 1/2 cup dry white wine or dry white French vermouth
  • 4 1/2 cups chicken stock or beef stock
  • 1/2 teaspoon saffron threads
  • 1 teaspoon Hungarian paprika
  • 6 coriander berries
  • 1/2 teaspoon thyme
  • 1/2 teaspoon oregano
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 3 large garlic cloves, chopped
  • 1 pound of shrimp, boiled and seasoned with salt, pepper, lemon juice, and oregano
  • Fresh mussels, cleaned and soaked in cold water
  • 2 cups of rice (Italian rice or converted rice)
  • Lemon wedges
  • Parsley (optional)

Instructions

  1. Sauté the pork until browned and rendered.
  2. Brown the sausage in a separate pan.
  3. Brown the chicken thighs in a large pan with pork fat or olive oil.
  4. While browning the chicken, sauté the green pepper and onions in a separate pan.
  5. Once the chicken is browned, add the sautéed vegetables to the pan.
  6. Simmer the chicken and vegetables together with white wine and chicken or beef stock.
  7. Add saffron, paprika, coriander, thyme, oregano, bay leaf, and garlic to the simmering liquid.
  8. Simmer the chicken and vegetables for 20 minutes, covered.
  9. Degrease the chicken and vegetables and add 2 cups of rice.
  10. Stir the rice to ensure it is evenly distributed and not sticking to the chicken.
  11. Cook the rice uncovered for 5-7 minutes, until it has swelled slightly.
  12. Add mussels, chickpeas, peas, and seasoned shrimp to the paella.
  13. Do not stir the rice after adding the remaining ingredients.
  14. Continue cooking until the rice is tender and the liquid is absorbed.
  15. Garnish with lemon wedges and parsley (optional).
  16. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=NduuWpy2gAg

pastry_shells.txt - Pastry Shells and Fillings for a New Year's Party

Objectives

  • Learn to make pastry shells for a New Year's party
  • Explore various savory and sweet fillings for pastry shells
  • Understand the importance of baking pastry shells ahead of time
  • Learn how to make a professional glaze for pastry

Ingredients

Pastry:

  • 2 cups all-purpose flour
  • 6 tablespoons chilled butter
  • 2 tablespoons Crisco
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1/3 cup cold water

Savory Fillings:

  • Béchamel sauce (flavored with shallots, garlic, and vermouth)
  • Diced cheese
  • Chopped chutney
  • Chopped canned frankfurters
  • Ham mix (canned Virginia ham paste)
  • Optional: Additional cheese for topping

Sweet Fillings:

  • 4 tablespoons softened butter
  • 1/4 cup sugar
  • 1/2 egg
  • 1/3 cup pulverized almonds
  • 1 tablespoon orange liqueur (optional)
  • Almond extract (1/4 teaspoon)
  • Apricot jam (optional)

Instructions

  1. Make the pastry: Combine flour, chilled butter, Crisco, and salt. Gradually add cold water, mixing with your fingers until a pliable dough forms. Knead into a ball, wrap in wax paper, and chill or freeze.
  2. Prepare the pastry shells: Roll out the dough to 1/16 inch thickness. Use a cutter slightly larger than your molds (individual French molds or muffin tins).
  3. Butter the molds: Butter the bottom of each mold. Place a pastry circle in the bottom of each mold and press it down gently. Prick the pastry with a fork to prevent it from puffing up too much.
  4. Assemble the molds: Butter the inside of a second mold (if using individual French molds) and place it on top of the pastry-lined mold. This will hold the pastry in place while it bakes. Alternatively, use a twin muffin tin.
  5. Bake the shells: Bake the pastry shells for 5 minutes in a 450-degree oven until they just hold their shape. This is called "baking à blanc" or white baking.
  6. Cool and store: Let the shells cool slightly on the molds, then unmold them onto a rack to allow them to crisp up. You can bake and freeze the shells ahead of time for later use.
  7. Make the savory fillings:
    • Cheese and chutney: Combine béchamel sauce, diced cheese, and chopped chutney.
    • Ham and cheese: Combine béchamel sauce, chopped frankfurters, and diced cheese.
    • Ham mix: Combine béchamel sauce and ham mix.
    • Optional: Add a little egg glaze to the fillings for puffing.
  8. Fill the shells: Spoon the savory fillings into the cooled pastry shells. Top with a little extra cheese if desired.
  9. Bake the savory tarts: Bake the filled pastry shells in a 375-degree oven for 10-15 minutes, until puffed and golden brown. Serve hot or cold.
  10. Make the sweet almond tart filling: Cream together softened butter and sugar. Add egg, pulverized almonds, orange liqueur (optional), and almond extract. Mix well.
  11. Assemble the almond tarts: Brush the inside of the baked pastry shells with apricot jam (optional). Spoon the almond filling into the shells.
  12. Bake the almond tarts: Bake the almond tarts in a 375-degree oven until puffed and brown. Dust with powdered sugar before serving.
  13. Make the cheese straws: Roll out the pastry dough. Sprinkle with grated Swiss cheese and roll up from the bottom. Roll out again and add more cheese. Cut into rectangles and bake in a 425-degree oven for 10-12 minutes, until golden brown.
  14. Make the pastry turnovers: Roll out the pastry dough. Cut out circles. Place desired filling in the center of each circle. Wet the edges of the pastry. Fold the pastry over the filling and crimp the edges. Poke holes in the top with a finger and make fork marks. Bake in a 425-degree oven for 10-12 minutes, until golden brown.
  15. Serve and enjoy: Arrange the savory and sweet pastry shells on a platter. Serve with your favorite drinks and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EOabFyCACnM

pate_a_choux.txt - Pâte à Choux

Objectives

  • Learn to make pâte à choux, a versatile quick-change pastry
  • Master the technique for making puffs, éclairs, and potato dumplings
  • Explore different fillings and serving options for pâte à choux creations

Ingredients

  • 1 cup water
  • 6 tablespoons butter
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 2-3 grinds of pepper
  • pinch of nutmeg
  • 1 cup all-purpose flour
  • 4 large eggs
  • 1 teaspoon water
  • 1 whole egg
  • 2 cups mashed potatoes
  • 1 cup pâte à choux mixture
  • 1/3 cup grated Swiss cheese
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • vanilla ice cream
  • chocolate sauce
  • whipped cream
  • pastry cream
  • chopped nuts
  • pastry cream
  • grated Swiss cheese
  • grated Parmesan cheese
  • minced parsley and chives
  • canned clams
  • shallot
  • vermouth
  • thick cream sauce
  • diced Swiss cheese
  • bread
  • diced ham or crumbled bacon
  • 2-3 tablespoons cream
  • minced clams or diced cheese

Instructions

  1. Combine 1 cup water, 6 tablespoons butter, 1 teaspoon salt, 2-3 grinds of pepper, and a pinch of nutmeg in a saucepan.
  2. Bring the mixture to a boil over medium heat.
  3. Remove from heat and immediately whisk in 1 cup of all-purpose flour, using the flat end of a knife to level the flour in the measuring cup.
  4. Return the mixture to the heat and cook, stirring constantly, until it leaves the sides of the pan and a thin film forms on the bottom.
  5. Remove from heat and let cool slightly.
  6. Beat in 4 large eggs, one at a time, mixing well after each addition.
  7. To make puffs, fill a pastry bag fitted with a 3/8-inch tube with the pâte à choux.
  8. Pipe small mounds of pâte à choux onto a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  9. Brush the puffs with a mixture of 1 whole egg and 1 teaspoon of water.
  10. Bake in a preheated 425°F oven for 20-30 minutes, or until golden brown and puffed.
  11. To prevent the puffs from becoming soggy, make a small slit in the top of each puff and return them to the oven for 10 minutes with the oven turned off and the door slightly ajar.
  12. For larger puffs, follow the same baking and drying process, but reduce the oven temperature to 375°F and dry for 10-15 minutes.
  13. Once the puffs are cool, carefully remove any uncooked pastry from the inside.
  14. To make potato dumplings (gnocchi à la Parisienne), combine 2 cups of mashed potatoes with 1 cup of pâte à choux mixture, 1/3 cup of grated Swiss cheese, and salt and pepper to taste.
  15. Form the mixture into small cylindrical shapes or balls.
  16. Poach the dumplings in gently simmering salted water for 15-20 minutes, or until they float to the top.
  17. Remove the dumplings from the water with a slotted spoon and drain.
  18. Arrange the dumplings in an ovenproof dish, sprinkle with grated cheese, and bake in a preheated 375°F oven for 30 minutes, or until slightly puffed and browned.
  19. For sweet puffs (désire du roi or profiteroles), fill small puffs with vanilla ice cream and top with chocolate sauce.
  20. Fill larger puffs with whipped cream.
  21. To reheat frozen puffs, place them on a baking sheet and bake in a preheated 400°F oven for 2-3 minutes.
  22. To make cheese puffs, combine 1 cup of pâte à choux with 1/3 cup of grated Swiss cheese or a combination of Swiss and Parmesan cheese.
  23. Pipe the mixture onto a baking sheet, brush with egg wash, and sprinkle with a pinch of cheese.
  24. Bake in a preheated oven until golden brown and puffed.
  25. To make croquembouche, fill small sweet puffs with whipped cream, dip them in caramel, and arrange them in a cone shape.
  26. Serve puffs, potato dumplings, and croquembouche as appetizers, first courses, or main courses.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Igmk5iKOn70

pears_macaroon_dessert.txt - Poires au Gratin (Baked Pears with Macaroons)

  • Macaroons (crumbled)

Instructions

pea_soup.txt - Cold Pea Soup with Rosemary and Bacon

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a delicious cold pea soup with fresh ingredients.
  • Understand the importance of sweating vegetables and cooling the soup quickly.
  • Discover the secrets of making a perfect green salad.

Ingredients

  • 4 kinds of peas (snow peas, sugar snaps, english peas, fava beans)
  • 1 slab bacon (or thick sliced bacon cut into big cubes)
  • 1 leek (split in 4, washed, and chopped)
  • 1 sweet onion (or scallion, split and diced)
  • 1 bunch celery (chopped)
  • 1 stem rosemary
  • 1/2 cup olive oil
  • salt
  • 1 teaspoon of MSG
  • chicken stock
  • 1/4 cup Italian parsley
  • 1 ice bath
  • heavy cream
  • 2 cloves garlic (lightly crushed)
  • black pepper
  • white bread (cut into tiny dice)
  • 1 stem rosemary
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 1/2 cup olive oil
  • Dijon mustard
  • sherry vinegar
  • fresh thyme

Instructions

  1. Render the fat from the bacon in a pot over medium heat.
  2. Drain the fat from the pot and add a small amount of olive oil.
  3. Sweat the leeks, onion, and celery in the pot until soft.
  4. Add the rosemary to the pot.
  5. Add the snow peas, sugar snaps, and English peas to the pot.
  6. Season with salt and MSG.
  7. Pour the chicken stock into the pot until it reaches the level of the peas.
  8. Bring the soup to a boil and cook for 7 minutes.
  9. Add the parsley to the soup and cook for another 7 minutes.
  10. Cool the soup quickly in an ice bath.
  11. Remove the bacon, rosemary, and parsley from the soup.
  12. Blend the soup until smooth.
  13. While the soup is chilling, bring the heavy cream to a boil.
  14. Add rosemary, garlic, pepper, and salt to the cream and simmer for 5-7 minutes.
  15. Chill and strain the cream.
  16. Cook the bacon in the oven until crispy.
  17. Grind the bacon into a powder.
  18. Cook the white bread in a hot pan with olive oil, rosemary, and garlic until crispy.
  19. Combine the shallot, Dijon mustard, sherry vinegar, salt, pepper, thyme, and olive oil in a bowl and mix well.
  20. Toss the salad with the dressing just before serving.
  21. Plate the soup and garnish with the cream, bacon powder, croutons, and peas.
  22. Enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oVpG3kxiKkM

petit_fours.txt - Petit Fours

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French fondant frosting
  • Understand the importance of sugar boiling stages
  • Decorate petit fours with chocolate and fondant

Ingredients

1 cup water 3 cups sugar 3 tablespoons white corn syrup Kirsch (for melting fondant) Apricot jam (for glaze) Buttercream (for filling) Genoise cake or sponge cake Chocolate (for chocolate fondant)

Instructions

  1. Combine 1 cup water, 3 cups sugar, and 3 tablespoons of white corn syrup in a saucepan.
  2. Heat over medium-high heat, ensuring all sugar is dissolved and the liquid is clear.
  3. Bring the mixture to a boil, then cover the pan to prevent sugar crystallization.
  4. Boil for 2-3 minutes, or until the syrup reaches the soft-boil stage.
  5. Test the syrup by dropping a spoonful into cold water; it should form a soft ball.
  6. Remove from heat and immediately pour onto a marble slab or jelly-roll pan.
  7. Let cool for 10 minutes, then begin working the fondant.
  8. Use a pastry scraper or spatula to push and pull the fondant until it whitens and becomes smooth.
  9. Cover the fondant with cheesecloth and let it cure for at least one day.
  10. To make the fondant icing, melt the cured fondant with a little water or kirsch over moderate heat.
  11. Stir until smooth and lump-free.
  12. Dip petit fours in the melted fondant using a fork, allowing excess to drip off.
  13. For chocolate fondant, melt chocolate in the oven and add to the melted white fondant.
  14. Stir until combined and adjust consistency with water or kirsch as needed.
  15. Decorate the petit fours with chocolate or white fondant using a decorating cone.
  16. Let the petit fours set before serving.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yzs5MsVGuHY

pickled_onion_salad.txt - Jicama Salad with Pickled Onions

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing Mexican-style jicama salad.
  • Understand the process of pickling onions for a flavorful bite.
  • Discover the unique flavors of Mexican oregano and spices.

Ingredients

Pickled Onions - 1 red onion, thinly sliced - 1/4 teaspoon cumin seeds - 1/4 teaspoon black peppercorns - 1/2 teaspoon Mexican oregano - 1/4 teaspoon salt - 1/3 cup cider vinegar - 2 cloves garlic, sliced in half - Water

Jicama Salad - 1 1/2 pounds jicama, peeled - 1 English cucumber - 6 radishes, sliced - 1/4 cup lime juice - 1/2 teaspoon salt - 1 orange, sliced - 1/4 cup chopped cilantro

Chile-Glazed Country Pork Ribs - 6 cloves garlic, unpeeled - 6 Chile Guajillo, dried - 3 Chile Ancho, dried - 1/2 inch piece of Mexican cinnamon stick - 1/4 teaspoon ground cumin - 8 black peppercorns - 3/4 teaspoon Mexican oregano - 2 tablespoons cider vinegar - 1/2 cup meat or poultry broth - 1 teaspoon sugar - 1 1/2 teaspoon salt - 2 tablespoons honey

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Pickled Onions:
  2. Place thinly sliced red onions in boiling water for 30 seconds to a minute.
  3. Drain the onions and set aside.
  4. In a bowl, combine cumin seeds, black peppercorns, Mexican oregano, salt, cider vinegar, and garlic.
  5. Add enough water to cover the onions.
  6. Stir to mix spices thoroughly with the liquid.

  7. Set aside to marinate for at least 4 to 6 hours.

  8. Prepare the Jicama Salad:

  9. Peel the jicama using a sharp knife, ensuring a deep peel to remove the fibrous layer.
  10. Cut the jicama in half and slice each half into 1/4 inch pieces.
  11. Slice the English cucumber in half lengthwise and then into thin slices.
  12. Slice the radishes into thin slices.
  13. Combine the jicama, cucumber, radishes, lime juice, and salt in a bowl.

  14. Let the salad marinate for 20 to 30 minutes for the juices to draw out.

  15. Prepare the Chile-Glazed Country Pork Ribs:

  16. Preheat oven to 325 degrees Fahrenheit.
  17. Roast the unpeeled garlic cloves in a heavy cast-iron pan until soft and sweet.
  18. Remove the garlic from the pan and set aside.
  19. Toast the Chile Guajillo and Chile Ancho in a dry heavy pan over medium heat for a few seconds on each side.
  20. While toasting, press the chilies flat with a spatula for even toasting.
  21. Place the toasted chilies in a bowl and add water to cover.
  22. Let them soak for 30 minutes.
  23. Peel the roasted garlic cloves.
  24. Combine the soaked chilies, garlic, Mexican cinnamon stick, ground cumin, black peppercorns, Mexican oregano, cider vinegar, broth, sugar, and salt in a blender.
  25. Blend until smooth, adding more liquid if needed to prevent clogging.
  26. Strain the mixture through a medium mesh sieve to remove the chili skins.

  27. Combine the strained marinade with the pork ribs and marinate for at least 4 hours, or overnight.

  28. Bake the Ribs:

  29. Preheat oven to 325 degrees Fahrenheit.
  30. Place the marinated ribs in a roasting pan, adding a little water around them.
  31. Cover the ribs with foil to steam and tenderize.
  32. Bake for 45 minutes.
  33. Remove the foil and baste the ribs with the remaining marinade.

  34. Return the ribs to the oven, uncovered, for another 15 minutes at 350 degrees Fahrenheit to get a nice crust.

  35. Assemble the Final Presentation:

  36. Remove the ribs from the oven and transfer them to a serving platter.
  37. Arrange romaine lettuce leaves, white onion slices, and radish slices around the ribs.
  38. Garnish with fresh cilantro sprigs.
  39. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Fbzgd-uY4sA

pipérade_omelet.txt - Pipérade Omelet

Objectives

  • Learn to make a Pipérade omelet, a Basque country dish
  • Prepare strawberry dessert in cookie cups
  • Learn to make cookie cups for desserts
  • Understand how to freeze and reheat strawberry dessert

Ingredients

Cookie Cups - 1/2 stick (2 ounces) of softened butter - 1/3 cup of granulated sugar - 1/4 cup of egg whites - 1/2 teaspoon of vanilla or grated lemon or orange rind - 1/3 cup of all-purpose flour

Pipérade - 2 tablespoons of olive oil - 2 cups of sliced onions - 1 1/2 to 2 cups of sliced green peppers - 1/4 teaspoon of garlic - 1/4 teaspoon of salt - Fresh basil - Freshly ground pepper - 2 to 3 tablespoons of parsley

Strawberry Dessert - 2 quarts of fresh strawberries - 1 cup to 1 1/4 cup of instant sugar - 1/4 to 1/3 cup of fresh lemon juice - 2 egg whites

Omelet - 8 eggs - 1/4 teaspoon of salt - Pepper - 1 tablespoon of olive oil

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 425 degrees F.
  2. Make the cookie cups:
  3. Cream together butter and sugar until light and fluffy.
  4. Beat in egg whites until thoroughly mixed.
  5. Stir in vanilla or grated rind.
  6. Gradually sift in flour and mix until just combined.
  7. Grease a cookie sheet and mark 5 1/2-inch circles on it.
  8. Place 1 tablespoon of batter on each circle and spread it out to 1/8-inch thickness.
  9. Bake for 4-5 minutes, or until golden brown around the edges.
  10. Immediately remove from oven and place over a greased plastic jar or similar form to shape into cups.
  11. Make the strawberry dessert:
  12. Puree strawberries in a sieve.
  13. Stir in instant sugar and lemon juice until sugar dissolves.
  14. Beat in egg whites until foamy.
  15. Pour into a freezer-safe container and freeze for at least an hour.
  16. Beat again once partially frozen to break up sugar crystals.
  17. Make the Pipérade:
  18. Heat olive oil in a skillet over medium heat.
  19. Add onions and cook until almost tender, about 5 minutes.
  20. Add green peppers and cook for 5 minutes.
  21. Add garlic and cook for 1 minute.
  22. Add sliced tomatoes, salt, pepper, and basil.
  23. Cover and cook for 5 minutes.
  24. Uncover and cook until juices evaporate.
  25. Stir in parsley.
  26. Make the omelet:
  27. Crack eggs into a bowl and beat until just mixed.
  28. Season with salt and pepper.
  29. Heat olive oil in a skillet over high heat.
  30. Pour in eggs and stir until just set.
  31. Top with pipérade mixture.
  32. Assemble the dessert:
  33. Scoop strawberry dessert into cookie cups.
  34. Top with a fresh strawberry.

Notes: - The pipérade can be made ahead of time and even frozen. - The omelet should be cooked at the last minute for best results. - You can serve a rosé wine with the pipérade. - The cookie cups can be made ahead of time and stored in the freezer.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Xc_3jnFSt5g

pita_bread.txt - Pita Bread

Objectives

  • Learn how to make pita bread from scratch.
  • Understand the importance of kneading dough.
  • Discover the different ways to cook pita bread, including in an oven and on a skillet.

Ingredients

  • 2 1/2 cups warm water
  • 1 teaspoon dry yeast
  • 2 1/2 cups whole wheat flour
  • 1 tablespoon salt
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • All-purpose flour (as needed)

Instructions

  1. In a large bowl, combine warm water and dry yeast. Let the yeast dissolve.
  2. Add whole wheat flour, salt, and olive oil to the bowl. Stir until combined.
  3. Gradually add all-purpose flour, kneading the dough until it is smooth and elastic.
  4. Cover the dough with plastic wrap and let it rise for 30 minutes to 5 hours.
  5. Once the dough has risen, punch it down and add more all-purpose flour as needed.
  6. Knead the dough for 10 minutes until it is smooth and has a slight sheen.
  7. Lightly oil a large bowl and place the dough inside. Cover with plastic wrap and let it rise until it is more than double in size.
  8. Once the dough has risen again, gently knead it for a couple of minutes.
  9. Cut the dough in half and place one half in the refrigerator.
  10. Divide the remaining dough into 8 pieces.
  11. Roll each piece into a ball and then flatten it into a disc.
  12. Place the discs on a lightly floured surface and flatten them with your fingertips.
  13. Preheat oven to 450 degrees Fahrenheit.
  14. Place the discs on a baking sheet lined with quarry tiles.
  15. Bake for 4 to 5 minutes, or until the discs are puffed up and golden brown.
  16. Remove the discs from the oven and place them in a towel to keep them warm.
  17. To cook pita bread in a skillet, heat a skillet over medium heat.
  18. Lightly oil the skillet and place a disc of dough in the skillet.
  19. Cook for 15 seconds, then flip the disc over and cook for another 15 seconds.
  20. Continue cooking the disc on all sides until it is puffed up and golden brown.
  21. Remove the disc from the skillet and place it in a towel to keep it warm.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=F0CbwAia3gg

pizza_dough.txt - Pizza Dough

Objectives

  • Learn to make a traditional Italian pizza dough
  • Understand the importance of proper dough handling and rising times
  • Learn a simple method to stretch and shape pizza dough

Ingredients

  • 1 ounce fresh yeast (or 1/2 tablespoon dry yeast)
  • 12 ounces unbleached all-purpose flour
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 2 pounds unbleached all-purpose flour
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 1/2 teaspoon black pepper
  • 1/2 teaspoon salt
  • 1/2 teaspoon balsamic vinegar
  • 1/2 cup fresh basil
  • 8 ounces fresh mozzarella cheese
  • 1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese
  • 1/2 cup mixed lettuce
  • 1/2 cup sliced mortadella

Instructions

  1. In a mixing bowl, dissolve 1 ounce of fresh yeast (or 1/2 tablespoon dry yeast) in 110-degree water.
  2. Add 12 ounces of flour and mix with your hand to create a batter.
  3. Cover with a towel and let it sit in a warm place for 30 minutes.
  4. After 30 minutes, the yeast will have come back to life and the batter will have doubled in volume.
  5. Add a teaspoon of salt to the remaining 2 pounds of flour and mix well.
  6. Put the flour mixture into the mixing bowl with the starter, and slowly add water while mixing.
  7. Continue mixing until the dough forms a single ball and absorbs all of the flour.
  8. Turn off the mixer and transfer the dough to a lightly floured surface.
  9. Knead the dough for 30 seconds.
  10. Place the dough in a large bowl, cover with flour and a towel, and let it rise for 2 hours in a warm place.
  11. After 2 hours, the dough will have doubled in size.
  12. Lightly flour the dough and knead it for a few seconds to remove air bubbles.
  13. Cut the dough into 8-ounce pieces.
  14. Roll each piece of dough into a ball, cover with flour, and let it rise for another 30 minutes.
  15. To stretch the dough, use your fingers to gently pull and fold the dough, turning it as you go.
  16. Continue stretching and folding the dough until it is thin and round.
  17. Place the dough on a baking sheet, brush with olive oil, and bake in a 500-degree oven for 4-6 minutes.

Tomato Sauce

  1. Remove the seeds from a can of Italian plum tomatoes.
  2. Smash the tomatoes with your hand or a fork.
  3. Add a smashed and chopped clove of garlic, torn fresh basil, salt, pepper, and olive oil.
  4. Taste and adjust seasonings as needed.

Panino di Pizza

  1. After the dough has been baked, carefully cut it in half.
  2. Fill with mixed lettuce, black pepper, salt, olive oil, balsamic vinegar, sliced mozzarella, and mortadella.
  3. Close the panino and enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2joowFLBo3w

pizza_with_hot_tiles.txt - Pizza with Hot Tiles

Objectives

  • Learn to make pizza with a crispy bottom using hot tiles in your oven
  • Discover the benefits of using a pizza stone or fire bricks for baking
  • Explore variations of pizza, including pissaladiere Nicoise and socca

Ingredients

Pizza Dough - 2 1/2 cups all-purpose flour (unbleached preferred) - 1 1/4 cups unbleached pastry flour - 2 1/4 teaspoons salt - 1 1/4 cups tepid water - 1 package active dry yeast (or fresh yeast) - 3 tablespoons olive oil

Pizza Topping - Freshly diced tomato pulp - Italian plum tomatoes - Mushrooms - Olive oil - Capers - Diced mozzarella, cheddar, and Swiss cheese - Oregano

Pissaladiere Nicoise - Pre-cooked onions (slow-cooked in olive oil) - Anchovies - Olives (canned, sliced) - Parmesan and Swiss cheese - Oregano - Olive oil

Socca - 3/4 cup chickpea flour - 1 cup water - 1/4 teaspoon salt - Olive oil

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 450 degrees Fahrenheit.
  2. Line oven rack with quarry tiles or fire bricks to create a hot baking surface.
  3. Heat the tiles or bricks for 45 minutes to an hour until they are very hot.
  4. Make the pizza dough:
    • In a large bowl, combine flour, salt, and yeast.
    • Add tepid water and mix until dough forms a mass.
    • Add olive oil and knead until dough is smooth and elastic.
    • Place dough in a clean bowl, cover, and let rise until tripled in size.
    • Punch down the dough and let rise again until tripled in size.
  5. Prepare the pizza:
    • Divide dough in half.
    • Roll out each half into a 14-inch circle on a floured surface.
    • Sprinkle a drawer top or board liberally with cornmeal.
    • Transfer the dough to the cornmeal-dusted surface.
    • Top with desired ingredients, such as tomatoes, mushrooms, cheese, and oregano.
    • Carefully slide the pizza onto the hot tiles in the oven.
    • Bake for 12-15 minutes, or until crust is golden brown and cheese is melted.
  6. Make the pissaladiere Nicoise:
    • Roll out pizza dough into a 14-inch circle.
    • Spread pre-cooked onions evenly over the dough.
    • Top with anchovies, olives, cheese, oregano, and olive oil.
    • Bake in the preheated oven for 12-15 minutes, or until crust is golden brown and cheese is melted.
  7. Make the socca:
    • Combine chickpea flour, water, and salt in a bowl.
    • Whisk until smooth.
    • Heat a 12-inch non-stick pan over medium heat.
    • Pour batter into the pan and spread evenly.
    • Drizzle with olive oil.
    • Bake in the preheated oven for 3-4 minutes.
    • Broil for 2-3 minutes until the top is golden brown and crispy.
  8. Serve:
    • Serve pizza and pissaladiere hot.
    • Serve socca warm, cut into wedges, and enjoy with a glass of wine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1MPhYkPWQeM

poached_chicken.txt - Poularde Demi Désossé

Objectives

  • Learn how to poach a chicken using the French technique
  • Create a delicious stuffing called Albufera
  • Prepare a rich curry sauce to complement the chicken

Ingredients

  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 2 cups mixed sliced vegetables (carrots, onions, leeks, celery)
  • 4 1/2 pound roasting chicken (poularde demi désossé)
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 2 cups stuffing (canned mushrooms, chicken liver, shallots, rice, egg, oregano, salt, pepper, Madeira or port)
  • 1/2 cup plain, raw rice
  • 1 egg
  • 1/4 teaspoon oregano
  • Salt and pepper
  • 1 cup good dry white wine or 3/4 cup good dry white French vermouth
  • Chicken stock (canned or homemade)
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1/2 teaspoon oregano
  • Salt
  • Pork fat or suet
  • 4 tablespoons butter
  • 5 tablespoons flour
  • 1 teaspoon curry powder
  • 1/4 cup flour
  • Heavy cream

Instructions

  1. Sauté aromatic vegetables: Heat 2 tablespoons of butter in a covered casserole over medium heat. Add 2 cups of mixed sliced vegetables (carrots, onions, leeks, celery) and cook for 8-10 minutes, or until softened.
  2. Prepare stuffing: In a pan, melt 1 tablespoon of butter over medium heat. Add chopped shallots and cook until softened.
  3. Add mushrooms and chicken liver: Add canned mushrooms and diced chicken liver to the pan. Season with salt, pepper, and a few drops of Madeira or port. Cook for 2 minutes, or until the liver is no longer raw.
  4. Cook rice: Boil 1/2 cup of plain, raw rice in a large quantity of water until tender. This should yield about 1 1/2 cups of cooked rice.
  5. Combine stuffing ingredients: Add the cooked rice, mushroom and liver mixture, and 2/3 of a beaten egg to a bowl. Stir to combine. Add oregano, salt, and pepper to taste.
  6. Stuff the chicken: Carefully place the stuffing into the chicken cavity. Push the legs back and secure them with a skewer. Place the sliced white meat over the stuffing and cover with the skin. Sew the skin back into place using a large knitting needle and thread.
  7. Truss the chicken: Tie the legs and wings together using a knitting needle and thread, ensuring the legs are tucked under the arms. Secure the tail with the same method.
  8. Prepare the poaching liquid: Add the sautéed vegetables, chicken, giblets, leftover mushroom juice, chicken stock, wine, herbs, salt, and a piece of flattened pork fat to the casserole. Bring to a simmer over medium heat.
  9. Poach the chicken: Cover the casserole with a piece of parchment paper and transfer to a preheated 325-degree oven. Poach for 1 hour and 35 to 45 minutes, or until the chicken is cooked through.
  10. Remove chicken from oven: Carefully remove the chicken from the oven and place it on a platter. Remove the trussing strings.
  11. Degrease the cooking liquid: Skim off as much fat as possible from the cooking liquid.
  12. Prepare the curry sauce: In a saucepan, melt 4 tablespoons of butter over medium heat. Add 1 teaspoon of curry powder and cook for 1 minute. Add 5 tablespoons of flour and cook for 2 minutes, or until the mixture is frothy.
  13. Add liquid to the sauce: Remove the saucepan from heat and let it cool for a few seconds

poached_chicken_with_aromatics.txt - Poulet Poché aux Aromates

Objectives

  • Learn to poach chicken in white wine and aromatic vegetables.
  • Create a simple, flavorful base for various chicken dishes.
  • Explore different variations and presentations of poached chicken.

Ingredients

  • 3 1/2 pound frying chicken
  • 1 tablespoon butter
  • 1 cup dry white vermouth
  • 1 cup chicken stock
  • 1 bay leaf
  • Salt
  • Italian seasoning or tarragon
  • 6 egg yolks
  • 1/2 cup heavy cream
  • 1 teaspoon cornstarch
  • Fresh parsley

Instructions

  1. Cut up the chicken.
    • Remove the leg by cutting through the skin and joint.
    • Separate the second joint from the drumstick.
    • Cut off a portion of the breast to serve with the wing.
    • Repeat on the other side.
    • Cut the breast free from the rib cage.
    • Cut the breast in half lengthwise or across halfway.
  2. Cook the aromatic vegetables.
    • Sauté celery, leeks, onions, and carrots in butter, chicken stock, salt, and a bay leaf.
    • Cook slowly until tender.
  3. Prepare the chicken for poaching.
    • Place the giblets, carcass, drumsticks, and second joints in a large pan.
    • Add the white meat on top.
  4. Add the poaching liquid.
    • Add chicken stock, vermouth, salt, herbs, and more chicken stock.
  5. Poach the chicken.
    • Cover the pan and simmer for 30 minutes or until tender.
  6. Degrease the chicken.
    • Skim off any excess fat from the cooking liquid.
  7. Serve the basic poached chicken.
    • Serve the chicken over rice.
  8. Make chicken aspic.
    • Dissolve unflavored gelatin in the cooking stock.
    • Pour into a mold and chill.
  9. Make chicken gratin.
    • Make a velouté sauce with the cooking liquid.
    • Top with cheese and butter.
    • Bake in a 375 degree oven until bubbly and browned.
  10. Make poulet à la waterzooi.
    • Place the chicken and vegetables in a casserole.
    • Heat the cooking stock.
    • Whisk together egg yolks, cream, and cornstarch.
    • Gradually whisk the hot stock into the egg yolk mixture.
    • Pour the egg yolk mixture into the casserole.
    • Heat until slightly thickened.
    • Garnish with parsley.
  11. Serve the waterzooi.
    • Serve in soup plates with boiled potatoes.
  12. Serve the chicken in aspic.
    • Serve with a green salad.

  • Learn to poach eggs the French way

  13. To make the soufflé base, whisk together 1/4 cup of flour and 3/4 cup of milk.
  14. Bring the mixture to a boil, stirring constantly.

poached_salmon.txt - Poached Salmon

Objectives

  • Learn to poach a whole salmon using a court bouillon.
  • Understand the importance of gentle heat and long cooking time.
  • Discover creative ways to decorate a poached salmon for a beautiful presentation.

Ingredients

  • 1 salmon (5-7 pounds)
  • 2 quarts water
  • 1.5 tablespoons wine vinegar
  • 1 tablespoon salt (kosher or coarse)
  • cheesecloth
  • heavy-duty aluminum foil
  • meat-roasting rack
  • Optional:
    • white wine
    • aromatic vegetables (carrots, onions)
    • herbs
    • mayonnaise
    • sour cream
    • chicken stock
    • gelatin
    • red pimiento strips
    • hard-boiled egg
    • pitted olive
    • green beans
    • sliced carrots
    • parsley
    • dill
    • lemons

Instructions

  1. Wash the salmon thoroughly and check for freshness:
    • The tail should be moist and have little spots for a king salmon.
    • The blood lines should be bright red.
    • If possible, keep the head on for a more attractive presentation.
  2. Wrap the salmon in washed cheesecloth to keep it together during cooking.
  3. Prepare a poaching container:
    • If you have a fish poacher, use it.
    • Otherwise, use a large pot like a turkey roaster or a washboiler.
    • If the container is too small, you can curve the fish to fit.
  4. Create a foil sling for easy removal:
    • Cut a piece of heavy-duty foil twice the length of the fish.
    • Fold it in half and place the fish inside.
  5. Prepare the court bouillon:
    • Combine 2 quarts of water, 1.5 tablespoons of wine vinegar, and 1 tablespoon of salt.
    • If using a plain white fish, add white wine, aromatic vegetables, and herbs for flavor.
  6. Place the salmon in the poaching container and ensure it is fully submerged by 2 inches.
  7. Cook the salmon over very gentle heat for 2.5 hours using three 45-minute periods:
    • First 45 minutes: Heat the court bouillon to just below a simmer (shivering).
    • Second 45 minutes: Lower the heat to very low and let the temperature drop to 140 degrees.
    • Third 45 minutes: Continue cooking at a low temperature.
  8. To serve hot, remove the salmon from the poaching liquid after 2.5 hours.
  9. To serve cold, let the salmon cool in the liquid for 2-3 hours, then drain and refrigerate.
  10. Remove the salmon from the poaching container:
    • If using a fish poacher with a rack, simply lift the rack.
    • If using a pot, use the foil sling to lift the salmon.
  11. Drain the salmon over a tray to remove excess water.
  12. Trim off the tail and remove the fins with shears.
  13. Transfer the salmon to a serving platter or board.
  14. Optional: Peel the salmon by scraping off the skin and brown flesh.
  15. Chill the salmon if serving cold.
  16. Decorate the salmon for presentation:
    • Cover the salmon with a cold aspic sauce:
      • Combine 2 cups of liquid (chicken stock, water, etc.) with 1 envelope of gelatin.
      • Add sour cream or mayonnaise for flavor.
      • Spoon the sauce over the salmon when it is almost set.
    • Add decorative elements:
      • Lemon slices, parsley, dill, red pimiento strips, hard-boiled egg, pitted olives, green beans, sliced carrots, etc.
    • Arrange the decorations to create a beautiful and realistic fish design.
  17. Serve the salmon hot with hollandaise sauce or beurre blanc, or cold with a clear aspic.
  18. Enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=3pou0kDp0Nc

pommes_duchesse_and_pommes_anna.txt - Pommes Duchesse and Pommes Anna

Objectives

  • Learn how to make Pommes Duchesse, a beautiful mashed potato border.
  • Master the art of making Pommes Anna, a delicious potato cake.
  • Understand the importance of using boiling potatoes and clarified butter for Pommes Anna.

Ingredients

Pommes Duchesse - 6 cups mashed potatoes (can be made from scratch or with instant potatoes) - 9 egg yolks - 1 stick softened butter - 1/3 cup cream - Salt and pepper to taste - Pinch of nutmeg

Pommes Anna - 6 cups sliced potatoes (about 2 pounds) - 2 tablespoons clarified butter - Salt and pepper to taste - Grated Swiss cheese (optional) - Melted butter (optional)

Instructions

Pommes Duchesse

  1. Make sure the mashed potatoes are warm.
  2. Beat 9 egg yolks into the potatoes.
  3. Stir in 1 stick of softened butter.
  4. Gradually add 1/3 cup of cream, stirring until the mixture holds its shape.
  5. Season with salt, pepper, and a pinch of nutmeg.
  6. Fill a pastry bag with the potato mixture.
  7. Pipe the potatoes onto a buttered platter to form a border or other designs.
  8. Sprinkle with grated Swiss cheese and drizzle with melted butter.
  9. Bake in a preheated 400-degree oven for about 30 minutes until golden brown.
  10. Serve immediately.

Pommes Anna

  1. Peel potatoes and cut into uniform cylinders about 1 1/4 inches in diameter and 1/16 to 1/8 inch thick.
  2. Soak the sliced potatoes in water to prevent discoloration.
  3. Drain the potatoes and dry them thoroughly with towels.
  4. Heat a heavy skillet over moderately high heat.
  5. Add 2 tablespoons of clarified butter to the skillet.
  6. Once the butter is bubbling, start layering the potatoes in the skillet, slightly overlapping each slice.
  7. Add more butter as needed.
  8. Season each layer with salt and pepper.
  9. Press the potatoes down with a piece of aluminum foil to form a cake.
  10. Cover the potatoes with a buttered lid.
  11. Bake in a preheated 450-degree oven for 20 minutes.
  12. Remove the lid and press the potatoes down again.
  13. Bake uncovered for another 20 minutes.
  14. Drain off excess butter.
  15. Carefully invert the skillet onto a buttered cookie sheet to unmold the Pommes Anna.
  16. Garnish with parsley and serve with chicken or steak.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hc68DPK-xqk

pork_wellington.txt - Pork Wellington

Objectives

  • Learn to make a brioche crust for pork Wellington
  • Understand the importance of slow cooking for tender, juicy pork
  • Assemble a delicious and elegant pork Wellington dish

Ingredients

Brioche Dough: - 1 package active dry yeast - 1/4 cup tepid water - 1/2 teaspoon sugar - 4 large eggs - 1/4 cup milk - 3 1/2 cups all-purpose flour - 1 1/2 teaspoons salt - 1 stick (4 ounces) unsalted butter, cut into small pieces

Pork Marinade: - 1 tablespoon salt - 1/2 teaspoon allspice powder - 1/2 teaspoon sage or thyme

Stuffing: - 1/2 cup cooked onions - 1 1/2 cups cooked ground pork - 1/4 cup dry white wine - 1/4 teaspoon allspice - Salt and pepper to taste - 2 cups cooked chopped fresh spinach - 1/2 cup chicken stock - 1/4 cup fresh white breadcrumbs - 2 large eggs

Pork Wellington: - 1 boneless pork loin, center cut, cut into 1-inch pieces - 1/3 cup chicken stock - 1/4 cup white wine or vermouth - Butter and oil for sautéing

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Brioche Dough:
  2. In a small bowl, combine yeast, tepid water, and sugar. Let stand until foamy (about 5 minutes).
  3. In a separate bowl, whisk together eggs and milk.
  4. In a food processor, combine flour, salt, and butter. Pulse until the butter is evenly distributed.
  5. Add the yeast mixture and pulse until combined.
  6. Gradually add the egg mixture, pulsing until the dough begins to form a ball around the blade.
  7. Let the dough rest for 2 minutes.
  8. Remove the dough from the processor and knead for a few seconds until smooth.
  9. Place the dough in a greased bowl, cover, and let rise for 2 1/2 to 3 hours, or until doubled in size.
  10. Deflate and Rise Again:
  11. Punch down the dough and shape it into a rectangle. Fold the
