tart_o_rama.txt - Tart-O-Rama

Objectives

  • Learn how to make perfect pie crusts for fresh fruit tarts
  • Explore different tart fillings, including yogurt and blackberry, apple, and nectarine and blueberry
  • Master the techniques of blind baking and crimping tart shells

Ingredients

Pie Crust: - 5 ¼ cups pastry flour (or 3 cups all-purpose flour + 1 cup cake flour) - 1 tablespoon salt - 12 tablespoons (1 ½ sticks) chilled, unsalted butter, cut into small pieces - 1 ¾ cups chilled shortening (3 ½ sticks) - 1 cup ice water

Apple Tart: - 6 Granny Smith apples, peeled, cored, and cut into thirds - ¾ cup sugar - 1 tablespoon flour - Cinnamon (generous pinch) - Lemon juice (to taste) - 1 cup fluffy bread crumbs - Butter (for brushing) - Sugar (½ tablespoon, for sprinkling)

Yogurt and Blackberry Tart: - 4 large eggs - 1 ⅓ cup sugar - 3 cups plain, non-fat yogurt - 2 tablespoons vanilla extract - 1 ¼ cup all-purpose flour - Blackberries (as needed) - Toasted almonds (with skin)

Nectarine and Blueberry Tart: - 3 cups blueberries - 2 nectarines, sliced - ¾ cup sugar - 1 ½ tablespoons flour - Lemon zest (a big pinch) - Lemon juice (a little bit)

Instructions

  1. Combine flour and salt in a large bowl.
  2. Cut butter into small pieces and add to the flour mixture.
  3. Work butter into the flour using your fingertips, creating a coarse crumb texture.
  4. Add shortening and work it into the flour mixture.
  5. Make a well in the center of the mixture and add ice water.
  6. Gently mix the ingredients with your hands until a dough forms.
  7. Turn dough out onto a lightly floured counter and knead briefly to incorporate any dry flour.
  8. Divide dough into two portions and chill for at least two hours.
  9. On a lightly floured surface, roll out one portion of dough into a circle slightly larger than your tart pan.
  10. Gently press the dough into the tart pan, creating a slight ledge around the edge.
  11. Chill the tart shell for 20 minutes.
  12. Line the chilled tart shell with parchment paper and fill with rice or beans.
  13. Bake in a 400-degree oven for 20-25 minutes, until the crust is light brown.
  14. Remove the rice or beans and bake for an additional 5-10 minutes to ensure the crust is fully cooked.
  15. While the crust is baking, prepare the apple filling:
    • Combine apples, sugar, flour, cinnamon, and lemon juice in a bowl.
    • Toss to coat.
    • Bake in a 375-400 degree oven for 10-15 minutes, until softened.
    • Mash the apples and stir in bread crumbs.
  16. Spread the apple filling into the baked tart shell.
  17. Arrange apple slices in concentric circles on top of the filling.
  18. Brush apple slices with butter and sprinkle with sugar.
  19. Bake in a 375-degree oven for 25-35 minutes, until the apples are golden brown and the crust is cooked through.
  20. Prepare the yogurt and blackberry filling:
    • Cream eggs and sugar together in a bowl until pale yellow.
    • Add yogurt and vanilla extract and mix well.
    • Sift in flour and fold gently until combined.
  21. Pour the filling into the baked tart shell.
  22. Top with blackberries and sprinkle with toasted almonds.
  23. Bake in a 325-degree oven for 35-40 minutes, until set.
  24. Prepare the nectarine and blueberry filling:
    • Combine blueberries, nectarines, sugar, flour, lemon zest, and lemon juice in a bowl.
    • Cook over medium heat until the juices thicken.
    • Chill to room temperature.
  25. Roll out the second portion of dough and cut a circle slightly larger than the tart pan.
  26. Place the chilled nectarine and blueberry filling in the baked tart shell.
  27. Carefully place the dough circle on top of the filling and trim the edges.
  28. Crimp the edges of the dough to seal the tart.
  29. Brush the top of the tart with egg wash and sprinkle with coarse sugar.
  30. Bake in a 375-degree oven for 40 minutes, until the crust is golden brown and the filling is set.
  31. Serve warm or at room temperature.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ulD728JBKf8

tequila_cured_gravlax.txt - Tequila Cured Gravlax with Dill Pancakes and Tomato Creme Fraiche

Objectives

  • Learn to cure salmon with tequila and lime juice
  • Make homemade tomato paste for a flavorful creme fraiche
  • Create savory dill pancakes for a delicious appetizer

Ingredients

Gravlax

  • 1/2 side salmon (skin on)
  • 2 parts brown sugar
  • 1 part kosher salt
  • 1/2 cup tequila
  • 1/2 cup fresh lime juice
  • 1 lemon, zested
  • 1 orange, zested
  • 2 teaspoons coriander seeds
  • 2 sprigs dill
  • 2 sprigs mint
  • 2 sprigs basil

Tomato Creme Fraiche

  • 1 shallot
  • 1 clove garlic
  • 2 tablespoons oil
  • 4-5 tomatoes (peeled, de-seeded, and chopped)
  • 1/4 cup red wine vinegar
  • 1 cup creme fraiche (or sour cream)

Dill Pancakes

  • 1 1/4 cup all-purpose flour
  • 1 teaspoon cumin
  • 2 teaspoons baking powder
  • 1 cup milk
  • 1/2 cup cucumbers (diced)
  • 1/2 cup red onion (diced)
  • 1/2 cup green onions (thinly sliced)
  • 1/4 cup fresh dill (finely chopped)
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Watercress Oil

  • 1 bunch watercress (juiced)
  • 1 tablespoon lemon juice
  • Olive oil (enough to emulsify)
  • Salt and pepper to taste

Additional

  • Plastic wrap
  • Cookie sheet pan
  • Weights (5 lbs)
  • Sharp thin knife
  • Deep fryer
  • Non-stick pan
  • Olive oil

Instructions

  1. Remove pin bones from salmon using pliers or a spoon.
  2. First Cure:
  3. Mix brown sugar and kosher salt in a 2:1 ratio.
  4. Spread a 1/4 inch layer of the cure on a cookie sheet pan lined with plastic wrap.
  5. Place salmon flesh-side down on the cure, ensuring it's long enough to hold the entire filet.
  6. Add additional cure on the sides and ends.
  7. Fold salmon up on the sides and end.
  8. Weigh down the salmon with 5 lbs of weight.
  9. Refrigerate for 24 hours.
  10. Second Cure:
  11. Combine tequila, lime juice, lemon zest, orange zest, coriander seeds, dill, mint, and basil.
  12. Line a clean cookie sheet pan with plastic wrap.
  13. Pour the liquid ingredients on the pan, creating a bed of herbs and rind.
  14. Add a little more cure on the bottom.
  15. Place salmon flesh-side down on the bed.
  16. Add additional cure on the sides and ends.
  17. Tighten with plastic wrap.
  18. Weigh down the salmon.
  19. Refrigerate for 24 hours.
  20. Remove salmon from the second cure.
  21. Cut off the belly piece of the salmon.
  22. Slice salmon thinly from the tail end using long, thin strokes.
  23. Tomato Creme Fraiche:
  24. Sweat shallot and garlic over medium heat in a pan with 2 tablespoons of oil.
  25. Add chopped tomatoes and cook slowly until all moisture is released.
  26. Add red wine vinegar and continue cooking for 2-3 minutes until a paste forms.
  27. Strain the paste to remove any seeds.
  28. Cool down immediately.
  29. Mix with creme fraiche or sour cream until a nice red color.
  30. Refrigerate until ready to use.
  31. Dill Pancakes:
  32. Whisk together flour, cumin, and baking powder.
  33. Slowly add milk and whisk until a batter forms.
  34. Add diced cucumbers, red onion, green onions, and dill.
  35. Add a tad more milk if needed.
  36. Season with salt and pepper.
  37. Refrigerate for 6 hours.
  38. Watercress Oil:
  39. Juice watercress.
  40. Whisk together lemon juice and watercress juice over ice.
  41. Slowly drizzle olive oil into the mixture, whisking constantly.
  42. Season with salt and pepper.
  43. Refrigerate until ready to use.
  44. Deep-Fried Capers:
  45. Heat oil in a deep fryer.
  46. Gently drop capers into the hot oil and stand back.
  47. Drain on paper towels.
  48. Assemble the Dish:
  49. Heat a non-stick pan with a little olive oil.
  50. Cook dill pancakes until bubbles appear, then flip.
  51. Keep pancakes warm in a 150-200 degree oven.
  52. Place a bed of greens on a plate.
  53. Top with a slice of tequila gravlax.
  54. Drizzle with tomato creme fraiche and watercress oil.
  55. Repeat layers with a second pancake.
  56. Garnish with deep-fried capers and dill sprigs.
  57. Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oVNCgFCVyUg

texas_red_jalapeno_salad_w_shrimp_tamales.txt - Red Jalapeño Salad with Shrimp Tamales

Objectives

  • Prepare a Diablo sauce with mango, habanero peppers, and ginger.
  • Create a Southwestern-inspired Caesar salad dressing.
  • Assemble a hearty salad with corn puree, smoked garlic, jalapeños, and shrimp.
  • Make simple corn tamales using fresh corn husks.
  • Garnish the salad with pico de gallo, toasted pumpkin seeds, and cotija cheese.

Ingredients

Diablo Sauce - 1 ripe mango, diced - 2 habanero peppers, finely chopped (remove seeds for less heat) - 1 shallot, chopped - 2 large cloves garlic, minced - 1/2 teaspoon cumin seeds - 1 tablespoon canola or olive oil - 1 tablespoon grated ginger - 1 red bell pepper, roughly chopped - 1 cup to 1 1/2 cups chicken stock - Salt to taste - Lime juice to taste

Caesar Dressing - 3 egg yolks - 6 cloves garlic, minced - 1 green jalapeño pepper, finely chopped (remove seeds) - 1 tablespoon chopped shallots - 2-3 anchovy fillets - 1 teaspoon Worcestershire sauce - 1/2 teaspoon balsamic vinegar - 2-3 drops Tabasco sauce - 1 cup canola oil - 1/2 cup olive oil - 1/4 cup chopped cilantro - Lime juice to taste - Dijon mustard to taste - Kosher salt to taste

Corn Puree - 4 ears of corn, shucked - Salt to taste - Maple syrup (optional, for wintertime)

Shrimp Tamales - 1 pound shrimp, peeled and deveined (leave tails on) - Salt to taste - 1 flour tortilla - Fresh corn husks - Corn puree

Salad - Romaine lettuce, washed and chopped - Diablo sauce - Smoked garlic mayonnaise - Pico de gallo - Toasted pumpkin seeds - Dried corn kernels - Diced red bell pepper - Cotija cheese

Instructions

  1. Prepare the Diablo sauce:
    • Dice the mango and set aside.
    • Finely chop the habanero peppers, removing the seeds for less heat.
    • Chop the shallot and mince the garlic.
    • Heat the oil in a saucepan over medium heat.
    • Add the shallots, garlic, cumin seeds, and habanero peppers.
    • Sweat the ingredients for a few minutes until fragrant.
    • Grate the ginger and add it to the saucepan.
    • Add the red bell pepper and cook until softened.
    • Add the chicken stock and bring to a boil.
    • Reduce heat to a simmer and cook for 15-20 minutes.
    • Blend the sauce until smooth.
    • Add the diced mango and season with salt and lime juice to taste.
  2. Make the Caesar dressing:
    • Combine the egg yolks, garlic, jalapeño pepper, shallots, anchovies, Worcestershire sauce, balsamic vinegar, and Tabasco sauce in a blender.
    • Slowly drizzle in the canola oil, followed by the olive oil, while blending until emulsified.
    • Stir in the cilantro, lime juice, Dijon mustard, and kosher salt.
  3. Prepare the corn puree:
    • Preheat oven to 350°F.
    • Grate the corn kernels using a large-hole grater.
    • Spread the grated corn in a casserole pan.
    • Bake for 20 minutes, or until the corn has released its liquid and thickened.
    • Season with salt to taste.
    • Add a touch of maple syrup if desired, especially in winter.
  4. Cook the shrimp:
    • Season the shrimp with salt.
    • Heat a non-stick pan over medium heat.
    • Add a small amount of oil to the pan.
    • Sauté the shrimp for a few minutes until cooked through.
    • Toss the shrimp with the Diablo sauce.
  5. Make the tamales:
    • Heat a flour tortilla in a pan or on an electric stove until warm.
    • Cut the tortilla in half and roll each half into a cornucopia shape.
    • Prepare the corn husks by tying the ends together to form a small canoe shape.
    • Fill the corn husks with the corn puree.
  6. Assemble the salad:
    • Toss the romaine lettuce with the Caesar dressing.
    • Add the corn puree, smoked garlic mayonnaise, and pico de gallo.
    • Garnish with toasted pumpkin seeds, dried corn kernels, diced red bell pepper, and crumbled cotija cheese.
    • Top with the glazed shrimp.
    • Serve immediately.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uIPhQYwIz9k

thai_beef_with_rice_noodles.txt - Thai Beef with Rice Noodles

Objectives

  • Learn to make a Thai-inspired beef dish with a spicy marinade.
  • Understand how to prepare and cook rice noodles.
  • Learn how to make a simple chicken jus for a flavorful sauce.

Ingredients

For the marinade: - 1 lime leaf - 1 lemon grass stalk - 2 small shallots - 1 garlic clove - 1 teaspoon of sugar - 1 tablespoon of red curry paste - 1 tablespoon of hot curry powder - 1 teaspoon of turmeric - 1/2 finger chili - 2 tablespoons of coconut milk

For the chicken jus: - 1 cup of chicken wings, cut into 1-inch pieces - 1 garlic clove - 1/2 onion, sliced - 1 sliced lemon grass stalk - 4 cups of water - 1 tablespoon of green peppercorns - 1 tablespoon of soy sauce

For the dish: - 2 seven-ounce strip loin steaks, trimmed - 1 handful of snow peas per serving - 1 handful of Japanese mushrooms (igimeji) per serving - 1 handful of rice noodles per serving - 1/4 cup of rice vinegar - 1 teaspoon of soy sauce - 1 garlic clove - 1/3 cup of tamarind paste - 2 tablespoons of sugar - 1 Thai bird chili - 1/2 cup canola oil - Butter lettuce leaves - Mint leaves - Cilantro sprigs - 1/4 pineapple - 1 banana - 2 kiwis - 1 prune - 3 tablespoons of passion fruit puree - 1/2 cup of water - 3 tablespoons of sugar - 1 branch of thyme - 1.5 tablespoons of kirschwasser - White pepper - Vanilla ice cream - Candied rose petals

Instructions

  1. Prepare the marinade by combining all ingredients in a food processor and blending until a fine paste is formed.
  2. Rub the marinade onto the steaks on both sides and refrigerate for at least six hours or overnight.
  3. Soak the rice noodles in warm water for two hours.
  4. Prepare the chicken jus by roasting the chicken wings in the oven until golden brown.
  5. Add garlic, onion, lemon grass, and water to the pan and simmer for 30 minutes.
  6. Strain the chicken jus and add green peppercorns and soy sauce.
  7. Heat a skillet over high heat and add a drop of oil.
  8. Grill the steaks for 1.5 minutes per side, creating a crisscross pattern.
  9. Let the steaks rest for a couple of minutes.
  10. Saute the mushrooms in a pan with a little oil and salt.
  11. Saute the chive buds in water for a few seconds.
  12. Add snow peas to the mushrooms and saute briefly.
  13. Dip the rice noodles in hot water for 10 seconds to soften.
  14. Arrange the rice noodles on a plate.
  15. Slice the steaks thinly and place them on top of the noodles.
  16. Arrange the sauteed vegetables on top of the steak.
  17. Pour the chicken jus over the dish.
  18. Garnish with chive buds.
  19. Prepare the dipping sauce by blending all ingredients in a food processor.
  20. Fry the spring rolls in hot oil for 45-50 seconds.
  21. Drain the spring rolls on paper towels.
  22. Place a spring roll on a butter lettuce leaf and top with mint and cilantro.
  23. Dip the spring roll in the dipping sauce.
  24. To prepare the dessert, combine water and sugar in a saucepan and bring to a boil.
  25. Add thyme and simmer for a few minutes.
  26. Add kirschwasser and let the mixture sit overnight.
  27. Strain the syrup and discard the thyme.
  28. Cut the pineapple into slices.
  29. Peel the kiwis and cut them into quarters.
  30. Add the pineapple, kiwi, banana, and prune to the syrup and macerate for a couple of minutes.
  31. Prepare the candied rose petals by beating egg whites until frothy.
  32. Dip the rose petals in the egg whites and coat them with sugar on both sides.
  33. Let the petals dry overnight.
  34. Place the macerated fruit on a plate.
  35. Add a scoop of vanilla ice cream.
  36. Garnish with candied rose petals.
  37. Serve immediately.

three_melon_salad_thai_shrimp_peanut_sauce.txt - Three Melon Salad with Thai Shrimp and Peanut Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn to make a refreshing Thai melon salad with a spicy sauce.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh ingredients and balancing flavors.
  • Discover how to make a delicious peanut sauce from scratch.

Ingredients

  • 1/4 cup Thai fish sauce
  • 1/4 cup coconut palm sugar
  • 2-3 kaffir lime leaves, or zest of 1 lime
  • 1 tablespoon fresh lime juice
  • 1/4 cup unsalted peanuts, toasted and roughly chopped
  • 1/4 cup dried shrimp
  • 1 clove garlic, minced
  • 1 small serrano chile, thinly sliced
  • 1/4 cup fresh cilantro, chopped
  • 1 cantaloupe, diced
  • 1 watermelon, diced
  • 1 honeydew melon, diced

Instructions

  1. In a small bowl, combine fish sauce, coconut palm sugar, kaffir lime leaves (or zest), lime juice, and dried shrimp.
  2. Using a mortar and pestle or food processor, grind the dried shrimp until finely powdered.
  3. Add peanuts to the bowl and stir until well combined.
  4. Taste the sauce and adjust seasonings as needed.
  5. In a large bowl, combine diced melons.
  6. Pour the sauce over the melons and toss to coat.
  7. Garnish with fresh cilantro leaves.
  8. Serve immediately.

triple_chocolate_truffle_treat.txt - Triple Chocolate Truffle Treat

Objectives

  • Learn to make a decadent triple chocolate truffle treat
  • Master the pâte sucre technique for a flaky, cookie-like crust
  • Create a rich and creamy truffle filling with biscotti, milk chocolate, and white chocolate
  • Assemble a visually stunning dessert with an espresso parfait, cocoa cookie, and fresh fruit

triple_citrus_tart.txt - Triple Citrus Tart

Objectives

  • Learn to make a triple citrus tart with a unique, easy-to-make crust.
  • Discover how to use a food processor to make a flaky tart crust.
  • Learn how to blanch lemons to remove wax and impurities.

Ingredients

Crust - 1 1/4 cups unbleached flour - 1/4 cup superfine sugar - 1/2 teaspoon kosher salt - 1/2 cup cold unsalted butter, cut into small pieces - 1/4 cup orange juice - 1 tablespoon water - 1 teaspoon orange zest

Lime Curd - 2 large eggs - 2 egg yolks - 1/2 cup sugar - 3/4 cup fresh lime juice - 1/2 cup heavy cream

Meringue - 4 large egg whites - 1/2 cup superfine sugar - 2 lemons, sliced thinly

Other - Confectioners' sugar, for dusting

Instructions

  1. Combine the flour, sugar, and salt in a plastic bag.
  2. Add the cold butter pieces to the bag and shake until the butter is coated with flour.
  3. Place the flour mixture in a food processor and pulse until the butter is the size of peas.
  4. Combine the orange juice, water, and zest in a measuring cup.
  5. With the food processor running, slowly pour the liquid ingredients into the flour mixture.
  6. Pulse until the dough comes together.
  7. Form the dough into a disk, wrap in aluminum foil, and refrigerate for at least two hours.
  8. Preheat oven to 450 degrees F (232 degrees C).
  9. Remove the dough from the refrigerator and lightly flour your hands.
  10. Form the dough into a circle on a floured surface.
  11. Roll out the dough to a thickness of 1/8 to 1/16 inch.
  12. Transfer the dough to a baking sheet.
  13. Arrange the lemon slices on the dough, leaving a 1 1/2-inch border.
  14. Fold the dough over the lemon slices, overlapping the edges.
  15. Refrigerate the tart for at least 10 minutes.
  16. Bake the tart for 15 minutes.
  17. While the tart is baking, make the lime curd.
  18. Combine the eggs, yolks, and sugar in a saucepan.
  19. Whisk the ingredients together until combined.
  20. Add the lime juice and heavy cream.
  21. Cook over medium heat, stirring constantly, until the curd thickens and boils.
  22. Immediately transfer the curd to an ice bath and stir until it reaches room temperature.
  23. Refrigerate the curd until ready to use.
  24. Make the meringue by whipping the egg whites in a stand mixer until frothy.
  25. Gradually add the sugar, a tablespoon at a time, while whipping until stiff peaks form.
  26. Spread the lime curd over the baked tart crust.
  27. Pipe or spoon the meringue over the curd, covering it completely.
  28. Use a fork to create peaks on the meringue.
  29. Bake the tart for an additional 10 minutes.
  30. Allow the tart to cool slightly before dusting with confectioners' sugar.
  31. Serve the tart warm.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UNoZNwubzzg

turban_of_sole.txt - Turban of Sole

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French fish dish, Turban of Sole.
  • Master the art of creating a light and flavorful fish mousse.
  • Understand the importance of using fresh, high-quality fish.

Ingredients

Fish Mousse - 1 1/2 cups pureed fish (sole, halibut, or whiting) - 1 1/2 cups panade (see instructions below) - 1/2 to 2/3 cup heavy cream - Pinch of nutmeg - Salt and white pepper to taste

Panade - 1/2 cup water - 1/2 cup fish stock (or clam juice) - 4 tablespoons butter - 1 teaspoon salt - 3/4 cup all-purpose flour (about 3 1/2 ounces) - 2 large eggs - 2 egg whites (1/4 cup)

Fish Stock - 3 sole frames (or 1 cup fish meat) - Water to cover - 1 cup dry white wine or vermouth - 1/2 bay leaf - Parsley stems (about 1/3 cup) - 1 onion, chopped - 1 carrot, chopped - 1 teaspoon salt

turkey_ballotine.txt - Boned Turkey Ballotine

Objectives

  • Learn how to bone a turkey for a stuffed roast
  • Understand the importance of scraping against the bone
  • Discover ways to stuff and roast a boned turkey

Instructions

  1. Using a small, sharp knife, cut through the skin along the turkey's backbone, starting from the tail end.
  2. Cut against the bone, always scraping away from the skin to avoid tearing.
  3. Work your way up the backbone, separating the meat from the rib cage.
  4. When you reach the wing, cut through the ligaments attaching it to the shoulder blade.
  5. Continue scraping and pulling the meat away from the breastbone, being careful not to cut through the skin.
  6. Once you've removed the backbone and ribs, you can optionally remove the second joint bones and drumstick bones.
  7. To simplify, cut off the wing tips and remove the second joint bones.
  8. Season the turkey meat with salt, pepper, and optionally cognac.
  9. Fill the turkey cavity with stuffing, using about 1 egg per 2 cups of stuffing.
  10. Sew or skewer the turkey closed, ensuring not to overstuff it.
  11. Tie the legs together with string to maintain shape.
  12. Tie the wings together at the top and bottom to hold them in place.
  13. Roast the turkey breast-up in a shallow roasting pan at 350 degrees Fahrenheit for 3 hours and 15 minutes to 3 hours and 30 minutes.
  14. Use a meat thermometer to ensure the turkey is cooked to an internal temperature of 180 to 185 degrees Fahrenheit.
  15. Baste the turkey regularly with melted fat and juices from the pan.
  16. Once cooked, remove the turkey from the oven, remove the strings, and let it rest for 20 to 30 minutes.
  17. Carve the turkey by removing the wings and slicing through the meat.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pGL5Uu6kAzs

turkey_galantine.txt - Turkey Galantine

Objectives

  • Learn to make a turkey galantine, a boned, stuffed turkey cooked and served in aspic.

  • Meat thermometer
  • Board or loaf pan
  • Aluminum foil
  • Weights (5 pounds)
  • Canned consommé with gelatin and wine flavoring (optional)
  • Paper towels

  • Cold stock
  • Sieve
  • Cheesecloth
  • Wax paper
  • Ice
  • Small saucepan
  • Large pan of melted gelatin
  • Olives or truffles (optional)
  • Hard-boiled egg (optional)
  • Green onion tops (optional)

Instructions

  1. Bone the turkey and stuff it with a meat stuffing.
  2. Wrap the turkey in a damp towel, twisting the ends and tying it securely with white string.
  3. Place the turkey in a large roasting pan.
  4. Add chopped carrots, onions, celery, turkey bones, raw veal or pork bones, and the turkey carcass to the pan.
  5. Cover the turkey with homemade turkey stock or canned consommé and water.
  6. Poach the turkey uncovered over moderate heat for about 2.5 hours, or until the meat thermometer reads 180-185 degrees Fahrenheit.
  7. Let the turkey sit in the poaching liquid for an hour to absorb flavor.
  8. Remove the turkey from the liquid and let it cool to room temperature under a weight to firm up the stuffing.
  9. Once the turkey

vanilla_chiffon_cake_jelly_roll.txt - Vanilla Chiffon Cake Jelly Roll with Walnut Mousse

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a basic vanilla chiffon cake.
  • Discover a unique twist by rolling the cake around a delicious walnut mousse.
  • Master the art of making a rich and flavorful walnut mousse.

Ingredients

Cake Batter - 4 egg yolks - 1/2 cup vegetable oil (safflower oil can be used) - 2 tablespoons vanilla extract - 1 cup all-purpose flour - 1 cup granulated sugar - 1 teaspoon baking powder (double-acting) - 1/2 teaspoon baking soda - 1/4 teaspoon kosher salt

Walnut Mousse - 6 ounces (1 2/3 cup) toasted walnuts - Walnut oil (or safflower oil) - Walnut extract (optional) - 5 ounces bittersweet chocolate, melted (milk chocolate can be used) - 1/3 cup granulated sugar - 1/4 cup water - 3 egg yolks - 1 cup heavy cream, whipped

Caramelized Walnuts - 1/2 cup granulated sugar

Other - Vegetable spray - Parchment paper - Cocoa powder - Confectioners' sugar - Mint sprigs (for garnish) - Cranberries (for garnish)

Instructions

  1. Prepare the cake batter:
  2. In a bowl, whisk together 4 egg yolks, 1/2 cup vegetable oil, and 2 tablespoons vanilla extract.
  3. In a separate bowl, sift together 1 cup all-purpose flour, 1 cup granulated sugar, 1 teaspoon baking powder, 1/2 teaspoon baking soda, and 1/4 teaspoon kosher salt.
  4. Gradually add the dry ingredients to the wet ingredients, whisking until just combined.
  5. Gently fold in the whipped egg whites to lighten the batter.
  6. Bake the cake:
  7. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C).
  8. Grease and flour a jelly roll pan.
  9. Pour the batter into the prepared pan and spread evenly.
  10. Bake for 10-12 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
  11. Prepare the walnut mousse:
  12. In a food processor, pulse 6 ounces of toasted walnuts until finely chopped.
  13. Add walnut oil (or safflower oil) and walnut extract (optional) and process until a smooth paste forms.
  14. Add melted chocolate and process until combined.
  15. Make the sugar syrup:
  16. In a small saucepan, combine 1/3 cup granulated sugar and 1/4 cup water.
  17. Bring to a boil over medium heat.
  18. Cook the egg yolks:
  19. In a large bowl, whisk together 3 egg yolks.
  20. Slowly pour the boiling sugar syrup into the egg yolks, whisking constantly.
  21. Continue whisking until the mixture is hot to the touch.
  22. Whip the egg yolks:
  23. Transfer the egg yolk mixture to a stand mixer fitted with a whisk attachment.
  24. Beat on high speed until the mixture has doubled in volume and is cool to the touch.
  25. Assemble the mousse:
  26. Fold the chocolate walnut paste into the whipped egg yolks.
  27. Fold in the whipped cream until just combined.
  28. Caramelize the walnuts:
  29. Heat 1/2 cup granulated sugar in a saucepan over medium-high heat, stirring constantly.
  30. Continue cooking until the sugar melts and turns a golden brown color.
  31. Quickly dip toasted walnuts into the caramel and place on a piece of wax paper to cool.
  32. Roll the cake:
  33. Sprinkle a light layer of granulated sugar over the cooled cake.
  34. Invert the cake onto a piece of parchment paper.
  35. Carefully peel away the parchment paper from the cake.
  36. Spread the walnut mousse evenly over the cake.
  37. Using the parchment paper, roll the cake up tightly.
  38. Refrigerate for at least 2 hours or overnight.
  39. Decorate and serve:
  40. Trim the edges of the rolled cake.
  41. Place strips of parchment paper across the cake.
  42. Dust with cocoa powder and confectioners' sugar.
  43. Carefully remove the parchment paper strips.
  44. Garnish with caramelized walnuts, mint sprigs, and cranberries.
  45. Slice and serve.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZzJmdNOObiE

veal_prince_orloff.txt - Veal Prince Orloff

Objectives

  • Learn to make a classic French dish, Veal Prince Orloff
  • Understand the importance of proper veal selection and browning
  • Master the techniques of making a Mornay sauce, soubise, and duxelles

Ingredients

  • 3.5 lbs boneless veal (boned and tied leg)
  • 1/4 cup plain raw rice
  • 1/2 cup roughly sliced carrots
  • 1 cup roughly sliced onions
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 1/2 tsp thyme
  • 1 tsp salt
  • Freshly ground pepper
  • 4 tbsp butter
  • 4 tbsp olive oil (or cooking oil)
  • Thin sheet of fresh pork fat or suet
  • 4 tbsp butter
  • 3.5 cups sliced onions
  • 1/2 tsp salt
  • Freshly ground pepper
  • 2 cups chopped mushrooms
  • 4 tbsp butter
  • 5 tbsp flour
  • 2 cups hot milk
  • Nutmeg
  • Thick cream
  • Grated Swiss cheese

Instructions

  1. Bring 3 quarts of water to a boil with 2 tbsp salt.
  2. Add 1/4 cup of rice and cook for 5 minutes.
  3. Drain the rice in a sink.
  4. Dry the veal thoroughly.
  5. Heat olive oil in a pan until almost smoking.
  6. Brown the veal on all sides for about 10 minutes.
  7. While the veal is browning, melt 4 tbsp butter in a pan.
  8. Add 1/2 cup carrots, 1 cup onions, and 1 bay leaf.
  9. Cook slowly until softened.
  10. Place the browned veal in a covered casserole.
  11. Season the veal with salt, thyme, and an additional bay leaf.
  12. Cover the veal with a thin sheet of fresh pork fat or suet.
  13. Cover the casserole with aluminum foil and bake in a 325 degree oven for 1 hour and 15 minutes to 1 hour and 30 minutes.
  14. To check for doneness, insert a meat thermometer 15 minutes before the estimated time.
  15. The meat thermometer should read 175 to 180 degrees Fahrenheit.
  16. While the veal is baking, make the soubise.
  17. Melt 4 tbsp butter in a pan.
  18. Add 3.5 cups of sliced onions and cook slowly.
  19. Season with salt and pepper.
  20. Add the cooked rice to the onions and stir.
  21. Cover the pan with aluminum foil and bake in a 325 degree oven for 40 minutes.
  22. Puree the cooked soubise using a sieve, food mill, or blender.
  23. To make the duxelles, squeeze the juice out of 2 cups of chopped mushrooms.
  24. Sauté the mushrooms in a pan with butter for 5 to 6 minutes until they absorb the fat.
  25. While the mushrooms are sautéing, make the Mornay sauce.
  26. Melt 4 tbsp butter in a pan.
  27. Whisk in 5 tbsp flour and cook for 2 minutes.
  28. Remove from heat and whisk in 2 cups of hot milk.
  29. Heat the sauce and season with salt, pepper, and nutmeg.
  30. Combine the cooked duxelles with the soubise puree.
  31. Add a small amount of the Mornay sauce and a touch of cream to the soubise and duxelles mixture.
  32. Let the mixture simmer for 2 to 3 minutes.
  33. Remove the veal from the oven and let it rest.
  34. Remove the fat from the veal juices by straining them through a sieve.
  35. Degrease the juices using a separatory funnel.
  36. Carve the veal into 3/16 inch thick slices.
  37. Arrange the veal slices on a buttered platter.
  38. Spread the soubise and duxelles mixture on top of each veal slice.
  39. Pour the Mornay sauce over the veal.
  40. Broil the veal until the top is brown and bubbly.
  41. Serve the Veal Prince Orloff with braised celery and French bread.
  42. Pair with a red Bordeaux wine, such as a Médoc.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VFzFg6NlQBU

veal_saddle_stuffed_onions_asparagus.txt - Veal Saddle with Stuffed Onions and Asparagus

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and roast a whole veal saddle.
  • Discover the importance of resting meat after cooking.
  • Explore the art of making elegant chocolate truffles.
  • Master the technique of opening and preparing oysters.
  • Create a delicious curry-glazed oyster dish.
  • Learn to make a simple and refreshing glazed orange dessert.

Ingredients

Veal Saddle - 1 whole saddle of veal - Thyme - Salt - Blanched bacon

Stuffed Onions - 6 onions - Butter - Cooked rice - Swiss cheese - Breadcrumbs - Parsley - Cream - Salt - Pepper - Chicken stock - Dry white wine or dry white vermouth

Glazed Oranges - 6 navel oranges - Sugar - Water - Orange liqueur

Curry-Glazed Oysters - Fresh oysters - Butter - Shallots - Mild curry powder - Heavy cream - Beurre manié - Egg yolks - Carrots - Salt - White pepper - Tarragon vinegar - Hot rock salt - Seaweed

Instructions

  1. Season the tenderloins of the veal saddle lightly with thyme and salt.
  2. Cover the tenderloins with blanched bacon to protect them during roasting.
  3. Tie the veal saddle securely to keep the flaps from flapping.
  4. Brown the veal saddle on all sides in a mixture of butter and oil.
  5. Remove any burned fat from the pan.
  6. Place the browned veal saddle in a roasting pan.
  7. Drizzle melted butter over the veal saddle and add browned carrots, onions, and celery for flavor.
  8. Cover the veal saddle with additional blanched bacon.
  9. Pour a cup of dry Madeira wine into the roasting pan.
  10. Roast the veal saddle in a 325-degree oven for 1 hour and 45 minutes.
  11. Let the veal saddle rest for 20-30 minutes after roasting.
  12. Peel the onions from the top down, carefully shaving the root end.
  13. Cut a cone out of the top third of each onion and hollow it out further using a potato baller.
  14. Sauté the onion insides in butter until tender.
  15. Blanch the onion shells in simmering water for 8-9 minutes until tender.
  16. Combine the sautéed onion insides, cooked rice, Swiss cheese, breadcrumbs, parsley, cream, salt, and pepper for the stuffing.
  17. Fill the blanched onion shells with the stuffing.
  18. Sprinkle a pinch of breadcrumbs on top of each stuffed onion and drizzle with a little butter.
  19. Place the stuffed onions in a preheated 375-degree oven and bake for 1 hour until tender.
  20. Remove the veal saddle from the oven and check its temperature with a meat thermometer. It should register between 155 and 160 degrees.
  21. Carefully remove the peel from the oranges in a neat strip, avoiding any white pith.
  22. Cut the orange peel into juliennes.
  23. Blanch the orange peel in simmering water for 8-9 minutes until tender.
  24. Make a sugar syrup by boiling one cup of sugar and one-third cup of water until the sugar dissolves completely.
  25. Boil the sugar syrup until it reaches the hard ball stage (244 degrees).
  26. Add the blanched orange peel to the sugar syrup and stir.
  27. Remove the white part of the orange peel and cut the oranges into 3/8-inch slices.
  28. Drizzle orange liqueur over the orange slices.
  29. To carve the veal saddle, make a cut down one side of the backbone.
  30. Carve the meat away from the bone, keeping the slices on a slant for a nice presentation.
  31. Remove the tenderloin from the underside of the veal saddle and cut it into nuggets.
  32. Open the oysters by inserting a knife into the corner and twisting.
  33. Save the oyster juice and scrape the oysters into a strainer.
  34. Sauté minced shallots and curry powder in butter until fragrant.
  35. Add the strained oyster juice and reduce until syrupy.
  36. Stir in cream and reduce again.
  37. Add beurre manié to thicken the sauce.
  38. Temper egg yolks with hot sauce and then whisk them into the sauce.
  39. Cook the sauce until the yolks are set.
  40. Puree cooked carrots with salt, white pepper, and tarragon vinegar.
  41. Add cream to the carrot puree.
  42. Place a dollop of carrot puree in each oyster shell.
  43. Top the carrot puree with a plump oyster.
  44. Drizzle the curry-glazed sauce over the oysters.
  45. Broil the oysters for a minute or two until golden brown.
  46. Serve the oysters on a bed of seaweed.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8X9GE2an7ko

veal_scallops.txt - Veal Scallops

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and cook veal scallops.
  • Explore different ways to cook veal scallops.
  • Understand the importance of choosing high-quality veal.

Ingredients

  • Veal scallops (about 3/8 inch thick)
  • 1 1/2 tbsp butter
  • 1/2 tbsp olive oil
  • 2 cups sliced mushrooms
  • 1 tbsp shallots (or green onions)
  • 1/4 cup port wine (or Madeira or vermouth)
  • 1 tbsp shallots (or green onions)
  • Brown stock (or canned beef bouillon or cream)
  • 1/2 tbsp tarragon
  • 1 tsp cornstarch
  • Water (or port wine)
  • Cold beef stock
  • Salt and pepper
  • Butter
  • 4 tbsp flour
  • 3 tbsp butter
  • 2 cups chicken stock (or canned chicken bouillon)
  • 1/2 cup finely minced onions (cooked slowly in butter)
  • 2/3 cup sautéed mushrooms
  • Slices of ham
  • Grated Swiss cheese

Instructions

  1. Pound veal scallops to 1/4 inch thickness between sheets of wax paper.
  2. Heat olive oil and butter in a pan over medium-high heat.
  3. Sauté veal scallops for about 8 minutes, ensuring they are dry before adding to the pan.
  4. While veal cooks, sauté mushrooms in oil and butter.
  5. Add shallots to the mushrooms and cook for about 2 minutes.
  6. Remove veal scallops from the pan and set aside.
  7. Deglaze the pan with port wine and scrape up the brown bits.
  8. Add shallots, brown stock, tarragon, and cornstarch mixed with water or port wine.
  9. Simmer sauce until thickened and add veal scallops back to the pan.
  10. Season with salt and pepper and serve immediately.
  11. For Veau Gratinées: Prepare a velouté sauce with flour, butter, and chicken stock.
  12. Add cooked onions and sautéed mushrooms to the velouté sauce.
  13. Arrange veal scallops and slices of ham in an oven-proof dish.
  14. Pour sauce over veal and ham and sprinkle with grated Swiss cheese.
  15. Bake in a hot oven for 20 minutes until bubbly and brown.
  16. Serve Veau Gratinées with steamed rice, buttered peas, hot French bread, and red Medoc Bordeaux wine.

veal_stuffed_braised.txt - Veal Stuffed and Braised in Herbs and Wine

Objectives

  • Learn to bone a leg of veal
  • Create a flavorful marinade for the veal
  • Prepare a ham and cheese stuffing for the veal
  • Braise the stuffed veal in a casserole

Ingredients

  • 1 leg of veal (approx. 5 pounds)
  • 1/2 teaspoon thyme
  • 1 bay leaf
  • 6 peppercorns
  • 2 onions
  • 2 carrots
  • 1/3 cup port
  • 1/3 cup brandy (cognac)
  • 1 tablespoon olive oil
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • Pepper to taste
  • 1 quart simmering water
  • Thick-sliced fat bacon
  • Swiss cheese, sliced 1/8 inch thick
  • Boiled ham, sliced 1/8 inch thick
  • White string
  • Caul fat (optional)

Instructions

  1. Bone the leg of veal using a sharp knife, separating the flesh from the bone and keeping the flesh intact.
  2. Marinate the veal:
  3. Place the veal in a bowl.
  4. Tie together parsley sprigs with string.
  5. Create an herb packet with thyme, bay leaf, and peppercorns.
  6. Slice the carrots thinly and add to the bowl.
  7. Peel and chop the onions, adding them to the bowl.
  8. Add the port, brandy, olive oil, salt, and pepper.
  9. Marinate the veal for 6 hours or overnight.
  10. Blanch the bacon:
  11. Simmer the thick-sliced bacon in a quart of simmering water for 10 minutes.
  12. Remove the bacon and wash it in cold running water.
  13. Dry the bacon thoroughly.
  14. Prepare the stuffing:
  15. Spread the veal out flat.
  16. Layer the Swiss cheese and boiled ham between the slices of veal.
  17. Stuff and tie the veal:
  18. Tuck the stuffing into the veal.
  19. Use white string to tie the veal securely, covering the stuffing with the bacon.
  20. Brown the bottom of the veal:
  21. Heat the casserole over medium heat.
  22. Add the marinated vegetables to the casserole and cook for 10 minutes, until slightly browned.
  23. Place the veal in the casserole, bottom side down, and brown for 5-6 minutes.
  24. Braise the veal:
  25. Preheat the oven to 450 degrees Fahrenheit.
  26. Place the casserole uncovered in the oven and let the top brown.
  27. Baste the top of the veal with the juices every 3-4 minutes.
  28. Once the top is browned, pour the marinade into the casserole.
  29. Cover the casserole with aluminum foil and bake for 1 1/2 hours.
  30. Check for doneness:
  31. Prick the veal with a fork. The juices should run pale yellow. If there is any pinkness, cook for a few more minutes.
  32. Serve:
  33. Let the veal rest for 20 minutes before carving.
  34. Serve the veal on a bed of braised spinach, with sautéed potatoes and whole baked tomatoes.
  35. Thicken the braising juices with cornstarch, if desired, and serve as a sauce.
  36. Enjoy with a red Bordeaux wine.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TEYEEmBnp4M

venison_steak_with_cherry_sauce.txt - Pan-Seared Venison Steaks with Cherry Sauce

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare and cook venison steaks to achieve a rare doneness.
  • Understand the importance of using coarse salt and pepper for a flavorful crust.
  • Master the technique of deglazing a pan to create a rich, flavorful sauce.

Ingredients

  • 2 venison steaks, about 3/4 inch thick
  • Coarse salt and pepper
  • 1 tablespoon grape-seed oil
  • 1/2 cup sun-dried sour cherries, plumped in hot water
  • 2 shallots, minced
  • 3/4 cup Pinot Noir
  • 1/2 cup chicken stock
  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 1 tablespoon Italian parsley, minced
  • Butternut squash flan
  • Pommes Maxim
  • Whipped cream
  • Chocolate tuiles
  • Fresh mint
  • Cocoa powder

Instructions

  1. Season venison steaks generously with coarse salt and pepper, ensuring even coverage.
  2. Pound the steaks with a meat pounder to flatten them slightly and imbed the pepper.
  3. Heat a heavy-bottomed pan over high heat.
  4. Add 1 tablespoon of grape-seed oil to the pan.
  5. Once the oil shimmers, carefully place the venison steaks in the pan, ensuring they don't crowd.
  6. Sear the steaks for 2-3 minutes per side, allowing them to develop a crispy crust.
  7. Remove the steaks from the pan and set aside.
  8. Reduce heat to medium-low and drain most of the fat from the pan.
  9. Add the minced shallots to the pan and cook for a minute, allowing them to pick up any remaining fat.
  10. Deglaze the pan with 3/4 cup of Pinot Noir, scraping up any browned bits from the bottom.
  11. Add the chicken stock and reduce the mixture by half.
  12. Stir in the plumped cherries and minced parsley.
  13. Whisk in the butter, allowing it to melt and thicken the sauce.
  14. Season the sauce with salt to taste.
  15. Return the venison steaks to the sauce and baste them for a minute.
  16. To plate, arrange the butternut squash flan, pommes maxim, and venison steak on a plate.
  17. Drizzle the sauce around the steak and garnish with a chervil sprig.

Chocolate Mousse Cupcake with Tarragon

Objectives

  • Learn to create a decadent chocolate mousse cupcake with a subtle tarragon flavor.
  • Understand the importance of using a water bath to prevent burning the yolks and chocolate.
  • Master the technique of folding egg whites into a chocolate mixture to achieve a light and airy texture.

Ingredients

  • 1 cup bittersweet chocolate, chopped
  • 1/2 cup unsalted butter, cubed
  • 4 egg yolks
  • 1/4 cup granulated sugar
  • 4 egg whites
  • 1/4 teaspoon tarragon, sifted
  • Buttered stainless steel rings (or souffle cups)
  • Whipped cream
  • Chocolate tuiles
  • Fresh mint
  • Cocoa powder

Instructions

  1. Melt the chocolate and butter together over a water bath, stirring until smooth.
  2. In a separate bowl, whisk the egg yolks with the sugar over a water bath until light and fluffy.
  3. In a clean bowl, beat the egg whites until soft peaks form.
  4. Fold the chocolate mixture into the egg yolks, then gently fold in the egg whites.
  5. Sift the tarragon into the mixture and fold until just combined.
  6. Pour the mixture into buttered stainless steel rings, filling them about two-thirds full.
  7. Bake in a preheated 375-degree oven for about 15 minutes, or until the center is just set.
  8. Let the cupcakes cool slightly before serving.
  9. To plate, invert the cupcakes onto a plate.
  10. Top with a quenelle of whipped cream.
  11. Drizzle with chocolate sauce and garnish with a chocolate tuile and a sprig of fresh mint.

Chocolate Tuiles

Objectives

  • Learn how to make delicate chocolate tuiles, a playful garnish for desserts.
  • Understand the importance of bending the tuiles while they are still warm.

Ingredients

  • Chocolate tuile batter
  • Plastic template (cut from a cottage cheese container or similar)
  • 300-degree oven

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 300 degrees.
  2. Place a small amount of chocolate tuile batter onto the plastic template.
  3. Gently lift the template and transfer the batter to a baking sheet.
  4. Bake for 7-8 minutes, or until golden brown.
  5. Remove the tuiles from the oven and allow them to cool for 30 seconds to a minute.
  6. Bend the tuiles over a round object (like a bottle) while they are still warm to shape them.
  7. Let the tuiles cool completely before using.
  8. To use, simply place the tuile on the plate next to the dessert.

vienesse_poppy_seed_torte.txt - Viennese Poppy Seed Torte

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a Viennese poppy seed torte
  • Poach apricots in a ginger syrup
  • Create a light and airy batter using creamed butter, egg yolks, and meringue
  • Assemble the torte with a layer of poached apricots and a final dusting of powdered sugar

Ingredients

  • 2 sticks (1 cup) unsalted butter, softened
  • 7 tablespoons (1 cup minus 1 tablespoon) powdered sugar
  • 1 tablespoon cinnamon
  • Zest of 1 lemon
  • 7 egg yolks
  • 7 egg whites
  • 7 tablespoons sugar
  • 1 1/3 cups cake crumbs (ladyfingers, graham crackers, etc.)
  • 2 1/4 cups poppy seeds
  • 1 tablespoon espresso
  • Juice of 1/2 lemon
  • 12 poached apricots
  • Powdered sugar, for dusting
  • Whipped cream, for serving (optional)

Instructions

  1. Poach the apricots:
    • Combine 3 cups water, 1 1/2 cups sugar, 1/2 vanilla bean (split but not scraped), and a wedge of ginger in a saucepan.
    • Bring to a boil, then reduce heat to a simmer and maintain a gentle simmer, never letting it come to a boil again.
    • Meanwhile, skin the apricots by blanching them in boiling water for a few seconds, then shocking them in ice water.
    • Gently add the apricots to the simmering syrup and poach until tender, about 15-20 minutes.
    • Remove the apricots from the syrup and set aside.
  2. Cream the butter and sugar:
    • Cream together the softened butter and powdered sugar until light and fluffy.
    • Add the cinnamon and lemon zest and cream until well combined.
  3. Add the egg yolks:
    • Gradually add the egg yolks, one at a time, beating well after each addition.
    • If the mixture separates, warm it gently over low heat to help it come together.
  4. Prepare the meringue:
    • In a clean bowl, whisk the egg whites until soft peaks form.
    • Gradually add the sugar while whisking until stiff peaks form.
  5. Fold in the meringue:
    • Gently fold the meringue into the creamed butter mixture, starting with about 1/3 of the meringue and gradually adding the rest.
  6. Combine the dry ingredients:
    • Pulse the cake crumbs in a food processor until finely ground.
    • Grind the poppy seeds in a coffee grinder until fine.
    • Sift the poppy seeds and cake crumbs together.
  7. Fold in the dry ingredients:
    • Gently fold the dry ingredients into the batter, making sure to incorporate them evenly.
  8. Add the espresso and lemon juice:
    • Add the espresso and lemon juice to the batter and fold gently until combined.
  9. Prepare the baking pan:
    • Grease and flour a 9-inch springform pan or a 9x13 inch baking pan.
    • Line the bottom of the pan with parchment paper.
  10. Assemble the torte:
    • Spread half of the batter evenly in the prepared pan.
    • Arrange the poached apricots, cut side up, on top of the batter.
    • Spread the remaining batter over the apricots.
  11. Bake the torte:
    • Bake in a preheated oven at 350 degrees F (175 degrees C) for 35-40 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
  12. Unmold and serve:
    • Let the torte cool in the pan for 10 minutes, then run a knife around the edges to loosen it.
    • Invert the torte onto a serving plate.
    • Remove the parchment paper.
    • Place the remaining poached apricot halves on top of the torte.
    • Dust the torte with powdered sugar.
    • Serve warm or at room temperature with whipped cream, if desired.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oCFkVWf5fA4

wedding_cake.txt - Wedding Cake

Objectives

  • Learn to assemble a multi-layered wedding cake
  • Understand the importance of proper cake preparation and storage
  • Discover techniques for creating a smooth, professional-looking finish

Ingredients

  • 1 cup blanched almonds
  • 1 cup sugar
  • 2 tablespoons cornstarch
  • 8 egg whites
  • 1/4 teaspoon cream of tartar
  • 1/3 cup sugar
  • apricot jam
  • rum-flavored buttercream

Instructions

  1. Preheat oven to 200 degrees Fahrenheit.
  2. Trace the shape of the cake pan onto a piece of parchment paper.
  3. Grind the almonds in a food processor until they resemble a coarse meal.
  4. Combine the ground almonds with 1 cup of sugar and sift 2 tablespoons of cornstarch over the mixture.
  5. Beat 8 egg whites with 1/4 teaspoon of cream of tartar until almost stiff.
  6. Gradually add 1/3 cup of sugar to the egg whites, beating until stiff peaks form.
  7. Gently fold the almond mixture into the egg whites.
  8. Pipe the batter onto the parchment paper, creating a layer about 1/2 inch thick.
  9. Bake for 8 hours.
  10. Cool the cake completely and wrap it tightly in plastic wrap.
  11. Store the cake in the refrigerator for up to a week or in the freezer for a month.
  12. Using a serrated knife, cut the cake layers in half.
  13. Spread a thin layer of apricot jam on one half of the cake layer.
  14. Place the dacquoise layer on top of the apricot jam.
  15. Trim the dacquoise to fit the cake layer.
  16. Brush away any crumbs from the cake.
  17. Spread another thin layer of apricot jam on top of the dacquoise.
  18. Place the other half of the cake layer on top of the apricot jam.
  19. Repeat steps 12-18 for the remaining cake layers.
  20. Place the assembled cake on a turntable and apply a thin layer of buttercream called a "crumb coat" to seal in any crumbs.
  21. Refrigerate the cake until the crumb coat is firm.
  22. Apply a second, smoother layer of buttercream to the cake.
  23. Chill the cake again until the frosting is firm.
  24. Insert clear plastic straws into the cake layers for support.
  25. Stack the cake layers, ensuring there is a small space between each layer for stability.
  26. Secure the cake layers with bamboo skewers inserted through the straws.
  27. Pipe a beaded edge around the perimeter of the cake using a number two piping tip.
  28. Decorate the cake with marzipan fruits, raspberries, and leaves.
  29. Refrigerate the cake until ready to serve.
  30. To serve, cut a slice of cake and decorate it with a few marzipan fruits and leaves.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=k1xwDWIbtzs

white_chocolate_cake.txt - White Chocolate Cake with Raspberry Filling

Objectives

  • Learn how to make a white chocolate cake with a raspberry filling and chocolate balloon garnish.
  • Understand the importance of tempering chocolate for a smooth, shiny finish.
  • Discover the secrets to achieving a light and airy cake texture.

Ingredients

Cake - 12 ounces white chocolate - 4 tablespoons unsalted butter - 10 egg yolks - 1/2 cup granulated sugar - 6 egg whites - 1/4 cup granulated sugar - 1/2 cup cake flour - 2 cups frozen raspberries - 2 tablespoons granulated sugar - 1 tablespoon lemon juice

Garnish - Fresh raspberries - Chocolate sauce

Instructions

  1. Chop the white chocolate into 1/4-inch pieces.
  2. Fill a double boiler with about an inch of water and bring to a simmer.
  3. Place the chopped white chocolate in a heatproof bowl and set it over the simmering water, ensuring the bowl does not touch the water.
  4. Add 2 tablespoons of water and 4 tablespoons of unsalted butter to the white chocolate.
  5. Whisk the chocolate mixture constantly until it is completely melted and smooth.
  6. In a separate bowl, whisk 10 egg yolks and 1/2 cup of sugar together on high speed for 2 minutes.
  7. Reduce the speed to low and continue whisking until the egg yolks are light and lemon-colored.
  8. In another bowl, whisk 6 egg whites on high speed until soft peaks form.
  9. Gradually add 1/4 cup of sugar to the egg whites and continue whisking until stiff peaks form.
  10. Add the melted white chocolate mixture to the egg yolk mixture and whisk gently to combine.
  11. Sift 1/2 cup of cake flour into the chocolate mixture and gently fold it in, incorporating about 1/3 of the egg whites at a time.
  12. Grease and flour two 9-inch round cake pans.
  13. Pour the batter evenly into the prepared pans.
  14. Bake in a preheated 325-degree oven for 26-28 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted into the center comes out clean.
  15. Let the cakes cool in the pans for 20 minutes before inverting them onto a cooling rack to cool completely.
  16. While the cakes are cooling, prepare the raspberry filling.
  17. Puree 2 cups of frozen raspberries with 2 tablespoons of sugar and 1 tablespoon of lemon juice in a food processor until smooth.
  18. Once the cakes are completely cooled, carefully remove them from the cooling rack.
  19. Spread half of the raspberry puree evenly over one cake layer.
  20. Place the second cake layer on top of the raspberry layer.
  21. Spread the remaining raspberry puree over the top of the cake.
  22. Garnish the cake with fresh raspberries, chocolate sauce, and chocolate balloons.
  23. To make chocolate balloons, melt dark chocolate in a double boiler and temper it to 90 degrees.
  24. Inflate water balloons and dip them in the tempered chocolate.
  25. Place the chocolate-covered balloons on parchment paper to set.
  26. Refrigerate the balloons for 25-30 minutes.
  27. Once the balloons are hardened, carefully remove them from the parchment paper and pop them.
  28. Use the chocolate balloon shells as a garnish for the cake.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OTbz3Dtujq0

winged_victory_chicken.txt - Winged Victory Chicken

Objectives

  • Learn to prepare a whole chicken for custom cutting
  • Understand the technique for creating a "winged victory" chicken breast
  • Discover a simple and flavorful aromatic stuffing for chicken

Ingredients

  • 1 whole chicken
  • Salt and pepper to taste
  • 1/4 teaspoon dried tarragon
  • 2 tablespoons butter
  • 3/4 cup finely diced carrots

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=STo-KWYK9is

x_cookies_pizza_rustica.txt - X Cookies and Pizza Rustica

Objectives

  • Learn to make authentic Sicilian X cookies with a fig filling.
  • Understand the process of making pasta frolla dough.
  • Discover a unique recipe for pizza rustica using sweet dough.

Ingredients

For the Dough - 3 cups all-purpose flour (12 oz.) - 1 cup all-purpose flour (4 oz.) - ⅔ cup granulated sugar - 1 teaspoon salt - 1 teaspoon baking powder - 1 cup (2 sticks) unsalted butter, room temperature - 4 large eggs

For the Filling - 1 cup dried mission figs, diced - ¼ cup golden raisins - ¼ cup candied orange peel - ½ cup toasted and quartered almonds - 2 oz semisweet chocolate - ⅓ cup apricot jam - ½ teaspoon ground cinnamon - ¼ cup dark rum

For the Pizza Rustica - 2 cups all-purpose flour (8 oz.) - 1 cup (2 sticks) unsalted butter, room temperature - ⅔ cup granulated sugar - 1 teaspoon salt - 1 teaspoon baking powder - 4 large eggs - 1 pound ricotta cheese - 3 large eggs - 2 tablespoons chopped parsley - ¼ teaspoon ground pepper - ¼ pound fresh mozzarella, grated - 4 oz prosciutto, thinly sliced - ¼ cup pecorino romano cheese, grated

Instructions

  1. Make the Dough:
    • Combine 3 cups flour, sugar, salt, and baking powder in a food processor.
    • Pulse a few times to combine dry ingredients.
    • Add the butter and pulse 15-20 times until butter is finely mixed in.
    • Add the eggs and pulse until dough forms a ball.
    • Finish mixing by hand on a lightly floured surface.
    • Wrap dough in plastic and let it rest for a few minutes while making the filling.
  2. Make the Filling:
    • Combine figs, raisins, orange peel, almonds, chocolate, apricot jam, cinnamon, and rum in a food processor.
    • Pulse until ingredients are finely chopped and combined.
    • Form the filling into a cylinder and set aside.
  3. Assemble the X Cookies:
    • Divide the dough and filling into 12 equal pieces.
    • Roll out each piece of dough to approximately 12 inches long.
    • Roll out each piece of filling to the same length as the dough.
    • Brush dough with beaten egg.
    • Place the filling on top of the dough.
    • Wrap the dough around the filling, forming a log.
    • Cut the log into 2½- to 3-inch lengths.
    • Cut an “X” into each end of the cookie, pushing the seam to the bottom.
    • Place cookies on a baking sheet and bake at 350 degrees for 15-20 minutes.
  4. Make the Pizza Rustica Dough:
    • Roll out the dough into a disk about 12 inches in diameter.
    • Gently lift the dough and place it into a 9-inch pie pan.
    • Press the dough into the pan, patching any holes as needed.
  5. Make the Pizza Rustica Filling:
    • Combine ricotta, eggs, parsley, pepper, mozzarella, prosciutto, and pecorino romano in a bowl.
    • Mix well until ingredients are evenly distributed.
  6. Assemble the Pizza Rustica:
    • Pour the filling into the prepared pie crust.
    • Trim the excess dough around the edges.
    • Roll out the remaining dough into a square.
    • Cut the dough into 12 strips.
    • Arrange the strips over the filling in a lattice pattern.
    • Trim any excess dough.
    • Bake at 350 degrees for 40 minutes.
  7. Serve:
    • Let both the X cookies and the pizza rustica cool to room temperature before serving.
    • Enjoy!

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yXyriZQUmi8

zaleti_biscotti_amaretti_pizzelle.txt - Zaleti, Biscotti, Amaretti, and Pizzelle

Objectives

  • Learn how to make various Italian cookies, including zaleti, biscotti, amaretti, and pizzelle.
  • Understand the importance of using stone-ground cornmeal for a richer corn flavor.
  • Explore different techniques for baking and shaping cookies, such as piping and using a wet cloth for a smooth finish.
  • Discover how to make a festive assortment of cookies for special occasions.
  • Learn tips for baking amaretti and preventing them from sticking to the parchment paper.
  • Explore how to use a pizzelle iron and how to tell when the pizzelle are done baking.

Ingredients

Zaleti Biscotti

  • 1 cup all-purpose flour
  • 1 cup yellow cornmeal (stone-ground preferred)
  • 1/3 cup sugar
  • 1/4 teaspoon salt
  • 1 teaspoon baking powder
  • 1 large egg
  • 1 egg yolk (save egg white for amaretti)
  • 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
  • Zest of 1 lemon
  • 1 cup currants (rinsed)
  • 1 stick unsalted butter (cold)

Amaretti

  • 1/2 pound almond paste
  • 3/4 cup sugar (divided in half)
  • 2 egg whites (freshly separated)
  • Pine nuts (optional)

Pizzelle

  • 2 eggs
  • Pinch of salt
  • 1/2 cup granulated sugar
  • 1 tablespoon anisette
  • 6 tablespoons unsalted butter (melted and cooled)
  • 1 1/4 cups all-purpose flour
  • 1 1/2 teaspoons baking powder (double-acting)

Instructions

  1. Zaleti Biscotti: In a large bowl, whisk together the flour, cornmeal, sugar, salt, and baking powder.
  2. In a separate bowl, whisk together the egg, egg yolk, vanilla extract, and lemon zest.
  3. Add the wet ingredients to the dry ingredients and stir until just combined.
  4. Cut the cold butter into small pieces and add to the mixture.
  5. Use your hands to rub the butter into the flour mixture until it resembles coarse crumbs.
  6. Add the currants and mix well.
  7. Turn the dough out onto a lightly floured surface and knead gently until smooth.
  8. Divide the dough in half.
  9. Classic Biscotti: Form one half of the dough into a log about 12 inches long.
  10. Classic Biscotti: Place the log on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper or foil.
  11. Classic Biscotti: Flatten the log slightly.
  12. Classic Biscotti: Bake at 350°F for 20 minutes.
  13. Classic Biscotti: Let the log cool slightly before slicing it into 1/3-inch thick pieces.
  14. Classic Biscotti: Place the biscotti slices on a baking sheet and bake for an additional 10 minutes at 350°F.
  15. Classic Biscotti: Let the biscotti cool completely before serving.
  16. Zaleti: Form the remaining half of the dough into a log about 12 inches long.
  17. Zaleti: Flatten the log slightly and cut it diagonally into diamond shapes.
  18. Zaleti: Place the diamond shapes on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper or foil.
  19. Zaleti: Bake at 350°F for 12-15 minutes.
  20. Zaleti: Let the zaleti cool completely before serving.
  21. Amaretti: In a stand mixer fitted with the paddle attachment, combine the almond paste and half of the sugar.
  22. Amaretti: Mix until the almond paste is finely crumbed.
  23. Amaretti: Add the remaining sugar and mix until well combined.
  24. Amaretti: Add the egg whites one at a time, mixing until just combined.
  25. Amaretti: Transfer the amaretti mixture to a pastry bag fitted with a 1/2-inch plain tube.
  26. Amaretti: Pipe the amaretti onto a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.
  27. Amaretti: Use a clean, damp non-terry cloth towel to gently smack the top of the amaretti, smoothing out any imperfections and creating a crackled finish.
  28. Amaretti: Sprinkle pine nuts on top of one row of amaretti, if desired.
  29. Amaretti: Bake at 325°F for 10-15 minutes, or until lightly browned and firm.
  30. Amaretti: Let the amaretti cool completely on the baking sheet before transferring them to a wire rack.
  31. Pizzelle: In a large bowl, whisk together the eggs, salt, and sugar until well combined.
  32. Pizzelle: Add the anisette and whisk to combine.
  33. Pizzelle: Gradually whisk in the melted and cooled butter.
  34. Pizzelle: In a separate bowl, whisk together the flour and baking powder.
  35. Pizzelle: Gradually add the dry ingredients to the wet ingredients, folding until just combined.
  36. Pizzelle: Preheat a pizzelle iron according to the manufacturer's instructions.
  37. Pizzelle: Lightly grease the pizzelle iron with butter or cooking spray.
  38. Pizzelle: Spoon about 1/2 tablespoon of batter into the center of each impression in the pizzelle iron.
  39. Pizzelle: Close the iron and bake for 1-2 minutes, or until the steam stops.
  40. Pizzelle: Open the iron and carefully remove the pizzelle.
  41. Pizzelle: While the pizzelle are still warm, you can quarter them or serve them whole.
  42. Pizzelle: Sprinkle the pizzelle with confectioners' sugar, if desired.
  43. Pizzelle: Serve the pizzelle warm or let them cool completely.
  44. Assembling the Platter: Arrange the zaleti, biscotti, amaretti, and pizzelle on a platter with festive ribbons for a beautiful presentation.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Dl1TII03PBE

zucchini_recipes.txt - Zucchini Recipes

Objectives

  • Learn how to prepare zucchini for cooking
  • Explore various zucchini recipes, including a gratin and a soup
  • Understand the importance of proper cooking techniques for zucchini

Ingredients

  • 3 cups grated zucchini
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 1-1.5 cups sliced onions
  • 3 tablespoons flour
  • Zucchini juices
  • Milk
  • 1 tablespoon cream
  • Parmesan and Swiss cheese
  • Bread crumbs
  • Melted butter
  • 6 cups boiling water
  • 1 teaspoon salt
  • 2 cups lima beans
  • 1 cup peas
  • 2 cloves garlic
  • Chopped, blanched bacon
  • 1 teaspoon dried basil
  • Parsley
  • 2 egg yolks
  • 1/3 cup cheese
  • Olive oil

Instructions

  1. Cut off the ends of the zucchini.
  2. Scrub each zucchini under running water with a vegetable brush.
  3. Grate the zucchini and place in a colander.
  4. Sprinkle with salt and toss to coat.
  5. Let the zucchini drain in the colander over a bowl for at least 15 minutes.
  6. While the zucchini is draining, slice the onions.
  7. Heat butter or oil in a pan over medium heat.
  8. Add the onions and cook until tender.
  9. Squeeze the excess water from the grated zucchini using a potato ricer or by hand.
  10. Add the squeezed zucchini to the sauteed onions.
  11. Saute the zucchini and onions until tender.
  12. To make the gratin sauce, whisk the flour into the pan with the sauteed zucchini and onions.
  13. Cook for 2 minutes.
  14. Remove from heat and whisk in the zucchini juices.
  15. Return to heat and whisk in a little milk at a time until thickened.
  16. Stir in cream and cheese.
  17. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
  18. Transfer the zucchini mixture to a gratin dish.
  19. Top with a mixture of bread crumbs and cheese.
  20. Drizzle with melted butter.
  21. Bake in a preheated oven at 425 degrees F for 20-30 minutes, or until bubbling and browned on top.
  22. To make the soup, add the sauteed zucchini and onions to the boiling salted water.
  23. Add the lima beans and peas.
  24. Cook until the beans and peas are tender.
  25. Puree the soup in a food mill.
  26. To make the pistou, pound the garlic in a mortar.
  27. Add the chopped bacon, basil, parsley, and egg yolks.
  28. Pound until well combined.
  29. Stir in the cheese and olive oil.
  30. Add the pistou to the soup.
  31. Heat through and serve.
  32. For the boiled zucchini, boil the zucchini in salted water until tender.
  33. Hollow out the zucchini and fill with cooked vegetables.
  34. Drizzle with melted butter and season with salt and pepper.
  35. Serve hot or cold.

Video: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HxiLEpGPsmY
